# AI FACTORY PIPELINE v5.6 — COMPLETE UNIFIED SPECIFICATION

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Document Purpose** | Single authoritative specification for the AI Factory Pipeline v5.6. Designed for consumption by both AI systems and human engineers. An AI agent reading this document should be able to understand every subsystem, implement any component, and make architectural decisions consistent with the design intent. Every function called has a definition and a contract (§8.10). Every budget figure traces to `BUDGET_CONFIG`. Every factual claim has a source. Zero TBD. |
| **Version** | 5.6 "Clean Room" — Hardened, Clean & Production-Ready |
| **Supersedes** | v5.5 "Bulletproof", v5.4.2, v5.4.1, v5.4, v3.6 "Lean" |

# PART 14: VERIFICATION LEDGER & QUICK REFERENCE CARD

> **Purpose:** This part provides two critical reference tools: (1) the Verification Ledger — web-verified pricing and limits that back every cost claim in the specification, and (2) the Quick Reference Card — a single-page cheat sheet for the entire pipeline. Both are designed for rapid lookup and validation.

---

## 14.1 Verification Ledger — Web-Verified Pricing & Limits

Every cost figure and free-tier claim in this specification was verified against official sources. Do not rely on training data for current pricing.

| # | Tool/Service | Spec Claim | Verified Reality | Source URL | Date Checked | Verdict |
|---|-------------|------------|-----------------|------------|--------------|---------|
| V1 | Anthropic Claude Opus 4.5 | $5/$25 per M tokens (in/out) | $5/$25 per M tokens | platform.claude.com/docs/en/about-claude/pricing | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V2 | Anthropic Claude Sonnet 4.5 | $3/$15 per M tokens | $3/$15 per M tokens (≤200K); $6/$22.50 (>200K) | Same as V1 | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V3 | Anthropic Claude Haiku 4.5 | $1/$5 per M tokens | $1/$5 per M tokens | Same as V1 | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V4 | Anthropic 1M context | "200K standard, 1M beta for tier 4+" | 1M is beta for tier 4 orgs; 200K is universal | Same as V1 | 2026-02-19 | MATCH — C7 correct to baseline 200K |
| V5 | Anthropic extended context pricing | Opus >200K: $10/$37.50; Sonnet >200K: $6/$22.50 | Confirmed (long context rates auto-apply >200K input) | Same as V1 | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V6 | Perplexity Sonar | $1/$1 per M tokens | $1/$1 per M tokens | docs.perplexity.ai/docs/getting-started/pricing | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V7 | Perplexity Sonar Pro | $3/$15 per M tokens | $3/$15 per M tokens | Same as V6 | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V8 | Perplexity Sonar Reasoning Pro | $2/$8 per M tokens | $2/$8 per M tokens | Same as V6 | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V9 | Perplexity request fees (per 1K) | Sonar: Low $5/Med $8/High $12; Pro: Low $6/Med $10/High $14 | Sonar: $5/$8/$12; Sonar Pro & Reasoning Pro: $6/$10/$14 | Same as V6 | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V10 | MacinCloud PAYG | ~$1/hr, 30-hour prepaid blocks, rounds up to nearest hour per day | $1/hr PAYG, prepaid 25-hour or 7-day blocks, rounds to nearest hour daily | macincloud.com/pages/payg.html | 2026-02-19 | ADJUSTED — prepaid min is 25hrs not 30hrs; budget uses $30/mo conservatively |
| V11 | MacinCloud credit expiry | 60 calendar days after last usage | 60 days after last login | support.macincloud.com | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V12 | Telegram Bot API file limit | 50MB for `sendDocument` | 50MB for bots (verified in Bot API docs) | core.telegram.org/bots/api#senddocument | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V13 | FlutterFlow Growth Plan | $80/mo for API+Git export | $80/mo Growth plan (Standard discontinued) | flutterflow.io/pricing | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V14 | Supabase Pro | $25/mo | $25/mo | supabase.com/pricing | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V15 | Neo4j AuraDB Free | $0/mo for graph queries (GA); vector search = Public Preview | Free tier exists; vector indexes in Public Preview; GA timeline unconfirmed | neo4j.com/cloud/aura | 2026-02-19 | MATCH — C8 correct to default pgvector; FIX-13 caveat added |
| V16 | USD→SAR exchange rate | 3.75 fixed | 3.75 SAR/USD (SAMA peg since 1986) | — | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V17 | Apple Developer Program | $99/year membership | $99/year; required for TestFlight + App Store | developer.apple.com/programs | 2026-02-19 | MATCH — FIX-01 amortizes $8.25/mo into BUDGET_CONFIG |

**Ledger Policy:** Any cost figure in this spec that cannot be traced to this ledger or to `BUDGET_CONFIG` is a defect. Re-verify all pricing quarterly or before any production deployment.

**Post-Patch Status:** GREEN — Ready to Build

---

## 14.2 Quick Reference Card

This is the single-page cheat sheet for the entire AI Factory Pipeline v5.6. Print it, pin it, or load it as the first thing when starting work.

```
╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║              AI FACTORY PIPELINE v5.6 — QUICK REFERENCE             ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

PIPELINE:
  S0 Intake → S1 Legal+Preflight → S2 Blueprint+ComplianceArtifacts →
  S3 CodeGen+AssetIngest → S4 Build → S5 Test → [Deploy Gate] →
  S6 Deploy+IconGen → S7 Verify → S8 Handoff → COMPLETED

TERMINAL STATES:
  COMPLETED (success) | HALTED (failure/manual intervention) [C1]

STACKS:
  FlutterFlow | React Native | Swift | Kotlin | Unity | Python Backend
  [ONE per project, enforced]

EXECUTION MODES:
  Cloud (default) | Local (Cloudflare Tunnel) | Hybrid

AUTONOMY:
  Autopilot (full auto) | Copilot (4-way decisions via Telegram)

AI ROLES:
  Scout (Perplexity sonar/sonar-pro)
    → Strategist (Opus)
      → Engineer (Sonnet)
        → Quick Fix (Haiku)

MODELS:
  Configurable via MODEL_CONFIG env vars
  Fallback chains: opus-4.6 → opus-4.5 → sonnet-4.5 [M2]
  Override: STRATEGIST_MODEL_OVERRIDE /
            ENGINEER_MODEL_OVERRIDE /
            QUICKFIX_MODEL_OVERRIDE [FIX-03]

CONTEXT:
  200K tokens baseline (GA)
  1M opt-in via CLAUDE_MAX_CONTEXT env var (beta, tier 4+) [C7]

VECTORS:
  pgvector (default, GA)
  neo4j_vector (opt-in, Public Preview — NOT for prod) [C8, FIX-13]

BUDGET:
  ~$255/month baseline
  +15% buffer = ~$294
  $800 hard ceiling (3,000 SAR)
  (from BUDGET_CONFIG) [FIX-01]

BUDGET GOVERNOR:
  GREEN (0-79%)   → Normal operations
  AMBER (80-94%)  → Degrade models (Opus→Sonnet, Sonnet→Haiku)
  RED   (95-99%)  → Block new project intake
  BLACK (100%)    → Halt all AI calls [FIX-05]

SAFETY:
  Per-role circuit breaker ($2–$25/phase)
  $25/project cap | $80/month AI cap
  Distributed locking (Postgres advisory)
  Idempotency keys | Zero sudo | Audit log [C6]

RESEARCH:
  Web-grounded only; no ungrounded LLM fallback
  UNVERIFIED requires operator sign-off [C5]

TIME TRAVEL:
  /restore State_#N → Git reset + Supabase restore
    + Neo4j visibility mask (checksum-validated)

WAR ROOM:
  L1 (Haiku quick fix)
    → L2 (Scout research + Sonnet fix)
      → L3 (Opus rewrite / stack pivot)

ASSETS:
  Telegram → Supabase Storage (durable) → Git repo
    → platform-specific icons

RECOVERY:
  15-min stuck-project detection
  + advisory lock + auto-resume from last checkpoint [H1]

MAC SAFETY:
  OS-level shutdown -h +60 on session start
  Cancelled on success; $30/mo budget [C9]

COMPLIANCE:
  STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE flag (default false = advisory)
  /force_continue override [H2, FIX-06]
  ComplianceArtifactGenerator at S2: /legal/ templates
    committed to Git [FIX-07]

DEPLOY GATE:
  Copilot: /deploy_confirm required
  Autopilot: 15-min auto-approve timer [FIX-08]

LOCAL AGENT:
  One-click binary (PyInstaller) or manual pip install [H6]

CONTRACTS:
  All 10 key functions have formal contracts in §8.10 [FIX-04]
```

---

## 14.3 How to Use This Document

### For AI Systems

This document is structured so you can load it as context and then build, debug, or extend the pipeline. Every code block is mechanically correct Python or SQL/Cypher. Every schema is a Pydantic model. Every API call includes pricing. Every function called has a definition. Every budget figure reads from `BUDGET_CONFIG`. No section says "TBD" — everything is resolved.

### For Human Engineers

Use the Table of Contents (Part 15) to jump to any subsystem. Each section is self-contained but cross-references related sections. The Implementation Priority Order (§8.6) tells you what to build first.

### Key Conventions

- `§X.Y` = Section X.Y of this document (e.g., §2.1 = Polymorphic State Model)
- `[ADR-NNN]` = Architecture Decision Record (see §1.6 and §8.4)
- `[C1]`–`[C9]`, `[H1]`–`[H6]`, `[M1]`–`[M8]` = v5.4.2 patch IDs (see Part 13)
- `[FIX-01]`–`[FIX-27]` = v5.5 and v5.6 fix IDs (see Part 13)
- Role names are capitalized: **Scout**, **Strategist**, **Engineer**, **Quick Fix**
- Stage names use `S0`–`S8` format, plus `COMPLETED` (terminal success) and `HALTED` (terminal failure)
- All costs in USD unless noted; multiply by 3.75 for SAR
- All budget figures trace to `BUDGET_CONFIG` (§1.4) — no hardcoded dollar amounts in logic

---

*End of Part 14 — Verification Ledger & Quick Reference Card*

# PART 13: COMPLETE CHANGELOG & AUDIT TRAIL

> **Purpose:** This part documents every patch applied across four cross-model audit rounds, from v5.4.1 through v5.6. It serves as the authoritative record of what changed, why, who flagged it, and how it was validated. Total: 50 patches (12 inherited from v5.4.1 + 23 from v5.4.2 + 15 from v5.5 + 12 from v5.6). All patches PASS validation.

---

## 13.1 v5.6 Changelog — 12 Clean Room Fixes Applied

**Fourth audit round:** 7 independent AI models (Gemini, Grok, ChatGPT, Perplexity, DeepSeek, Qwen, Kimi) re-audited v5.5. After cross-validation and deduplication, 12 precisely scoped fixes identified. All changes additive or corrective — no v5.5 functionality removed. Backward compatibility maintained. New ADRs: 047–051.

| FIX ID | Title | Priority | Phase | Status |
|--------|-------|----------|-------|--------|
| FIX-16 | Version Hygiene Enforcement | CRITICAL | 1 | PASS — All governance text references v5.6; `spec_lint.py` added; ADR-047 |
| FIX-17 | Budget Buffer Segmentation | CRITICAL | 1 | PASS — `BUDGET_BUFFER_SEGMENTS`: $200+$200+$100+$44.70=$544.70; ADR-048 |
| FIX-18 | Orchestrator Supervisor Definition | CRITICAL | 1 | PASS — `startupProbe`, `UPTIME_CHECK_CONFIG`, 4-level supervision chain added |
| FIX-19 | Perplexity Context-Tier Cap | HIGH | 2 | PASS — `SCOUT_MAX_CONTEXT_TIER` env var + enforcement in `call_perplexity_safe()`; ADR-049 |
| FIX-20 | 3AM Runbook Operator Simplification | HIGH | 2 | PASS — Step 3 Telegram-native; GCP Console in §7.3.2a Advanced; ADR-050 |
| FIX-21 | App Store Submission Protocol | HIGH | 2 | PASS — `IOS_SUBMISSION_STEPS`: 5-step archive→export→validate→upload→poll |
| FIX-22 | Airlock Clarification | HIGH | 2 | PASS — "(Binary Delivery Fallback)" in header; clarification paragraph added |
| FIX-23 | Time Machine Header Rewording | MEDIUM | 3 | PASS — docstring updated: "Masks: Neo4j" explicit |
| FIX-24 | Per-Project Cost Disclaimer | MEDIUM | 3 | PASS — Merged into FIX-17; throughput-sensitivity table in §1.4.4 |
| FIX-25 | Perplexity Tiered Fee Annotation | MEDIUM | 3 | PASS — Tier breakdown comment added to `BUDGET_CONFIG` `variable_monthly` |
| FIX-26 | Multi-Stack Integration Example | MEDIUM | 3 | PASS — food-delivery program example in §H4; v7.0 integration testing deferred |
| FIX-27 | Operator Handoff Intelligence Pack | HIGH | 2 | PASS — 4 per-project + 3 per-program docs generated at S8; HandoffDoc nodes in Mother Memory; Janitor-exempt; ADR-051 |

**New ADRs (v5.6):**

| ADR | Title | Fix |
|-----|-------|-----|
| ADR-047 | Version Hygiene Enforcement — automated `spec_lint.py` for version contamination | FIX-16 |
| ADR-048 | Budget Buffer Segmentation — $544.70 split into 4 purpose-specific reserves | FIX-17 |
| ADR-049 | Scout Context-Tier Ceiling — `SCOUT_MAX_CONTEXT_TIER` prevents cost spikes | FIX-19 |
| ADR-050 | Telegram-Native Operator Recovery — 3AM runbook uses only `/admin` commands | FIX-20 |
| ADR-051 | Operator Handoff Intelligence Pack — S8 generates tailored operational docs for zero-IT operator | FIX-27 |

---

## 13.2 v5.5 Changelog — 15 Hardening Fixes Applied (Bulletproof)

**Third audit round:** 6 independent AI models re-audited v5.4.2. After cross-validation, deduplication, and contradiction resolution, 15 precisely scoped fixes were identified. Changes are additive or corrective — no v5.4.2 functionality removed. Backward compatibility maintained per governing rules. New ADRs: 043–046.

### Tier 1 — Foundation (FIX-01 to FIX-04)

| ID | Fix | Key Change | Priority | Source Model(s) | Validation |
|----|-----|------------|----------|-----------------|------------|
| FIX-01 | Apple Developer Fee Amortization | $8.25/mo amortized into `BUDGET_CONFIG`; `fixed_monthly_total`→$221.75; baseline→$255.30; all derived values cascaded | CRITICAL | Qwen, ChatGPT | PASS |
| FIX-02 | Illustrative Cost Markup | War Room cost approximations tagged "(illustrative)"; header note added to §2.5 | MEDIUM | Perplexity | PASS |
| FIX-03 | MODEL_OVERRIDE Env Vars | `STRATEGIST/ENGINEER/QUICKFIX_MODEL_OVERRIDE` env vars; `call_ai()` override path; ADR-043 | HIGH | Grok, Qwen | PASS |
| FIX-04 | Function Contract Appendix | §8.10 with 8 function contracts: params, return type, side effects, error behavior, target file | HIGH | Perplexity | PASS |

### Tier 2 — Enforcement (FIX-05 to FIX-09)

| ID | Fix | Key Change | Priority | Source Model(s) | Validation |
|----|-----|------------|----------|-----------------|------------|
| FIX-05 | Budget Governor Module | §2.14: 4-tier graduated degradation (GREEN/AMBER/RED/BLACK); `BudgetGovernor.check()` before every `call_ai()`; integer cents math; ADR-044 | CRITICAL | ChatGPT | PASS |
| FIX-06 | Strict Compliance Enforcement | STRICT=true + blockers >0.7 confidence → HALTED; `/force_continue` with typed confirmation; ADR-045 | CRITICAL | DeepSeek, Perplexity | PASS |
| FIX-07 | Compliance Artifact Generator | S2 generates `/legal/` templates: iOS privacy manifest, Android Data Safety YAML, `privacy_policy.md`, `terms_of_service.md`, `store_checklist.md` | HIGH | ChatGPT | PASS |
| FIX-08 | Pre-Deploy Operator Acknowledgment | Mandatory S5→S6 gate: Copilot=`/deploy_confirm`; Autopilot=15min auto-approve; race protection via C6 locks; ADR-046 | HIGH | Perplexity | PASS |
| FIX-09 | Airlock Disclaimer | Boxed scope disclaimer; all Preflight/StorePolicyEvent classified "advisory"; no guarantee language | MEDIUM | Perplexity, ChatGPT | PASS |

### Tier 3 — Documentation (FIX-10 to FIX-15)

# AI Factory Pipeline v5.6 — Complete Unified Specification

> **Document Purpose:** This is the single authoritative specification for the AI Factory Pipeline. It is designed for consumption by both AI systems and human engineers. An AI agent reading this document should be able to understand every subsystem, implement any component, and make architectural decisions consistent with the design intent. Every function called has a definition and a contract (§8.10). Every budget figure traces to `BUDGET_CONFIG`. Every factual claim has a source. Zero TBD.

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Version** | 5.6 "Clean Room" — Hardened, Clean & Production-Ready |
| **Date** | February 2026 |
| **Audit Basis** | 26 hardening fixes across four cross-model audit rounds |
| **Classification** | Internal — Operator & Engineering Use |
| **Status** | **GREEN — Ready to Build** |

---

## How to Use This Document

**For AI Systems:** This document is structured so you can load it as context and then build, debug, or extend the pipeline. Every code block is mechanically correct Python or SQL/Cypher. Every schema is a Pydantic model. Every API call includes pricing. Every function called has a definition. Every budget figure reads from `BUDGET_CONFIG`. No section says "TBD" — everything is resolved.

**For Human Engineers:** Use the Table of Contents to jump to any subsystem. Each section is self-contained but cross-references related sections. The Implementation Priority Order (§8.6) tells you what to build first.

### Key Conventions

- `§X.Y` = Section X.Y of this document (e.g., §2.1 = Polymorphic State Model)
- `[ADR-NNN]` = Architecture Decision Record (see §1.6 and §8.4)
- Role names are capitalized: **Scout**, **Strategist**, **Engineer**, **Quick Fix**
- Stage names use `S0`–`S8` format, plus `COMPLETED` (terminal success) and `HALTED` (terminal failure)
- All costs in USD unless noted; multiply by 3.75 for SAR
- All budget figures trace to `BUDGET_CONFIG` (§1.4) — no hardcoded dollar amounts in logic

---

## Quick Reference Card

| Aspect | Detail |
|--------|--------|
| **Pipeline** | S0 Intake → S1 Legal+Preflight → S2 Blueprint+ComplianceArtifacts → S3 CodeGen+AssetIngest → S4 Build → S5 Test → [Deploy Gate] → S6 Deploy+IconGen → S7 Verify → S8 Handoff → COMPLETED |
| **Terminal States** | `COMPLETED` (success) · `HALTED` (failure / manual intervention) |
| **Stacks** | FlutterFlow · React Native · Swift · Kotlin · Unity · Python Backend — **one per project, enforced** |
| **Execution Modes** | Cloud (default) · Local (Cloudflare Tunnel) · Hybrid |
| **Autonomy** | Autopilot (full auto) · Copilot (4-way decisions via Telegram) |
| **AI Roles** | Scout (Perplexity Sonar/Sonar Pro) → Strategist (Opus) → Engineer (Sonnet) → Quick Fix (Haiku) |
| **Models** | Configurable via `MODEL_CONFIG` env vars; fallback chains (opus-4.6 → opus-4.5 → sonnet-4.5) |
| **Model Override** | `STRATEGIST_MODEL_OVERRIDE` / `ENGINEER_MODEL_OVERRIDE` / `QUICKFIX_MODEL_OVERRIDE` |
| **Context** | 200K tokens baseline (GA); 1M opt-in via `CLAUDE_MAX_CONTEXT` env var (beta, tier 4+) |
| **Vectors** | pgvector (default, GA) · neo4j_vector (opt-in, Public Preview — not for production) |
| **Budget** | ~$255/month baseline · +15% buffer ≈ $294 · $800 hard ceiling (from `BUDGET_CONFIG`) |
| **Governor** | GREEN (0–79%) → AMBER (80–94%, degrade models) → RED (95–99%, block intake) → BLACK (100%, halt) |
| **Safety** | Per-role circuit breaker ($2–$25/phase) · $25/project cap · $80/month AI cap |
| **Locking** | Distributed locking (Postgres advisory) · Idempotency keys · Zero sudo · Audit log |
| **Research** | Web-grounded only; no ungrounded LLM fallback; `UNVERIFIED` requires operator sign-off |
| **Time Travel** | `/restore State_#N` → Git reset + Supabase restore + Neo4j visibility mask (checksum-validated) |
| **War Room** | L1 (Haiku quick fix) → L2 (Scout research + Sonnet fix) → L3 (Opus rewrite / stack pivot) |
| **Assets** | Telegram → Supabase Storage (durable) → Git repo → platform-specific icons |
| **Recovery** | 15-min stuck-project detection + advisory lock + auto-resume from last checkpoint |
| **Mac Safety** | OS-level `shutdown -h +60` on session start; cancelled on success; $30/mo budget |
| **Compliance** | `STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE` flag (default `false` = advisory); `/force_continue` override |
| **Compliance Artifacts** | `ComplianceArtifactGenerator` at S2: `/legal/` templates committed to Git |
| **Deploy Gate** | Copilot: `/deploy_confirm` required; Autopilot: 15-min auto-approve timer |
| **Agent** | One-click binary (PyInstaller) or manual `pip install` |
| **Contracts** | All 10 key functions have formal contracts in §8.10 |

## Part 1: Foundation & Evidence

### §1.1 Executive Summary

The AI Factory Pipeline is an autonomous system that produces multi-platform applications from natural language briefs. It is designed for a solo operator with zero IT background in the Kingdom of Saudi Arabia.

The pipeline incorporates seven architectural pillars:

**1. Polyglot Stack Selection** — The pipeline does not assume a single framework. A Stack Selector Brain analyzes each project and selects the optimal technology (FlutterFlow, React Native, Swift, Kotlin, Unity, or Python backend) based on requirements, complexity, and cost.

**2. Three-Mode Execution** — The pipeline runs in Cloud Mode (default), Local Mode (operator's machine via Cloudflare Tunnel for cost savings), or Hybrid Mode (parallel split: cloud does backend, local does heavy rendering).

**3. Eyes vs. Hands Intelligence Doctrine** — AI models have hardcoded roles to prevent competence drift. Perplexity Sonar is the read-only Scout (research), Claude Opus 4.6 is the Strategist (planning, legal, War Room), Claude Sonnet 4.5 is the Engineer (code, files, fixes).

**4. Variable Autonomy Control** — The operator toggles between Autopilot (full autonomy) and Copilot (4-way decision menus, no open-ended questions) via Telegram.

**5. Continuous Legal Guardian** — Compliance is not a single gate at S1. A parallel legal thread monitors every stage from blueprint to deployment, enforcing PDPL active consent, CST time-of-day restrictions, and Ministry of Commerce licensing.

**6. Time Travel** — Every pipeline state is a unified snapshot (Git commit + pipeline state JSON + knowledge graph visibility). The operator can command `/restore State_#891` and the factory restores pipeline state and repository code to that exact moment. Neo4j nodes created after the restore point are masked (set `_hidden=true`) rather than deleted. Database schema (Supabase DDL) is forward-only and is not restored.

**7. Budget Safety Circuit Breaker** — Per-role/phase budget limits (ranging from $2 for Scout research to $25 for CodeGen), plus a $25/project cap and $80/month global cap. Exceeded? Pipeline pauses and requests operator authorization.

#### Core Technology Stack

| Role | Component | Purpose |
|------|-----------|---------|
| Orchestration | LangGraph (Python) on Google Cloud Run | DAG execution engine |
| Stack Selection | Stack Selector Brain (Claude Opus 4.6) | Choose optimal tech stack per project |
| App Generation | FlutterFlow / React Native / Swift / Kotlin / Unity / Python | Polyglot — selected per project |
| Scout (Intel) | Perplexity Sonar API | READ-ONLY research: docs, laws, bugs, trends |
| Strategist (Brain) | Claude Opus 4.6 | Architecture, legal risk, War Room supervision |
| Engineer (Hands) | Claude Sonnet 4.5 | Code generation, file creation, fix application |
| Quick Fix | Claude Haiku 4.5 | Syntax fixes, lightweight tasks |
| GUI Automation | OmniParser V2 + UI-TARS 1.5 | Visual IDE control (FlutterFlow/Xcode) |
| Knowledge Graph | Neo4j AuraDB (Mother Memory v2) | Long-term patterns + vector ontology |
| State Persistence | Supabase PostgreSQL + Git | Dual-write + time-travel snapshots |
| Tunnel (Local Mode) | Cloudflare Tunnel (free) | Secure local machine ↔ pipeline connection |
| Platform Builds | GitHub Actions + MacinCloud + Local | Three-mode execution |
| Deployment | Firebase + Play Console + TestFlight | Web / Android / iOS staging |
| Operator Interface | Telegram Bot | Autopilot / Copilot control center |

#### Pipeline Flow

```
S0 Intake → S1 Legal → S2 Blueprint+StackSelect+Design → S3 CodeGen → S4 Build → S5 Test → S6 Deploy → S7 Verify → S8 Handoff
                                                    (with continuous legal thread S1–S8)
```

**Target throughput:** 4 projects/month at ~55 minutes automated time per project (slightly longer than minimal due to design mocks + stack selection).

---

### §1.2 Mission Constraints

These are non-negotiable constraints that govern every design decision in the pipeline.

#### Core Constraints

| Constraint | Target | Measurement |
|-----------|--------|-------------|
| Monthly cost ceiling | ≤ 3,000 SAR (~$800 USD) | Sum of all infrastructure, APIs, and services |
| Human intervention | ≤ 8% of total pipeline time at steady state | (Operator minutes) / (Total minutes) |
| Operator skill level | Zero IT background | All interactions via Telegram; no CLI, no code, no dashboards |
| Target platforms | iOS + Android + Web (minimum) | Every project produces at least these three |
| Regulatory compliance | KSA laws (CST, SAMA, NDMO, NCA, SDAIA, PDPL) | Continuous compliance thread, not just gate |
| Exchange rate | 3.75 SAR/USD | Fixed peg maintained by SAMA since 1986 |
| Zero sudo | Pipeline never executes with root/sudo | User-space only: npx, venv, rbenv, local installs |

#### Additional Constraints

| Constraint | Target | Measurement |
|-----------|--------|-------------|
| AI cost caps | Per-role phase limits ($2–$25), per-project $25, monthly $80 | Circuit breaker pauses + requests auth on breach |
| No portal UI login | Apple/Google portals never accessed via GUI automation | API-only (Service Accounts); binary to Telegram on failure |
| No open-ended questions | Copilot mode presents 4 choices, never blank prompts | Decision matrix enforced at every operator interaction |
| Model role enforcement | Each AI model has one role; no competence drift | Scout ≠ Engineer ≠ Strategist in code contracts |

#### Human Intervention: Honest Projections

| Phase | Timeline | Expected Intervention | Why |
|-------|----------|----------------------|-----|
| Ramp-up | Weeks 1–4 | ~12–18% | Stack selection learning curve; polyglot template library empty |
| Stabilization | Weeks 5–12 | ~8–12% | Mother Memory v2 accumulates cross-stack patterns |
| Steady state | Week 13+ | ~4–7% | Mature templates, tuned prompts, legal cache warm |

Improvement factors: War Room protocol reduces wasted retry cycles. Design mocks catch UI issues before build (eliminating late-stage rework). Continuous legal thread prevents deployment failures from compliance oversights.

---

*End of Part 1. Reply "Cont" for Part 2.*

## Part 2: Evidence Ledger, Budget, Architecture Overview & Decision Records

---

### §1.3 Evidence Ledger

Every component and price in this specification is verified against authoritative sources (February 2026).

#### §1.3.1 AI Model Pricing (Verified)

**The Four Roles:**

| Role | Model | Input $/M tokens | Output $/M tokens | Request Fee | Context | Source |
|------|-------|------------------:|-------------------:|-------------|---------|--------|
| Scout | Perplexity Sonar | $1.00 | $1.00 | Low $5 / Med $8 / High $12 per 1K req | 128K | docs.perplexity.ai [V6, V9] |
| Scout Pro | Perplexity Sonar Pro | $3.00 | $15.00 | Low $6 / Med $10 / High $14 per 1K req | 200K | docs.perplexity.ai [V7, V9] |
| Scout Reasoning | Perplexity Sonar Reasoning Pro | $2.00 | $8.00 | Low $6 / Med $10 / High $14 per 1K req | 200K | docs.perplexity.ai [V8, V9] |
| Strategist | Claude Opus (4.6 → 4.5 fallback) | $5.00 | $25.00 | — | 200K standard | platform.claude.com [V1] |
| Engineer | Claude Sonnet (4.5 → 4 fallback) | $3.00 | $15.00 | — | 200K standard | platform.claude.com [V2] |
| Quick Fix | Claude Haiku 4.5 | $1.00 | $5.00 | — | 200K | platform.claude.com [V3] |

**Perplexity pricing notes:** Token pricing web-verified 2026-02-19 [V6–V9]. Sonar Reasoning Pro is $2/$8 per official docs. Request fees use `search_context_size` tiers — budget calculations use Medium as baseline (±30% variance for High-context queries). Citation tokens are no longer billed for Sonar and Sonar Pro.

**Batch API discount:** 50% off input + output for all Claude models (non-urgent processing).

**Context baseline:** All prompts are designed for 200K tokens (GA, universally available). Extended context (1M tokens) is available as opt-in beta for usage tier 4+ organizations. Set `CLAUDE_MAX_CONTEXT=1000000` in env vars to enable. If the API request exceeds 200K input tokens without access, truncation logic applies gracefully.

**Extended context tiered pricing:** When using >200K input tokens, all tokens incur premium long-context rates: Opus $10/$37.50, Sonnet $6/$22.50, Haiku unchanged. Budget projections assume base contexts (≤200K). See [V4, V5] in Verification Ledger.

**Model version abstraction:** All model version strings are configuration targets, not hard dependencies. The system defaults to the latest available stable version via fallback chains: opus-4.6 → opus-4.5 → sonnet-4.5. No section guarantees a specific model version for launch. See `MODEL_CONFIG` (§2.4).

**Prompt caching:** Up to 90% reduction on cached input tokens (Claude). Cache write: 1.25× base; cache read: 0.1× base.

**OpenAI removal:** GPT-4o-mini and GPT-4o are not in the default cascade. Their roles are covered by Claude Haiku (quick tasks), Perplexity Sonar (research), and Claude Opus/Sonnet (planning/coding). An OpenAI key may optionally be retained for the GUI Supervisor if preferred for model independence.

**AI cost model (4 projects/month):**

| Role | Usage Pattern | Monthly Estimate |
|------|--------------|----------------:|
| Scout (Sonar) | ~150 research queries + ~300K tokens | $3.25 |
| Scout Pro (Sonar Pro) | ~30 deep research queries + ~200K tokens | $1.35 |
| Strategist (Opus 4.6) | ~400K input + 150K output/month | $5.75 |
| Engineer (Sonnet 4.5) | ~3M input + 800K output/month | $21.00 |
| Quick Fix (Haiku 4.5) | ~500K input + 200K output/month | $1.50 |
| GUI Supervisor (Haiku 4.5) | ~200K input + 100K output/month | $0.70 |
| **Total AI** | | **$33.55** |

Note: With prompt caching on repeated contexts (project blueprints, legal templates), effective cost drops ~20–30%. Budget uses uncached estimate for safety margin.

#### §1.3.3 GUI Automation Stack (Verified)

| Component | Platform | License |
|-----------|----------|---------|
| OmniParser V2 (perception) | macOS/Win/Linux (Python) | AGPL + MIT |
| UI-TARS 1.5 7B (action) | Cross-platform | Apache 2.0 |
| UI-TARS Desktop (macOS app) | macOS/Win/Linux | Apache 2.0 |

GUI automation is used when the selected stack requires a visual IDE (FlutterFlow, Xcode visual editor). For code-only stacks (React Native, Python), GUI automation is not needed — the Engineer (Sonnet) writes code directly.

#### §1.3.4 Polyglot Stack Options (Verified)

| Stack | When Selected | Build Toolchain | License | Cost |
|-------|--------------|-----------------|---------|-----:|
| FlutterFlow | Rapid MVP, non-technical operator, standard CRUD | FlutterFlow API + GUI agent | Proprietary ($80/mo) | $80/month |
| React Native | Complex custom UI, existing JS team, web-first | Expo CLI + Metro bundler | MIT | $0 |
| Swift (iOS native) | iOS-only premium app, ARKit/HealthKit | Xcode + SwiftPM | Apple EULA | $0 (Xcode free) |
| Kotlin (Android native) | Android-only, Jetpack Compose | Gradle + Android Studio | Apache 2.0 | $0 |
| Unity | Games, AR/VR, 3D apps | Unity Editor | Free (< $100K rev) | $0 |
| Python backend | API-only, data pipeline, ML service | FastAPI + Docker | MIT | $0 |

**Budget note:** FlutterFlow's $80/month is budgeted regardless of stack selection (the subscription is maintained for projects that need it). When the stack selector chooses a non-FF stack, that month's FF cost is "overhead" but remains within budget. Cancellation is possible if FF is consistently unused for 3+ months.

#### §1.3.5 Tunneling & Local Mode (Verified)

| Component | Purpose | Cost | Source |
|-----------|---------|-----:|--------|
| Cloudflare Tunnel (cloudflared) | Secure outbound-only connection from operator's machine to pipeline | $0 (free for all plans) | blog.cloudflare.com/tunnel-for-everyone |
| Heartbeat Agent | Lightweight daemon on local machine; pings pipeline every 30s | $0 (part of pipeline code) | Custom implementation |
| Ngrok (backup) | Alternative tunnel if Cloudflare is unavailable | $0 (free tier) or $8/month | ngrok.com/pricing |

**Cloudflare Tunnel free-tier scope:** The pipeline uses Cloudflare Tunnel in its basic free-tier configuration: outbound-only connection, no custom domain required (uses `.trycloudflare.com` quick tunnel or named tunnel with existing domain). Not required and not used: Argo Smart Routing ($0.10/GB), Zero Trust Access ($0/50 users but adds auth complexity), Load Balancing (paid). At 4 projects/month, traffic is negligible. Monitor if scaling to >20 projects/month where Argo may become cost-effective.

#### §1.3.6 Regulatory References (Verified)

| Body | Full Name | Coverage |
|------|-----------|----------|
| CST | Communications, Space & Technology Commission | App registration, push notification time-of-day restrictions |
| SAMA | Saudi Central Bank | Payment processing, financial data, sandbox enforcement |
| NDMO | National Data Management Office | Data classification, cross-border transfer, data residency |
| NCA | National Cybersecurity Authority | Cybersecurity controls, encryption requirements |
| SDAIA | Saudi Data & AI Authority | AI governance, PDPL enforcement, privacy policy generation |
| Ministry of Commerce | Ministry of Commerce | Business licensing by app category (e-commerce, food delivery, transport) |

**PDPL (Personal Data Protection Law):** The pipeline adds active consent enforcement — the DocuGen module generates compliant privacy policies and the continuous legal thread verifies UI consent checkboxes are present.

### §1.4 Verified Budget Ledger

All prices at 3.75 SAR/USD (fixed SAMA peg).

#### §1.4.0 Canonical Budget Configuration

All budget references throughout this specification read from this single object. No hardcoded dollar amounts in monitoring code, alerts, or prose. Any budget figure not traceable to `BUDGET_CONFIG` is a defect.

```python
# Single source of truth for all budget figures.
# Apple Developer fee amortized into fixed costs.
# Every monitoring threshold, alert, and prose reference reads from this config.
# To update pricing: change this object, re-run validation, update changelog.

BUDGET_CONFIG = {
    "version": "5.6",
    "fx_rate": 3.75,                             # USD→SAR (SAMA peg since 1986) [V16]

    "fixed_monthly": {
        "neo4j_aura_pro":              65.00,     # Graph queries (GA); vector search via pgvector [V15]
        "supabase_pro":                25.00,     # DB + Storage + Auth [V14]
        "flutterflow_growth":          80.00,     # 1 seat; required for API/Git export [V13]
        "domain_dns":                   1.50,     # ~$0.38/project
        "apple_developer_monthly":      8.25,     # $99/yr ÷ 12; TestFlight + App Store [V17]
        # ── Free-tier services ($0 within limits) ──
        "cloudflare_tunnel":            0.00,     # Free for basic outbound [M4]
        "cloud_run":                    0.00,     # Free: 2M req/mo, 360K vCPU-sec
        "cloud_scheduler":              0.00,     # Free: 3 jobs
        "github":                       0.00,     # Free: 2,000 Actions min/mo
        "firebase_spark":              0.00,     # Free: 1GB storage, 10GB/mo transfer
        "omniparser_v2":                0.00,     # Self-hosted on Cloud Mac
    },

    "variable_monthly_4proj": {
        "anthropic_opus":               5.75,     # Strategist: sparingly — planning, legal, War Room [V1]
        "anthropic_sonnet":            21.00,     # Engineer: S3 codegen, S4 planning, fixes [V2]
        "anthropic_haiku":              2.20,     # Quick Fix + GUI Supervisor [V3]
        "perplexity_sonar":             4.60,     # ~180 queries (Sonar + Sonar Pro + search fees) [V6-V9]
        # Perplexity tier breakdown (at SCOUT_MAX_CONTEXT_TIER="medium" default):
        #   Sonar (small context):  ~120 queries × $0.005 = $0.60  — quick lookups, regulation checks
        #   Sonar Pro (medium ctx): ~50  queries × $0.05  = $2.50  — market research, tech evaluations
        #   Sonar Pro (large ctx):  ~10  queries × $0.15  = $1.50  — deep-research (requires "large")
        #   Total: $4.60/month — scales with SCOUT_MAX_CONTEXT_TIER setting (ADR-049)
        "macincloud_payg":             30.00,     # ~25-30 hrs; iOS builds + GUI automation [V10]
        "ui_tars_openrouter":          12.00,     # ~400-800 GUI interactions/month
    },

    # ── Computed (never hardcoded) ──
    # fixed_subtotal:      sum(fixed_monthly.values())                = $179.75
    # variable_subtotal:   sum(variable_monthly_4proj.values())       = $75.55
    # total_baseline:      fixed_subtotal + variable_subtotal         = $255.30
    # total_baseline_sar:  total_baseline * fx_rate                   = 957.38 SAR
    # buffer_15pct:        total_baseline * 1.15                      = $293.60
    # hard_ceiling_usd:    800.00
    # hard_ceiling_sar:    3000.00
    # buffer_remaining:    hard_ceiling_usd - total_baseline          = $544.70 (68.1%)
    # cost_per_project:    total_baseline / 4                         = $63.83
}
```

#### Budget Buffer Segmentation (ADR-048)

The $544.70 buffer between baseline ($255.30) and hard ceiling ($800.00) is segmented into purpose-specific reserves. The Budget Governor (§2.14) draws from `elastic_spike` first, then `deterministic_growth`. The `incident_reserve` requires manual `/admin budget_override`.

```python
BUDGET_BUFFER_SEGMENTS = {
    "version": "5.6",
    "total_buffer_usd": 544.70,       # hard_ceiling - total_baseline

    "segments": {
        "deterministic_growth": {
            "usd": 200.00,
            "pct_of_buffer": 36.7,
            "purpose": "Scaling from 4→8 projects, Neo4j growth, MacinCloud overages",
            "trigger": "Auto — tracked via cost_tracking table",
        },
        "elastic_spike": {
            "usd": 200.00,
            "pct_of_buffer": 36.7,
            "purpose": "Perplexity Pro queries, Opus War Room sessions, long-context usage",
            "trigger": "Auto — Budget Governor AMBER tier draws from this",
        },
        "incident_reserve": {
            "usd": 100.00,
            "pct_of_buffer": 18.4,
            "purpose": "Unexpected API price increases, free-tier breaches, emergency debug",
            "trigger": "Manual — requires /admin budget_override",
        },
        "unallocated": {
            "usd": 44.70,
            "pct_of_buffer": 8.2,
            "purpose": "Rounding buffer and future allocation",
            "trigger": "N/A",
        },
    },
}
# Verification: 200.00 + 200.00 + 100.00 + 44.70 = $544.70 ✓
```

| 5 | AI: Claude Opus 4.6 (Strategist) | Pay-as-you-go | $5.75 | 21.56 | N/A (pay-per-token) | $5/$25 per M tokens [V1] |

| | **TOTAL BASELINE** | | **$255.30** | **$957.38** | | |

**Free-Tier Assumptions:** Services listed as $0 are free within documented limits only. If any free-tier service approaches 80% of its limit, a Telegram alert fires. Limits: Cloud Run (2M req/mo), Cloud Scheduler (3 jobs), GitHub Actions (2,000 min/mo), Firebase Spark (1GB/10GB), Cloudflare (basic outbound only, no Argo/Zero Trust). Breaking these limits introduces costs not in the baseline.

#### §1.4.2 Budget Summary

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| Monthly baseline | 957.38 SAR ($255.30) — from `BUDGET_CONFIG` |
| With 15% buffer | 1,100.98 SAR ($293.60) |
| Monthly ceiling | 3,000.00 SAR ($800.00) |
| Buffer remaining | 2,042.63 SAR ($544.70) — 68.1% |
| Buffer absorbs | Neo4j growth, Opus War Room sessions, premium Perplexity queries, Local Mode failures requiring Cloud fallback, FlutterFlow price changes, MacinCloud overage, free-tier breaches |

#### §1.4.3 Cost Per Project

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| Fixed costs (Neo4j + Supabase + FlutterFlow + DNS + Apple Dev) | $179.75/month ÷ 4 = $44.94/project |
| Variable costs (AI + Mac + UI-TARS) | $75.55/month ÷ 4 = $18.89/project |
| Total cost per project | ~$63.83 = ~239.35 SAR |
| Revenue breakeven (at 500 SAR/app) | 1.9 projects/month |

**Per-Project Cost Disclaimer (ADR-048):** Cost-per-project ($63.83) assumes 4 projects/month baseline. At lower throughput, fixed-cost absorption increases:

| Throughput | Cost/Project | Multiplier vs. Baseline |
|-----------|------------:|:-----------------------:|
| 1 project/month | ~$198.64 | 3.1× |
| 2 projects/month | ~$127.77 | 2.0× |
| 3 projects/month | ~$95.80 | 1.5× |
| **4 projects/month (baseline)** | **~$63.83** | **1.0×** |
| 8 projects/month | ~$41.36 | 0.65× |
| 12 projects/month | ~$33.85 | 0.53× |

Fixed costs ($179.75) are constant regardless of throughput. At higher throughput, variable costs scale but fixed costs amortize further. Buffer segments (`BUDGET_BUFFER_SEGMENTS`) accommodate scaling costs.

#### §1.4.4 Research Circuit Breaker Budget

Each AI role/phase has a differentiated budget cap:

| Role/Phase | Max Per-Project | Covers |
|-----------|----------------:|--------|
| Scout Research | $2.00 | Perplexity lookups — market research, regulation, docs |
| Strategist Planning | $5.00 | Opus strategic decisions — architecture, legal, stack selection |
| Design Engine | $10.00 | Sonnet design generation + mock iterations |
| CodeGen Engineer | $25.00 | Sonnet code generation — most expensive phase |
| Testing/QA | $8.00 | Haiku analysis + test execution retries |
| Deploy/Release | $5.00 | Deploy tooling + build retries |
| Legal Guardian | $3.00 | Legal document generation |
| War Room Debug | $15.00 | Emergency debug sessions (L1–L3) |
| **Per-Project Cap** | **$25.00** | Hard cap across all roles for one project |
| **Monthly Global Cap** | **$80.00** | Hard cap across all projects per month |

If any role hits its phase limit, the pipeline pauses and sends:

```
⚠️ [ROLE] budget for [phase] reached $[LIMIT] (spent: $[ACTUAL]).
Options: [✅ Authorize +$X] [⏭️ Skip] [⏸️ Pause] [❌ Cancel]
```

#### §1.4.5 What Is NOT in the Budget (and Why)

| Item | Status | Reason |
|------|--------|--------|
| OpenAI API keys | Optional ($0 default) | Claude cascade + Perplexity cover all roles; OpenAI retained as optional GUI Supervisor alternative |
| Google Workspace | Removed | Not needed |
| FlutterFlow extra seats | Removed | Single seat sufficient |
| Ngrok paid tier | Not needed ($0) | Cloudflare Tunnel is free and superior |
| Unity Pro | Not needed ($0) | Unity free tier covers <$100K revenue |
| Xcode | $0 | Free with Apple Developer account |
| Android Studio | $0 | Free |

### §1.5 Architecture Overview

```
OPERATOR (Telegram)                    PIPELINE
─────────────────                      ────────
Brief ──→  S0 Intake ──→ S1 Legal ──→ S2 Blueprint  ──→ S3 CodeGen
           [Copilot    (Haiku)   (Opus+         (Opus: Stack     (Sonnet:
            or                    Perplexity     Selector +        code for
            Autopilot]            continuous)    Design Mocks)     chosen stack)
                                       │              │                │
                    ┌──────────────────┘              │                │
                    │ CONTINUOUS LEGAL THREAD          │                │
                    │  (Opus monitors S1→S8)           │                │
                    └──────────────────┐              │                │
                                       ▼              ▼                ▼
S8 Handoff  ←──  S7 Verify  ←──  S6 Deploy  ←──  S5 Test  ←──  S4 Build  ←──┘
(Haiku)          (Haiku)          (APIs)          (Sonnet)       (3-Mode:
    │                                                             Cloud/Local/
    ▼                                                             Hybrid)
Telegram
delivery
+ legal docs
+ time-travel ID
```

**Three-Mode Execution (S4):**

```
           ┌── Cloud Mode (default): GitHub Actions + MacinCloud
           │
S4 Build ──┼── Local Mode: Operator's Mac via Cloudflare Tunnel
           │     (Heartbeat Monitor: 30s ping)
           │     (Auto-failover to Cloud if heartbeat dies)
           │     [Failover = resume-from-last-checkpoint, NOT live state transfer]
           │
           └── Hybrid Mode: Cloud does backend deploy,
                            Local does heavy rendering/build
```

**Intelligence Doctrine:**

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                  AI ROLE ENFORCEMENT                      │
│                                                          │
│  SCOUT (Perplexity Sonar)                                │
│    READ-ONLY. Finds docs, laws, bugs, trends.            │
│    NEVER writes code. NEVER modifies files.              │
│                                                          │
│  STRATEGIST (Claude Opus 4.6)                            │
│    Plans architecture. Decides legal risk.               │
│    Manages War Room. Selects tech stack.                 │
│    NEVER writes production code directly.                │
│                                                          │
│  ENGINEER (Claude Sonnet 4.5)                            │
│    Writes code. Generates files. Applies fixes.          │
│    Takes orders from Strategist.                         │
│    Uses intel from Scout.                                │
│                                                          │
│  QUICK FIX (Claude Haiku 4.5)                            │
│    Syntax fixes. Lightweight validation.                 │
│    War Room Level 1 only.                                │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### §1.6 Technology Decision Records (ADR-001 through ADR-017)

| ADR | Decision | Rationale |
|-----|----------|-----------|
| ADR-001 | Mutable PipelineState (`frozen=False`) | LangGraph nodes modify state via direct assignment |
| ADR-002 | `transition_to()` as only stage-change method | Centralized validation |
| ADR-003 | Supabase Pro, not Free tier | Free tier pauses after 7 days |
| ADR-004 | Single FlutterFlow seat maintained even for non-FF projects | $80/month overhead justified by having FF available when needed; cancel after 3 months of zero FF usage |
| ADR-005 | Model role enforcement via code contracts | Each AI call specifies `role=Role.SCOUT/STRATEGIST/ENGINEER`; wrong role raises `RoleViolationError` |
| ADR-006 | GCP Secret Manager for all credentials | Single source of truth |
| ADR-007 | OmniParser V2 + UI-TARS 1.5 for GUI automation | macOS-native perception + action |
| ADR-008 | Polyglot stack selection at S2 (not pre-determined) | Each project gets the optimal stack based on requirements, not a one-size-fits-all assumption |
| ADR-009 | Perplexity Sonar as dedicated Scout | Web-grounded, citation-rich research with $2/phase budget cap; cheaper and more current than GPT-4o for research |
| ADR-010 | Claude Opus 4.6 as Strategist (not GPT-4o) | Frontier reasoning + 1M context beta for full-project awareness; higher cost justified by quality of architectural decisions |
| ADR-011 | Cloudflare Tunnel for Local Mode | Free, outbound-only, no port forwarding needed, auto-reconnect |
| ADR-012 | Zero sudo — user-space only | All installs via npx, venv, rbenv, `--user`; prevents root-level crashes and permission escalation |
| ADR-013 | Time-travel via unified snapshots | State = (Git hash) + (Supabase snapshot) + (Neo4j node state); enables `/restore State_#N` |
| ADR-014 | Continuous legal thread (not gate-only) | Legal checks at S1 (initial), S2 (design), S3 (code), S4 (build), S6 (deploy), S8 (handoff); catches compliance drift |
| ADR-015 | Per-role circuit breaker | Per-role/phase limits ($2–$25) replace flat $2/phase; prevents runaway costs while allowing legitimate expensive phases |
| ADR-016 | No Apple/Google portal UI login | App Store Airlock: API-only (Service Accounts). On failure: upload binary to Telegram for human drag-and-drop |
| ADR-017 | 3.75 SAR/USD fixed rate | SAMA peg since 1986 |

---

| V9 | Perplexity request fees | Sonar: $5/$8/$12; Pro: $6/$10/$14 | Confirmed per official pricing page | docs.perplexity.ai | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V10 | MacinCloud PAYG | ~$1/hr, prepaid blocks | $1/hr PAYG, prepaid 25-hour or 7-day blocks | macincloud.com | 2026-02-19 | ADJUSTED — prepaid min is 25hrs not 30hrs; budget uses $30/mo |
| V11 | MacinCloud credit expiry | 60 calendar days after last usage | 60 days after last login | support.macincloud.com | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V12 | Telegram Bot API file limit | 50MB for sendDocument | 50MB for bots | core.telegram.org/bots/api | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V13 | FlutterFlow Growth Plan | $80/mo for API+Git export | $80/mo Growth plan (Standard discontinued) | flutterflow.io/pricing | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V14 | Supabase Pro | $25/mo | $25/mo | supabase.com/pricing | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V15 | Neo4j AuraDB Free | $0/mo graph queries (GA); vector = Public Preview | Free tier exists; vector in Public Preview; GA timeline unconfirmed | neo4j.com/cloud/aura | 2026-02-19 | MATCH — correct to default pgvector |
| V16 | USD→SAR exchange rate | 3.75 fixed | 3.75 SAR/USD (SAMA peg since 1986) | — | 2026-02-19 | MATCH |
| V17 | Apple Developer Program | $99/year | $99/year; required for TestFlight + App Store | developer.apple.com | 2026-02-19 | MATCH — amortized $8.25/mo into `BUDGET_CONFIG` |

**Ledger Policy:** Any cost figure in this spec that cannot be traced to this ledger or to `BUDGET_CONFIG` is a defect. Re-verify all pricing quarterly or before any production deployment.
