## Part 5: State Persistence, Mother Memory, Secrets, Architecture Delta & Budget Governor

---

### §2.9 State Persistence & Time Travel

#### §2.9.1 Transactional Triple-Write + Snapshot

Every stage completion triggers a triple-write: Supabase current state, Supabase append-only snapshot, and GitHub versioned commit. If any write fails, all successful writes are rolled back. A SHA-256 checksum links the Supabase and Git copies; restore operations validate this checksum before proceeding.

```python
import hashlib

class SnapshotWriteError(Exception):
    """Raised when triple-write fails and is rolled back."""
    pass

async def persist_state(state: PipelineState) -> int:
    """
    Transactional triple-write: Supabase current + Supabase snapshot + GitHub.
    Added rollback on partial failure + snapshot checksum.
    """
    state.snapshot_id = (state.snapshot_id or 0) + 1
    state.updated_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
    state_json = state.model_dump_json()
    snapshot_id = state.snapshot_id
    results = {"supabase_current": False, "supabase_snapshot": False, "git": False}

    try:
        # Write 1: Supabase current state (upsert)
        await supabase_client.table("pipeline_states").upsert({
            "project_id": state.project_id,
            "current_stage": state.current_stage.value,
            "snapshot_id": snapshot_id,
            "selected_stack": state.selected_stack.value if state.selected_stack else None,
            "execution_mode": state.execution_mode.value,
            "state_json": json.loads(state_json),
            "updated_at": state.updated_at,
        }).execute()
        results["supabase_current"] = True

        # Write 2: Supabase snapshots (append-only for time-travel)
        await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots").insert({
            "project_id": state.project_id,
            "snapshot_id": snapshot_id,
            "stage": state.current_stage.value,
            "state_json": json.loads(state_json),
            "git_commit_hash": None,
            "checksum": None,       # Backfilled after all writes succeed
            "created_at": state.updated_at,
        }).execute()
        results["supabase_snapshot"] = True

        # Write 3: GitHub (versioned)
        commit = await github_commit_file(
            repo=f"factory/{state.project_id}",
            path=f"state/snapshot_{snapshot_id:04d}_{state.current_stage.value}.json",
            content=state_json,
            message=f"Snapshot #{snapshot_id} at {state.current_stage.value}",
        )
        results["git"] = True

        # All three writes succeeded — compute + store checksum
        supabase_hash = hashlib.sha256(state_json.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]
        git_sha = commit["sha"]
        checksum = hashlib.sha256(
            f"{git_sha}:{supabase_hash}:{snapshot_id}".encode()
        ).hexdigest()

        await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots").update({
            "git_commit_hash": git_sha,
            "checksum": checksum,
        }).eq("project_id", state.project_id).eq(
            "snapshot_id", snapshot_id
        ).execute()

        return snapshot_id

    except Exception as e:
        # Rollback any successful writes
        if results["supabase_snapshot"]:
            await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots").delete().eq(
                "project_id", state.project_id
            ).eq("snapshot_id", snapshot_id).execute()

        if results["supabase_current"]:
            # Revert to previous snapshot
            state.snapshot_id = snapshot_id - 1
            state.updated_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()

        if results["git"]:
            # Git commits are harder to roll back; mark snapshot invalid
            pass

        # Mark snapshot as INVALID in audit log
        await supabase_client.table("audit_log").insert({
            "operator_id": "system",
            "project_id": state.project_id,
            "action": "snapshot_write_failed",
            "details": {"snapshot_id": snapshot_id, "error": str(e), "partial_writes": results},
        }).execute()

        raise SnapshotWriteError(
            f"Triple write failed: {e}. Partial writes rolled back: {results}"
        )
```

**Triple-write semantics:**

| Write | Target | Purpose | Rollback |
|-------|--------|---------|----------|
| 1 | Supabase `pipeline_states` | Current state (upsert) — fast read for dashboard | Revert `snapshot_id` to `n-1` |
| 2 | Supabase `state_snapshots` | Append-only history for time-travel | Delete row with `snapshot_id = n` |
| 3 | GitHub repo | Versioned JSON file — auditable, diff-able | Mark invalid (Git commits not auto-rolled back) |

**Checksum:** `SHA256(git_sha:supabase_hash_16:snapshot_id)` — links the Git commit to the Supabase snapshot. Validated on restore to detect corruption or partial writes.

#### §2.9.2 Time-Travel Restore

```python
class ChecksumMismatchError(Exception):
    pass

async def restore_state(project_id: str, target_snapshot_id: int) -> PipelineState:
    """
    Restore factory to a specific snapshot.

    Restores: pipeline state JSON + repository code.
    Masks:    Neo4j — sets _hidden=true on post-snapshot nodes (does NOT delete).
    Does NOT restore: database schema (Supabase DDL is forward-only).
    """
    snapshot = await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots") \
        .select("*").eq("project_id", project_id) \
        .eq("snapshot_id", target_snapshot_id).single().execute()

    if not snapshot.data:
        raise ValueError(f"Snapshot #{target_snapshot_id} not found")

    data = snapshot.data

    # Validate snapshot checksum before restore
    if data.get("checksum"):
        state_json = json.dumps(data["state_json"])
        supabase_hash = hashlib.sha256(state_json.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]
        expected = hashlib.sha256(
            f"{data.get('git_commit_hash', '')}:{supabase_hash}:{target_snapshot_id}".encode()
        ).hexdigest()
        if expected != data["checksum"]:
            # Partial Restore Warning — require operator confirmation
            raise ChecksumMismatchError(
                f"Snapshot #{target_snapshot_id} checksum mismatch. "
                f"State may be inconsistent. Operator confirmation required via Telegram."
            )

    state = PipelineState.model_validate(data["state_json"])

    # Restore Git
    if data.get("git_commit_hash"):
        await github_reset_to_commit(
            repo=f"factory/{project_id}", commit_sha=data["git_commit_hash"],
        )

    # Hide Neo4j nodes created after this snapshot (mask, not delete)
    await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (n) WHERE n.project_id = $pid AND n.created_at > $snap_time
        SET n:PostSnapshot, n._hidden = true
    """, {"pid": project_id, "snap_time": data["created_at"]})

    # Update current state
    state.snapshot_id = target_snapshot_id
    await persist_state(state)

    await send_telegram_message(
        state.operator_id,
        f"⏪ Time travel complete.\n"
        f"Restored to: Snapshot #{target_snapshot_id}\n"
        f"Stage: {state.current_stage.value}\n"
        f"Reply /continue to resume.",
    )
    return state
```

**Restore scope:**

| System | Restore behavior |
|--------|-----------------|
| Pipeline state (Supabase) | Full restore from snapshot JSON |
| Code repository (GitHub) | `git reset --hard` to snapshot commit SHA |
| Knowledge graph (Neo4j) | Post-snapshot nodes get `_hidden=true` label (NOT deleted) |
| Database schema (Supabase DDL) | **Not restored** — DDL is forward-only; operator must handle manually |

**Neo4j masking rationale:** Deleting Neo4j nodes would destroy cross-project learning data. Instead, nodes created after the restore point are labeled `:PostSnapshot` with `_hidden=true`. Queries filter these out. The Janitor Agent (§2.10.2) archives `PostSnapshot` nodes older than 30 days.

#### §2.9.3 Supabase Schema for Snapshots

```sql
CREATE TABLE state_snapshots (
    id             BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    project_id     TEXT NOT NULL,
    snapshot_id    INTEGER NOT NULL,
    stage          TEXT NOT NULL,
    state_json     JSONB NOT NULL,
    git_commit_hash TEXT,
    checksum       TEXT,
    created_at     TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(project_id, snapshot_id)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_snapshots_project ON state_snapshots(project_id, snapshot_id);

ALTER TABLE pipeline_states
    ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS snapshot_id      INTEGER,
    ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS selected_stack   TEXT,
    ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS execution_mode   TEXT DEFAULT 'cloud';
```

---

### §2.10 Mother Memory v2 (Self-Healing Knowledge Graph)

Mother Memory is a Neo4j knowledge graph that stores cross-project learning, regulatory decisions, design patterns, component success/failure rates, and store policy rejection history. It is "self-healing" via the Janitor Agent, which runs every 6 hours to archive rotting data.

#### §2.10.1 Node Types & Constraints

```cypher
-- Stack patterns: successful patterns per tech stack
CREATE CONSTRAINT stack_pattern_id IF NOT EXISTS
    FOR (sp:StackPattern) REQUIRE sp.id IS UNIQUE;

-- Graveyard: archived/dead data (Janitor sends here)
CREATE CONSTRAINT graveyard_id IF NOT EXISTS
    FOR (g:Graveyard) REQUIRE g.id IS UNIQUE;

-- Design DNA: color palettes, typography, layout patterns
CREATE CONSTRAINT design_dna_id IF NOT EXISTS
    FOR (d:DesignDNA) REQUIRE d.id IS UNIQUE;

-- Legal document templates
CREATE CONSTRAINT legal_doc_id IF NOT EXISTS
    FOR (ld:LegalDocTemplate) REQUIRE ld.id IS UNIQUE;

-- Store policy rejection tracking
CREATE CONSTRAINT store_policy_id IF NOT EXISTS
    FOR (sp:StorePolicyEvent) REQUIRE sp.id IS UNIQUE;
-- Node: StorePolicyEvent {id, platform, rejection_reason, date, project_id,
--        resolution, guidelines_version}
-- Relationship: (:Project)-[:REJECTED_BY]->(:StorePolicyEvent)
-- Queried by Preflight Compliance Gate at S1 to warn about known rejection patterns.

-- [FIX-27] Handoff Intelligence Pack documentation
CREATE CONSTRAINT handoff_doc_id IF NOT EXISTS
    FOR (hd:HandoffDoc) REQUIRE (hd.project_id, hd.doc_type) IS UNIQUE;
-- Node: HandoffDoc {project_id, program_id, stack, app_category, doc_type,
--        filename, content, generated_at, permanent}
-- Relationship: (:Project)-[:HAS_HANDOFF_DOC {doc_type: str}]->(:HandoffDoc)
-- Janitor-exempt (permanent = true). Created by S8; queried by S2 for
-- cross-project learning and by Operator for direct use.

CREATE INDEX stack_pattern_stack IF NOT EXISTS
    FOR (sp:StackPattern) ON (sp.stack);
CREATE INDEX handoff_doc_category IF NOT EXISTS
    FOR (hd:HandoffDoc) ON (hd.app_category);
```

**Node type summary:**

| Node Label | Purpose | Created by | Queried by |
|------------|---------|-----------|------------|
| StackPattern | Successful code patterns per stack | S3 Codegen (on success) | S3 Codegen (reuse) |
| Component | Individual components with success/failure counts | S3–S5 | S3 (reuse), Janitor (prune) |
| DesignDNA | Color palettes, typography, layout patterns | S2 Blueprint | S2 (design consistency) |
| LegalDocTemplate | Legal document templates | S8 Handoff | S1 Legal, S8 DocuGen |
| StorePolicyEvent | App Store / Play Store rejection history | S7 Verify (on rejection) | S1 Preflight (warn about known issues) |
| RegulatoryDecision | KSA regulatory classification decisions | S1 Legal | S1 Legal (precedent lookup) |
| Pattern | General patterns (architecture, error resolution) | War Room (on resolution) | War Room (prior art lookup) |
| HandoffDoc | Operator handoff documentation (runbooks, guides, service maps) per project [FIX-27] | S8 Handoff (FIX-27) | S2 (cross-project reference), Operator (direct use) |
| Graveyard | Archived dead data (via Janitor) | Janitor Agent | Not queried (archived) |
| PostSnapshot | Nodes hidden by time-travel restore | restore_state() | Not queried (_hidden=true) |
| WarRoomEvent | War Room session logs | War Room (§2.2.8) | War Room (cross-project learning) |

#### §2.10.2 Janitor Agent (6-Hour Cycle)

```python
async def janitor_agent_cycle() -> dict:
    """
    Runs every 6 hours. Finds rotting data → _GRAVEYARD → :Archived.
    """
    results = {"archived_count": 0, "categories": {}}

    # 1. Broken components (0 successes, 2+ failures, >14 days)
    broken = await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (c:Component)
        WHERE c.success_count = 0 AND c.failure_count > 2
          AND c.created_at < datetime() - duration({days: 14})
        RETURN c.id AS id
    """)
    for r in broken:
        await neo4j_run("""
            MATCH (c:Component {id: $id})
            REMOVE c:Component SET c:Graveyard:Archived
            SET c.archived_at = datetime()
            SET c.archived_reason = 'Broken: 0 successes, 2+ failures'
        """, {"id": r["id"]})
    results["categories"]["broken"] = len(broken)
    results["archived_count"] += len(broken)

    # 2. Expired regulatory decisions (>6 months)
    expired = await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (d:RegulatoryDecision)
        WHERE d.date < datetime() - duration({months: 6})
        RETURN d.id AS id
    """)
    for r in expired:
        await neo4j_run("""
            MATCH (d:RegulatoryDecision {id: $id})
            REMOVE d:RegulatoryDecision SET d:Graveyard:Archived
            SET d.archived_at = datetime()
        """, {"id": r["id"]})
    results["categories"]["expired_decisions"] = len(expired)
    results["archived_count"] += len(expired)

    # 3. Orphaned patterns (no project references, >30 days)
    orphans = await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (p:Pattern) WHERE NOT (p)<-[:USED_PATTERN]-(:Project)
          AND p.created_at < datetime() - duration({days: 30})
        RETURN p.id AS id
    """)
    for r in orphans:
        await neo4j_run("""
            MATCH (p:Pattern {id: $id})
            REMOVE p:Pattern SET p:Graveyard:Archived
            SET p.archived_at = datetime()
        """, {"id": r["id"]})
    results["categories"]["orphans"] = len(orphans)
    results["archived_count"] += len(orphans)

    # 4. PostSnapshot orphans (>30 days, from time-travel)
    post = await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (n:PostSnapshot) WHERE n._hidden = true
          AND n.created_at < datetime() - duration({days: 30})
        RETURN n.id AS id
    """)
    for r in post:
        await neo4j_run("""
            MATCH (n {id: $id}) WHERE n:PostSnapshot
            REMOVE n:PostSnapshot SET n:Graveyard:Archived
            SET n.archived_at = datetime()
        """, {"id": r["id"]})
    results["categories"]["post_snapshot"] = len(post)
    results["archived_count"] += len(post)

    return results
```

**Janitor rules:**

| Category | Criteria | Action |
|----------|----------|--------|
| Broken components | 0 successes, 2+ failures, older than 14 days | Archive to `:Graveyard` |
| Expired regulatory decisions | Older than 6 months | Archive to `:Graveyard` |
| Orphaned patterns | No `:USED_PATTERN` relationship, older than 30 days | Archive to `:Graveyard` |
| PostSnapshot nodes | `_hidden=true`, older than 30 days | Archive to `:Graveyard` |
| HandoffDoc nodes [FIX-27] | `permanent = true` | **SKIP** — never archive or prune (high-value operator knowledge) |

**Archiving vs. deleting:** The Janitor never deletes nodes. It relabels them as `:Graveyard:Archived` with an `archived_at` timestamp and `archived_reason`. This preserves audit trails and allows manual recovery if needed. Standard queries exclude `:Graveyard` nodes via label filtering. `HandoffDoc` nodes are exempt from this process entirely — they are permanent and never enter the Graveyard.

---

### §2.11 Secrets Management

All secrets are stored in GCP Secret Manager and injected as environment variables at Cloud Run startup. The pipeline validates their presence on boot.

```python
REQUIRED_SECRETS = [
    "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY",        # Opus 4.6, Sonnet 4.5, Haiku 4.5
    "PERPLEXITY_API_KEY",       # Sonar + Sonar Pro (Scout)
    "SUPABASE_URL",
    "SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY",
    "NEO4J_URI",
    "NEO4J_PASSWORD",
    "GITHUB_TOKEN",
    "TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN",
    "GCP_PROJECT_ID",
    "FLUTTERFLOW_API_TOKEN",
    "UI_TARS_ENDPOINT",
    "UI_TARS_API_KEY",
    "APPLE_ID",
    "APP_SPECIFIC_PASSWORD",
    "FIREBASE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT",
    # Optional: "OPENAI_API_KEY" (GUI Supervisor independence)
]
```

The `OPENAI_API_KEY` is optional — it enables GUI Supervisor independence from Anthropic if needed. All other secrets are required. Missing secrets cause the pipeline to refuse startup with an explicit error listing the missing keys.

---

### §2.12 Architecture Delta Summary

This table summarizes the architectural changes from v3.6 (the previous FlutterFlow-only pipeline) to the current polyglot architecture.

| Component | v3.6 (Previous) | Current Architecture | Change Type |
|-----------|-----------------|---------------------|-------------|
| PipelineState | FF-specific fields | Polymorphic `project_metadata` + `TechStack` enum | Breaking |
| Stack selection | Assumed FlutterFlow | Stack Selector Brain (Opus) at S2 | New |
| Execution modes | Cloud only | Cloud / Local / Hybrid + Heartbeat Monitor | New |
| AI model roles | Ad-hoc per stage | Hardcoded role contracts with enforcement | New |
| Error handling | Simple retry loops | War Room L1→L2→L3 escalation | Upgraded |
| Legal compliance | Single gate at S1 | Continuous parallel thread S1→S8 | Upgraded |
| State persistence | Dual-write | Triple-write (current + snapshots + Git) | Upgraded |
| Time travel | None | Unified Snapshot + `/restore` command | New |
| Mother Memory | Basic graph + quarterly prune | Graph + Janitor (6-hour cycle) + `:Archived` | Upgraded |
| Security | Informal no-sudo | Code-enforced User-Space Enforcer | Formalized |
| Budget safety | Buffer awareness | Per-phase circuit breaker | New |
| Budget governance | None | 4-tier graduated degradation (GREEN/AMBER/RED/BLACK) | New |

---

### §2.14 Budget Governor (ADR-044)

#### §2.14.1 Problem Statement

The circuit breaker (§3.6) provides a hard stop at 100% of the monthly budget ceiling. The 80% monitoring alert (§8.4) warns the operator. But there is no defined behavior for the 80–100% range — a cliff edge where the pipeline operates normally at 79% and halts abruptly at 100%. The Budget Governor fills this gap with graduated degradation.

**Kill switch:** Set `BUDGET_GOVERNOR_ENABLED=false` to restore exact pre-Governor behavior (80% alert + hard stop at cap). Default is `true`.

#### §2.14.2 Tier Definitions

| Tier | Range | Behavior | Model Impact | Operator Alert |
|------|-------|----------|-------------|----------------|
| GREEN | 0–79% of monthly cap | Normal operation | All models at default per `MODEL_CONFIG` | None |
| AMBER | 80–94% of monthly cap | Degraded operation | Strategist: Opus 4.6→Opus 4.5; Engineer: context capped at 100K; Scout: prefer cached results (live only if cache >24h stale) | Telegram: budget %, remaining USD, degradation active |
| RED | 95–99% of monthly cap | Intake blocked | AMBER degradations + no new S0 Intake accepted (queue held); in-flight projects continue degraded | Telegram: budget %, new projects blocked, `/admin budget_override` to force |
| BLACK | 100% of monthly cap | Hard stop | Existing circuit breaker fires; all pipeline activity halted | Telegram: budget exhausted, pipeline halted, reset date |

#### §2.14.3 Implementation

```python
import os
from enum import Enum
from datetime import datetime, timezone

BUDGET_GOVERNOR_ENABLED = os.getenv("BUDGET_GOVERNOR_ENABLED", "true").lower() == "true"

class BudgetTier(str, Enum):
    GREEN = "GREEN"   # 0-79%: normal
    AMBER = "AMBER"   # 80-94%: degrade models
    RED   = "RED"     # 95-99%: block new intake
    BLACK = "BLACK"   # 100%: hard stop

# Thresholds are percentages of BUDGET_CONFIG hard_ceiling_usd ($800).
# Using integer cents to prevent floating-point comparison errors.
BUDGET_TIER_THRESHOLDS = {
    BudgetTier.AMBER: 80,    # 80% of ceiling = $640.00
    BudgetTier.RED:   95,    # 95% of ceiling = $760.00
    BudgetTier.BLACK: 100,   # 100% of ceiling = $800.00
}

class BudgetGovernor:
    """
    Graduated budget degradation.
    Called before every call_ai() invocation. Determines current tier
    and applies appropriate model/context degradation.

    Precedence chain (ADR-043/044):
      operator MODEL_OVERRIDE > Budget Governor > MODEL_CONFIG default.
    If operator has set a MODEL_OVERRIDE, Governor logs a warning but
    does NOT override the override — preserving operator agency.
    """
    def __init__(self):
        # All calculations in integer cents to avoid float errors
        self.ceiling_cents = int(BUDGET_CONFIG["hard_ceiling_usd"] * 100)
        self._last_tier = BudgetTier.GREEN
        self._last_alert_tier = None  # Track to avoid duplicate alerts

    def get_current_spend_cents(self) -> int:
        """Read current month's total spend from Supabase cost_tracking table.
        Returns total in integer cents."""
        # Implementation reads from Supabase; sum of all cost entries
        # for current calendar month in cents.
        pass

    def determine_tier(self, spend_cents: int) -> BudgetTier:
        """Determine budget tier based on current spend."""
        pct = (spend_cents * 100) // self.ceiling_cents if self.ceiling_cents > 0 else 0
        if pct >= BUDGET_TIER_THRESHOLDS[BudgetTier.BLACK]:
            return BudgetTier.BLACK
        elif pct >= BUDGET_TIER_THRESHOLDS[BudgetTier.RED]:
            return BudgetTier.RED
        elif pct >= BUDGET_TIER_THRESHOLDS[BudgetTier.AMBER]:
            return BudgetTier.AMBER
        else:
            return BudgetTier.GREEN

    async def check(
        self,
        role: AIRole,
        state: PipelineState,
        contract: RoleContract,
    ) -> RoleContract:
        """
        Called before every call_ai(). Returns a (possibly degraded) contract.
        - GREEN: return contract unchanged
        - AMBER: downgrade model, reduce context
        - RED:   block new S0 intake, allow in-flight with AMBER degradations
        - BLACK: raise BudgetExhaustedError (circuit breaker)
        """
        if not BUDGET_GOVERNOR_ENABLED:
            return contract  # Kill switch: exact pre-Governor behavior

        spend_cents = self.get_current_spend_cents()
        tier = self.determine_tier(spend_cents)
        remaining_usd = (self.ceiling_cents - spend_cents) / 100
        spend_pct = (spend_cents * 100) // self.ceiling_cents if self.ceiling_cents > 0 else 0

        # Alert on tier transition (not on every call)
        if tier != self._last_alert_tier:
            await self._send_tier_alert(tier, spend_pct, remaining_usd, state)
            self._last_alert_tier = tier

        self._last_tier = tier

        if tier == BudgetTier.BLACK:
            # Hard stop — existing circuit breaker behavior
            raise BudgetExhaustedError(
                f"Monthly budget exhausted ({spend_pct}% of "
                f"${self.ceiling_cents/100:.2f}). "
                f"Pipeline halted. Resets on {self._next_month_date()}."
            )

        if tier == BudgetTier.RED:
            # Block new intake
            if state.current_stage == Stage.S0_INTAKE:
                raise BudgetIntakeBlockedError(
                    f"Budget at {spend_pct}%. New project intake blocked. "
                    f"In-flight projects continue with degraded models. "
                    f"Override: /admin budget_override"
                )
            # In-flight continues with AMBER degradation (fall through)

        if tier in (BudgetTier.AMBER, BudgetTier.RED):
            # Apply model degradation
            contract = self._degrade_contract(role, contract, tier)

        return contract  # GREEN: unchanged

    def _degrade_contract(
        self, role: AIRole, contract: RoleContract, tier: BudgetTier
    ) -> RoleContract:
        """Apply AMBER/RED degradation to role contract."""
        degraded = RoleContract(**{**contract.__dict__})

        if role == AIRole.STRATEGIST:
            # Opus 4.6 → Opus 4.5 (same family, similar capability)
            if degraded.model == "claude-opus-4-6":
                degraded = RoleContract(**{**degraded.__dict__, "model": "claude-opus-4-5-20250929"})
                log.info(f"AMBER: Strategist downgraded to opus-4.5")

        elif role == AIRole.ENGINEER:
            # Context window capped: max_output_tokens halved
            degraded = RoleContract(**{
                **degraded.__dict__,
                "max_output_tokens": min(degraded.max_output_tokens, 8192)
            })
            log.info(f"AMBER: Engineer context capped at 100K")

        elif role == AIRole.SCOUT:
            # Prefer cached results — handled in call_perplexity_safe()
            # Flag added for call_perplexity_safe() to check
            log.info(f"AMBER: Scout preferring cached results")

        # QUICK_FIX: unchanged (already cheapest model)

        return degraded

    async def _send_tier_alert(
        self, tier: BudgetTier, pct: int, remaining: float, state: PipelineState
    ):
        """Send Telegram alert on tier transition."""
        alerts = {
            BudgetTier.AMBER: (
                f"🟡 Budget at {pct}% — AMBER mode active\n"
                f"Remaining: ${remaining:.2f}\n"
                f"Strategist downgraded to opus-4.5\n"
                f"Engineer context capped at 100K\n"
                f"Scout preferring cached results"
            ),
            BudgetTier.RED: (
                f"🔴 Budget at {pct}% — RED mode active\n"
                f"Remaining: ${remaining:.2f}\n"
                f"New projects BLOCKED. In-flight continues degraded.\n"
                f"Override: /admin budget_override"
            ),
            BudgetTier.BLACK: (
                f"⛔ Monthly budget EXHAUSTED ({pct}%)\n"
                f"Pipeline HALTED. All activity stopped.\n"
                f"Resets on {self._next_month_date()}"
            ),
            BudgetTier.GREEN: (
                f"🟢 Budget back to GREEN ({pct}%)\n"
                f"Normal operation restored."
            ),
        }
        msg = alerts.get(tier)
        if msg:
            await notify_operator(state, NotificationType.BUDGET_ALERT, msg)

    def _next_month_date(self) -> str:
        now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
        if now.month == 12:
            return f"{now.year + 1}-01-01"
        return f"{now.year}-{now.month + 1:02d}-01"


class BudgetExhaustedError(Exception):
    """BLACK tier — monthly budget fully consumed."""
    pass

class BudgetIntakeBlockedError(Exception):
    """RED tier — new project intake blocked."""
    pass

# Singleton governor instance
budget_governor = BudgetGovernor()
```

#### §2.14.4 Integration with `call_ai()`

The Budget Governor is checked after the MODEL_OVERRIDE check (ADR-043) but before role boundary enforcement:

```
call_ai() execution order:
  1. Load role contract from ROLE_CONTRACTS
  2. Check MODEL_OVERRIDE → if valid, override contract.model
  3. BudgetGovernor.check() → may degrade contract OR raise error
  4. Enforce role boundaries (RoleViolationError)
  5. Route to provider (Anthropic or Perplexity)
  6. Track cost against circuit breaker (per-role limits)
```

**Precedence (ADR-043/044):** If an operator has set `STRATEGIST_MODEL_OVERRIDE=claude-opus-4-6` but the Governor is in AMBER mode wanting to downgrade to opus-4.5, the operator override wins. The Governor logs a warning: "Override active during AMBER budget mode. Burn rate elevated." This preserves operator agency while maintaining visibility.

#### §2.14.5 `/admin budget_override` Command

Available when Budget Governor is in RED tier (95–99%). Allows operator to force-accept new projects despite RED tier.

```python
async def handle_budget_override(operator_id: str, state: PipelineState):
    """Requires explicit confirmation. Logged with disclaimer."""
    await bot.send_message(operator_id,
        "⚠️ Budget Override Request\n\n"
        "You are requesting to accept new projects while budget is at RED tier (>95%).\n"
        "This may cause the pipeline to hit BLACK tier (100%) and halt mid-project.\n\n"
        "To confirm, reply: /admin budget_override_confirm\n"
        "To cancel, reply: /admin budget_override_cancel"
    )

async def handle_budget_override_confirm(operator_id: str, state: PipelineState):
    """Log override and temporarily allow intake."""
    await audit_log(operator_id, "budget_override", {
        "tier": "RED",
        "spend_pct": budget_governor._last_tier,
        "timestamp": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        "disclaimer": "Operator accepted risk of BLACK tier halt.",
    })
    # Override lasts for current session (until next tier recalculation)
    budget_governor._last_alert_tier = None  # Reset to allow re-alerting
    await bot.send_message(operator_id,
        "✅ Budget override active. New projects will be accepted.\n"
        "⚠️ Budget may hit BLACK tier and halt mid-project."
    )
```

## Part 6: Intelligence Doctrine — Eyes vs. Hands

This part defines the AI intelligence layer: how the pipeline's four AI roles discover, decide, create, and repair. The Scout sees; the Strategist plans; the Engineer builds; Quick Fix patches.

---

### §3.1 The Perplexity Sonar Integration (The Scout)

The Scout is the pipeline's only internet-facing research agent. It uses Perplexity's Sonar API for web-grounded answers with citations. No other AI role may access the internet.

#### §3.1.1 API Client

```python
import httpx, json
from typing import Optional

class PerplexityClient:
    """
    Perplexity Sonar API client — the Scout's sole interface.

    Models:
      - sonar:               $1/$1   per M tokens (fast, lightweight search)
      - sonar-pro:           $3/$15  per M tokens (deep, multi-search)
      - sonar-reasoning-pro: $3/$15  per M tokens (complex reasoning)

    Pricing: Request fees vary by search_context_size (Low/Medium/High),
    not a flat per-request fee. Budget uses Medium as baseline.
    Auto-selects model based on query complexity via MODEL_CONFIG.
    """
    BASE_URL = "https://api.perplexity.ai/chat/completions"

    def __init__(self, api_key: str):
        self.api_key = api_key
        self.total_cost = 0.0

    async def search(
        self,
        query: str,
        use_pro: bool = False,
        max_tokens: int = 2048,
        search_context: str = "low",
    ) -> tuple[str, float]:
        """Execute a Sonar search. Returns (response_text, cost_usd)."""
        model = "sonar-pro" if use_pro else "sonar"
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30) as client:
            resp = await client.post(
                self.BASE_URL,
                headers={
                    "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
                    "Content-Type": "application/json",
                },
                json={
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": query}],
                    "max_tokens": max_tokens,
                    "web_search_options": {"search_context_size": search_context},
                },
            )
            resp.raise_for_status()
            data = resp.json()

            text = data["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]
            citations = data.get("citations", [])
            usage = data.get("usage", {})
            input_tokens = usage.get("prompt_tokens", 0)
            output_tokens = usage.get("completion_tokens", 0)

            if use_pro:
                cost = (input_tokens / 1e6 * 3.0) + (output_tokens / 1e6 * 15.0)
            else:
                cost = (input_tokens / 1e6 * 1.0) + (output_tokens / 1e6 * 1.0)

            # Search fees vary by search_context_size (Low/Medium/High).
            # Actual cost is included in API response usage.
            # Budget estimate uses Medium mode.
            self.total_cost += cost
            return text, cost
```

#### §3.1.2 Scout Auto-Select (Sonar vs. Sonar Pro)

The Scout automatically selects Sonar Pro for complex regulatory, debugging, or market analysis queries:

```python
SONAR_PRO_TRIGGERS = [
    "regulation", "compliance", "legal", "PDPL", "CST", "SAMA",
    "ministry of commerce", "license", "permit",
    "root cause", "dependency conflict", "breaking change",
    "migration guide", "deprecated",
    "competing apps", "market analysis", "trending", "design trends",
]

def should_use_pro(query: str) -> bool:
    query_lower = query.lower()
    return any(trigger in query_lower for trigger in SONAR_PRO_TRIGGERS)
```

#### §3.1.3 Scout Usage Across Pipeline Stages

| Stage | Scout Purpose | Model Tier | Example Query |
|-------|--------------|------------|---------------|
| S0 | Market research, competitor apps | Sonar | "Top to-do list apps KSA 2026 features" |
| S1 | KSA regulatory lookups | Sonar Pro | "PDPL requirements for food delivery app KSA" |
| S2 | Framework comparison, API docs, design trends | Sonar/Pro | "Best React Native vs FlutterFlow for e-commerce 2026" |
| S3 | Library docs, known bugs | Sonar | "flutter_secure_storage latest version breaking changes" |
| S4 | Build error research (War Room L2) | Sonar Pro | "Xcode 16 code signing error ITMS-90901 fix" |
| S5 | Test framework docs | Sonar | "Expo EAS test runner configuration" |
| S6 | Deployment docs | Sonar | "Firebase Hosting deploy custom domain steps" |
| S8 | App Store guidelines check | Sonar Pro | "Apple App Store review guidelines payment processing 2026" |

---

### §3.2 The Strategist (Claude Opus 4.6)

#### §3.2.1 Strategist Responsibilities

The Strategist never writes code and never searches the web. It receives Scout intel and makes decisions.

| Context | Responsibilities |
|---------|-----------------|
| S1 Legal | Classify data sensitivity, determine regulatory bodies, block/flag features, set payment mode |
| S2 Blueprint | Select tech stack, design architecture, approve design, generate Blueprint |
| War Room L3 | Map dependency tree, identify root cause, order cleanup commands, produce rewrite plan |
| Continuous Legal | Decide if legal failures are blocking, classify MoC licensing, review DocuGen, final sign-off |

#### §3.2.2 Strategist Cost Control

Opus 4.6 ($5/$25 per M tokens) is used sparingly with per-context call limits:

```python
STRATEGIST_USAGE_LIMITS = {
    "S1_LEGAL":     {"max_calls": 2, "max_input_tokens": 8000},
    "S2_BLUEPRINT": {"max_calls": 3, "max_input_tokens": 16000},
    "WAR_ROOM_L3":  {"max_calls": 2, "max_input_tokens": 16000},
    "LEGAL_CHECKS": {"max_calls": 1, "max_input_tokens": 4000},
}

async def call_strategist_with_limits(
    prompt: str, state: PipelineState, context: str, action: str = "plan_architecture",
) -> str:
    limits = STRATEGIST_USAGE_LIMITS.get(context, {"max_calls": 1, "max_input_tokens": 8000})
    context_key = f"strategist_{context}_calls"
    current_calls = state.phase_costs.get(context_key, 0)

    if current_calls >= limits["max_calls"]:
        if action != "decide_legal":
            # Fallback to Engineer for non-critical tasks
            return await call_ai(
                role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
                prompt=f"[Delegated from Strategist] {prompt}",
                state=state, action="general",
            )
        # Legal decisions: allow one extra with warning
        await send_telegram_message(
            state.operator_id,
            f"⚠️ Strategist budget for '{context}' exceeded. Allowing critical legal call.",
        )

    if len(prompt) > limits["max_input_tokens"] * 4:
        prompt = prompt[:limits["max_input_tokens"] * 4] + "\n[TRUNCATED]"

    response = await call_ai(role=AIRole.STRATEGIST, prompt=prompt, state=state, action=action)
    state.phase_costs[context_key] = current_calls + 1
    return response
```

**Fallback behavior:** When the Strategist exhausts its call budget for a context, non-legal tasks are delegated to the Engineer (Sonnet 4.5) with a `[Delegated from Strategist]` prefix. Legal decisions always get an extra call with operator warning.

---

### §3.3 The Engineer (Claude Sonnet 4.5)

#### §3.3.1 Polyglot Code Generation

The Engineer generates code differently based on the selected stack. Each stack has a dedicated generator function producing the correct file structure:

```python
async def generate_code(state: PipelineState, blueprint: Blueprint) -> dict[str, str]:
    """Generate code for the selected stack. Returns {file_path: content}."""
    stack = blueprint.selected_stack

    # Query Mother Memory for reusable patterns
    reusable = await query_mother_memory(
        stack=stack.value,
        screens=[s["name"] for s in blueprint.screens],
        auth_method=blueprint.auth_method,
    )

    generators = {
        TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW:    _generate_flutterflow,
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE:   _generate_react_native,
        TechStack.SWIFT:          _generate_swift,
        TechStack.KOTLIN:         _generate_kotlin,
        TechStack.UNITY:          _generate_unity,
        TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND: _generate_python_backend,
    }
    return await generators[stack](state, blueprint, reusable)
```

**React Native generator (representative example):**

```python
async def _generate_react_native(state, blueprint, reusable) -> dict[str, str]:
    scaffold = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
        prompt=(
            f"Generate React Native Expo project.\n\n"
            f"Blueprint:\n{blueprint.model_dump_json(indent=2)}\n\n"
            f"Reusable components:\n{json.dumps(reusable)}\n\n"
            f"Return JSON: {{file_path: file_content}}\n"
            f"Required: package.json, app.json, App.tsx, "
            f"src/navigation/AppNavigator.tsx, "
            f"src/screens/[Name]Screen.tsx per screen, "
            f"src/services/api.ts, src/services/auth.ts, "
            f"src/store/index.ts, firestore.rules"
        ),
        state=state, action="write_code",
    )
    files = json.loads(scaffold)

    # Validate all screens have files
    for screen in blueprint.screens:
        key = f"src/screens/{screen['name']}Screen.tsx"
        if key not in files:
            code = await call_ai(
                role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
                prompt=f"Generate React Native screen: {json.dumps(screen)}\n"
                       f"Design: {blueprint.color_palette}\nReturn TSX only.",
                state=state, action="write_code",
            )
            files[key] = code
    return files
```

**Swift generator:**

```python
async def _generate_swift(state, blueprint, reusable) -> dict[str, str]:
    scaffold = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
        prompt=(
            f"Generate SwiftUI iOS project.\n\n"
            f"Blueprint:\n{blueprint.model_dump_json(indent=2)}\n\n"
            f"Return JSON: {{file_path: file_content}}\n"
            f"Required: Package.swift, Sources/App/[App]App.swift, "
            f"Sources/Views/[Screen]View.swift per screen, "
            f"Sources/Models/[Model].swift, Sources/Services/APIService.swift, "
            f"Sources/Services/AuthService.swift\n"
            f"Min iOS 16.0. SwiftUI + async/await."
        ),
        state=state, action="write_code",
    )
    return json.loads(scaffold)
```

The Kotlin, Unity, Python Backend, and FlutterFlow generators follow the same pattern: Engineer prompt with stack-specific file structure requirements. The FlutterFlow generator reuses the v3.6 YAML generation logic.

### §3.4 The Design Engine (Hunter-Gatherer)

#### §3.4.1 Autonomous Vibe Check

Replaces manual templates with AI-driven design discovery at S2. The pipeline researches trending apps, extracts design DNA, refines for KSA audience (RTL + WCAG), and validates through the Grid Enforcer.

```python
async def vibe_check(state: PipelineState, requirements: dict) -> dict:
    """
    1. Scout finds trending apps in same category
    2. Scout extracts Design DNA (colors, fonts, spacing)
    3. Strategist refines for KSA audience + RTL + WCAG
    4. Grid Enforcer validates
    """
    category = requirements.get("app_category", "general")

    # Step 1+2: Scout discovers trends and extracts DNA
    trend_research = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.SCOUT,
        prompt=(
            f"Find top 5 trending {category} apps in KSA and globally 2026.\n"
            f"For each: primary colors (hex), typography, layout patterns, spacing, visual style.\n"
            f"Focus on apps similar to: {requirements.get('app_description', '')}"
        ),
        state=state, action="general",
    )

    design_dna = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.SCOUT,
        prompt=(
            f"From these trends:\n{trend_research}\n\n"
            f"Extract unified Design DNA as JSON:\n"
            f'{{"color_palette": {{"primary":"#hex","secondary":"#hex","accent":"#hex",'
            f'"background":"#hex","surface":"#hex","text_primary":"#hex",'
            f'"text_secondary":"#hex","error":"#hex"}},'
            f'"typography": {{"heading_font":"...","body_font":"...","size_base":16,"scale_ratio":1.25}},'
            f'"spacing": {{"unit":4,"page_padding":16,"card_padding":12,"element_gap":8}},'
            f'"layout_patterns": ["cards","bottom_nav"],'
            f'"visual_style": "minimal"}}'
        ),
        state=state, action="general",
    )
    design = json.loads(design_dna)

    # Step 3: Strategist refines
    refined = await call_strategist_with_limits(
        prompt=(
            f"Refine for KSA audience:\n{json.dumps(design, indent=2)}\n\n"
            f"App: {requirements.get('app_description', '')}\n"
            f"Ensure: RTL support, WCAG AA contrast (4.5:1), 4px grid, "
            f"KSA cultural preferences.\nReturn refined JSON."
        ),
        state=state, context="S2_BLUEPRINT", action="plan_architecture",
    )

    # Step 4: Grid Enforcer
    return grid_enforcer_validate(json.loads(refined))
```

#### §3.4.2 Grid Enforcer (Pydantic Validators)

```python
class DesignSpec(BaseModel):
    """Validated design spec. Enforces 4px grid + WCAG contrast. 'No Ugly Apps.'"""
    color_palette: dict
    typography: dict
    spacing: dict
    layout_patterns: list[str]
    visual_style: str

    @model_validator(mode="after")
    def enforce_4px_grid(self):
        for key, value in self.spacing.items():
            if isinstance(value, (int, float)) and key != "unit":
                if value % 4 != 0:
                    self.spacing[key] = max(4, round(value / 4) * 4)
        return self

    @model_validator(mode="after")
    def enforce_wcag_contrast(self):
        bg = self.color_palette.get("background", "#FFFFFF")
        for text_key in ("text_primary", "text_secondary"):
            text_color = self.color_palette.get(text_key, "#000000")
            if contrast_ratio(bg, text_color) < 4.5:
                self.color_palette[text_key] = darken_until_contrast(bg, text_color, 4.5)
        return self

    @model_validator(mode="after")
    def enforce_font_sizes(self):
        base = self.typography.get("size_base", 16)
        if base < 12:
            self.typography["size_base"] = 12
        elif base % 2 != 0:
            self.typography["size_base"] = base + 1
        return self
```

**Contrast utility functions:**

```python
def hex_to_rgb(h: str) -> tuple:
    h = h.lstrip("#")
    return tuple(int(h[i:i+2], 16) for i in (0, 2, 4))

def relative_luminance(rgb: tuple) -> float:
    def lin(c): c = c/255; return c/12.92 if c <= 0.03928 else ((c+0.055)/1.055)**2.4
    r, g, b = [lin(c) for c in rgb]
    return 0.2126*r + 0.7152*g + 0.0722*b

def contrast_ratio(h1: str, h2: str) -> float:
    l1, l2 = relative_luminance(hex_to_rgb(h1)), relative_luminance(hex_to_rgb(h2))
    return (max(l1,l2)+0.05) / (min(l1,l2)+0.05)

def darken_until_contrast(bg: str, text: str, target: float) -> str:
    r, g, b = hex_to_rgb(text)
    for _ in range(50):
        if contrast_ratio(bg, f"#{r:02x}{g:02x}{b:02x}") >= target:
            return f"#{r:02x}{g:02x}{b:02x}"
        r, g, b = max(0,int(r*0.95)), max(0,int(g*0.95)), max(0,int(b*0.95))
    return "#000000"

def grid_enforcer_validate(design: dict) -> dict:
    return DesignSpec.model_validate(design).model_dump()
```

#### §3.4.3 Pre-Build Visual Mocks (3 Mocks to Telegram)

Before code generation begins, the pipeline generates 3 HTML mock variations, captures them as PNG screenshots, and sends them to the operator via Telegram for selection.

```python
async def generate_visual_mocks(
    state: PipelineState, blueprint: Blueprint, design: dict
) -> tuple:
    """Generate 3 HTML mock variations, capture as PNG, send to Telegram."""
    mock_paths = []
    key_screens = blueprint.screens[:2]
    variations = [
        {"name": "Clean Minimal", "hint": "Max whitespace, thin borders, subtle shadows"},
        {"name": "Bold Modern",   "hint": "Vivid colors, rounded corners, card-heavy"},
        {"name": "Professional",  "hint": "Structured grid, muted tones, data-dense"},
    ]

    for i, var in enumerate(variations):
        html = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt=(
                f"Generate single HTML file mocking these screens:\n"
                f"{json.dumps(key_screens)}\n"
                f"Design: {json.dumps(design)}\n"
                f"Style: {var['name']} — {var['hint']}\n"
                f"Mobile viewport 375x812. RTL support. All spacing multiples of 4px.\n"
                f"Return ONLY HTML with inline CSS."
            ),
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
        html_path = f"/tmp/mock_{state.project_id}_{i}.html"
        png_path = f"/tmp/mock_{state.project_id}_{i}.png"
        await write_file(html_path, html)
        await execute_command(enforce_user_space(
            f"npx puppeteer-cli screenshot {html_path} {png_path} --viewport 800x900"
        ))
        mock_paths.append(png_path)

    state.design_mocks = mock_paths

    if state.autonomy_mode == AutonomyMode.COPILOT:
        await send_telegram_mocks(
            state.operator_id, mocks=mock_paths,
            labels=[v["name"] for v in variations],
            message=(
                f"🎨 Design options for {blueprint.app_name}:\n\n"
                f"1️⃣ Clean Minimal\n2️⃣ Bold Modern\n3️⃣ Professional\n"
                f"4️⃣ Custom: Describe what you want\n\nReply 1-4."
            ),
        )
        selection = await wait_for_operator_reply(
            state.operator_id, timeout=3600, default="1"
        )
        return mock_paths, int(selection) - 1 if selection.isdigit() else 0
    else:
        return mock_paths, 0  # Autopilot picks first (Clean Minimal)
```

### §3.5 DocuGen Module (The Corporate Secretary)

#### §3.5.1 Document Types

```python
DOCUGEN_TEMPLATES = {
    "privacy_policy":           {"required_for": ["all"]},
    "terms_of_use":             {"required_for": ["all"]},
    "merchant_agreement":       {"required_for": ["marketplace", "e-commerce"]},
    "driver_contract":          {"required_for": ["delivery", "transport", "ride-hailing"]},
    "data_processing_agreement":{"required_for": ["saas", "b2b"]},
}
```

#### §3.5.2 Generation Flow

DocuGen uses all three AI roles in sequence: Scout researches → Strategist structures → Engineer writes.

```python
async def generate_legal_documents(
    state: PipelineState, blueprint: Blueprint
) -> dict[str, str]:
    """Generate all required legal docs. Scout researches →
    Strategist structures → Engineer writes."""
    business_model = blueprint.business_model or "general"
    documents = {}

    for doc_type, template in DOCUGEN_TEMPLATES.items():
        required = template["required_for"]
        if "all" not in required and business_model not in required:
            continue

        # Scout: current KSA requirements
        intel = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.SCOUT,
            prompt=f"KSA legal requirements for {doc_type.replace('_',' ')} "
                   f"for {business_model} app. Include PDPL, SAMA, MoC. 2025-2026 changes.",
            state=state, action="general",
        )

        # Strategist: legal structure
        structure = await call_strategist_with_limits(
            prompt=f"Draft structure: {doc_type.replace('_',' ')}\n"
                   f"Business: {business_model}\nApp: {blueprint.app_name}\n"
                   f"Research:\n{intel}\n\nReturn JSON with sections and key clauses.",
            state=state, context="LEGAL_CHECKS", action="decide_legal",
        )

        # Engineer: full document
        doc = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt=f"Write complete {doc_type.replace('_',' ')}.\n"
                   f"Structure:\n{structure}\n"
                   f"App: {blueprint.app_name}\nBusiness: {business_model}\n"
                   f"Requirements: Professional legal language, Arabic+English bilingual, "
                   f"PDPL compliant, KSA jurisdiction. Include [EFFECTIVE_DATE] and "
                   f"[COMPANY_NAME] placeholders. Return Markdown.",
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
        documents[doc_type] = doc

    state.legal_documents = documents
    return documents
```

**Legal disclaimer (mandatory):** All AI-generated legal documents (Terms of Service, Privacy Policy, EULA, Merchant Agreement, etc.) are DRAFTS requiring mandatory human legal review before publication or use. The pipeline flags all legal outputs with `REQUIRES_LEGAL_REVIEW` status and sends a Telegram reminder:

> "⚠️ Legal documents generated for [APP_NAME]. These are AI-generated DRAFTS — not final legal instruments. Have them reviewed by a qualified KSA legal professional before publishing."

DocuGen must include citation sources for all legal claims (drawn from Scout's Perplexity research with inline citations). Claims without citations are flagged as `[UNVERIFIED]`.

---

### §3.6 Circuit Breaker Implementation

#### §3.6.1 Per-Role/Phase Enforcement

The circuit breaker tracks costs per budget category, maps AI role + stage combinations to categories, and presents the operator with 4-way decisions when limits are reached.

```python
PHASE_BUDGET_LIMITS = {
    "scout_research":     2.00,
    "strategist_planning":5.00,
    "design_engine":     10.00,
    "codegen_engineer":  25.00,
    "testing_qa":         8.00,
    "deploy_release":     5.00,
    "legal_guardian":     3.00,
    "war_room_debug":    15.00,
}

PER_PROJECT_CAP  = 25.00
MONTHLY_GLOBAL_CAP = 80.00

def _budget_category(role: AIRole, stage: str) -> str:
    if role == AIRole.SCOUT:
        return "scout_research"
    if role == AIRole.STRATEGIST:
        if "legal" in stage.lower() or "S1" in stage:
            return "legal_guardian"
        return "strategist_planning"
    if role == AIRole.ENGINEER:
        if "S3" in stage:
            return "codegen_engineer"
        if "S2" in stage:
            return "design_engine"
        if "S5" in stage:
            return "testing_qa"
        return "deploy_release"
    if role == AIRole.QUICK_FIX:
        return "war_room_debug" if "war_room" in stage.lower() else "testing_qa"
    return "scout_research"
```

**Budget trip behavior:**

```python
async def check_circuit_breaker(
    state: PipelineState, role: AIRole, cost_increment: float
) -> bool:
    """Check if cost would breach role/phase limit.
    Returns True if OK, False if tripped."""
    category = _budget_category(role, state.current_stage.value)
    limit = PHASE_BUDGET_LIMITS.get(category, 5.00)
    current = state.phase_costs.get(category, 0.0)

    if current + cost_increment > limit:
        state.circuit_breaker_triggered = True
        await send_telegram_decision(
            state.operator_id,
            message=f"⚡ [{category}] budget: ${current:.2f}/${limit:.2f}.\n"
                    f"Role: {role.value} | Stage: {state.current_stage.value}\n"
                    f"Next call: ~${cost_increment:.3f}.",
            options=[
                f"💰 Authorize additional ${limit:.2f}",
                "📋 Skip research, use existing intel",
                "⏸ Pause and review costs",
                "🛑 Cancel this phase",
            ],
        )
        response = await wait_for_operator_reply(
            state.operator_id, timeout=3600, default="2"
        )
        if response == "1":
            state.circuit_breaker_triggered = False
            return True
        elif response == "2":
            state.circuit_breaker_triggered = False
            return False
        elif response == "4":
            transition_to(state, Stage.HALTED)
            return False
    return True
```

---

### §3.7 The 4-Way Decision Matrix (Copilot Mode)

#### §3.7.1 Decision Protocol

In Copilot mode, every operator interaction presents exactly 4 options. Options 1–3 are AI recommendations. Option 4 is always custom input. In Autopilot mode, the recommended option is auto-selected.

```python
async def present_decision(
    state: PipelineState, question: str, options: list[dict],
) -> str:
    """Present 4-way decision. In Autopilot, auto-picks recommended."""
    if state.autonomy_mode == AutonomyMode.AUTOPILOT:
        for opt in options:
            if opt.get("recommended"):
                return opt["label"]
        return options[0]["label"]

    lines = [f"❓ {question}\n"]
    for i, opt in enumerate(options, 1):
        star = " ⭐" if opt.get("recommended") else ""
        desc = f"\n   {opt.get('description','')}" if opt.get("description") else ""
        lines.append(f"{i}️⃣ {star}{opt['label']}{desc}")
    lines.append(f"\n4️⃣ Custom: Type your preference or send media")

    await send_telegram_message(state.operator_id, "\n".join(lines))
    reply = await wait_for_operator_reply(
        state.operator_id, timeout=3600, default="1"
    )
    return options[int(reply)-1]["label"] if reply in ("1","2","3") else reply
```

#### §3.7.2 Decision Points

| Stage | Decision | Opt 1 (⭐ default) | Opt 2 | Opt 3 | Opt 4 |
|-------|----------|-------------------|-------|-------|-------|
| S0 | App scope | As described | Simplified MVP | Enhanced | Custom |
| S1 | Legal action | Register now | Proceed SANDBOX | Remove feature | Custom |
| S2 | Tech stack | AI pick | Alternative A | Alternative B | Custom |
| S2 | Design | Mock 1 | Mock 2 | Mock 3 | Custom |
| S4 | Exec mode | Cloud | Local | Hybrid | Custom |
| S5 | Test fail | Auto-fix | Skip non-critical | Full retry | Custom |
| Circuit | Budget | Authorize $2 | Skip research | Pause | Cancel |

---

### §3.8 Information Flow Summary

```
SCOUT (Perplexity Sonar)
  READ-ONLY — finds docs, laws, bugs, trends
  │
  Intel (citations, facts)
  │
  ▼
STRATEGIST (Claude Opus 4.6)
  Plans, decides, manages War Room
  NEVER writes code
  │
  Plans & orders
  │
  ▼
ENGINEER (Claude Sonnet 4.5)
  Writes code, generates files, applies fixes
  NEVER makes arch/legal decisions
  │
  If error →
  ▼
QUICK FIX (Claude Haiku 4.5)
  Syntax fixes, GUI supervision
```

**Cost distribution (illustrative, per project):** Scout ~14% ($4.60), Strategist ~17% ($5.75), Engineer ~62% ($21.00), Quick Fix ~7% ($2.20). The most expensive model (Opus) is used sparingly for critical decisions only.
