## Part 7: Pipeline Stages — S0 through S3

*PART 4 of the specification (first half). Covers the Stage Execution Model and stages S0 (Intake), S1 (Legal Gate), S2 (Blueprint + Stack Selection + Design), and S3 (Code Generation).*

---

### §4.0 Stage Execution Model

Every stage follows the same wrapper pattern (from §2.7.2):

```
Pre-Legal Check → Stage Logic → Post-Legal Check → Snapshot Persist
```

Each stage node receives `PipelineState`, mutates it, and returns it. The `@pipeline_node` decorator handles legal hooks and persistence automatically. The decorator's implementation is defined in §2.7.3 (Continuous Legal Thread).

---

### §4.1 S0 — INTAKE

**Role:** Haiku (Quick Fix) — lightweight extraction. **Purpose:** Parse operator's natural language request into structured requirements. **Cost Target:** <$0.10.

```python
@pipeline_node(Stage.S0_INTAKE)
async def s0_intake_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """
    S0: Intake — parse operator message into structured requirements.
    Input:  Telegram message (text + optional media: screenshots, voice, documents)
    Output: state.s0_output = structured requirements dict
    Uses Haiku (cheapest) because intake is extraction, not reasoning.
    """
    raw_input = state.project_metadata.get("raw_input", "")
    attachments = state.project_metadata.get("attachments", [])

    # ── Step 1: Extract requirements (Haiku) ──
    extraction_prompt = (
        f"Extract structured app requirements from this request.\n\n"
        f"Request: {raw_input}\n\n"
        f"Return JSON:\n"
        f'{{\n'
        f'  "app_name": "short_name",\n'
        f'  "app_description": "1-2 sentence description",\n'
        f'  "app_category": "e-commerce|social|productivity|health|education|'
        f'finance|delivery|games|utility|other",\n'
        f'  "target_platforms": ["ios", "android", "web"],\n'
        f'  "features_must": ["list of must-have features"],\n'
        f'  "features_nice": ["list of nice-to-have features"],\n'
        f'  "target_audience": "who uses this app",\n'
        f'  "monetization": "free|ads|subscription|one-time|'
        f'marketplace_commission|none",\n'
        f'  "language_primary": "ar|en|both",\n'
        f'  "has_payments": true/false,\n'
        f'  "has_user_accounts": true/false,\n'
        f'  "has_location": true/false,\n'
        f'  "has_camera": true/false,\n'
        f'  "has_notifications": true/false,\n'
        f'  "has_realtime": true/false,\n'
        f'  "estimated_complexity": "simple|medium|complex"\n'
        f'}}'
    )
    result = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.QUICK_FIX, prompt=extraction_prompt,
        state=state, action="general",
    )
    requirements = json.loads(result)

    # ── Step 2: Scout quick market scan (optional, if budget allows) ──
    can_research = await check_circuit_breaker(state, 0.02)
    if can_research:
        market_intel = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.SCOUT,
            prompt=(
                f"Quick scan: What are the top 3 competing apps for "
                f"'{requirements['app_description']}' in Saudi Arabia? "
                f"Key features they offer?"
            ),
            state=state, action="general",
        )
        requirements["market_intel"] = market_intel

    # ── Step 3: Copilot confirmation ──
    if state.autonomy_mode == AutonomyMode.COPILOT:
        selection = await present_decision(
            state=state,
            question=f"I understood your app as: {requirements['app_description']}",
            options=[
                {"label": "Correct, proceed", "recommended": True},
                {"label": "Simplify to MVP",
                 "description": f"Only: {requirements['features_must'][:3]}"},
                {"label": "Add more features",
                 "description": "I'll describe additions"},
            ],
        )
        if "simplify" in selection.lower():
            requirements["features_must"] = requirements["features_must"][:3]
            requirements["features_nice"] = []
            requirements["estimated_complexity"] = "simple"
        elif selection not in ("Correct, proceed", "1"):
            # Custom input — re-extract with additional context
            requirements["operator_additions"] = selection

    state.s0_output = requirements
    return state
```

---

### §4.2 S1 — LEGAL GATE

**Roles:** Scout (research) + Strategist (decisions). **Purpose:** Initial legal classification, regulatory mapping, feature risk assessment. **Cost Target:** <$0.80.

```python
@pipeline_node(Stage.S1_LEGAL)
async def s1_legal_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """
    S1: Legal Gate — classify data sensitivity, map regulatory bodies,
    assess feature-level risk.
    This is the INITIAL legal assessment. The Continuous Legal Thread
    (§2.7.3) continues monitoring S2→S8.
    """
    requirements = state.s0_output

    # ── Step 1: Scout researches applicable KSA regulations ──
    legal_research = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.SCOUT,
        prompt=(
            f"What KSA regulations apply to this app?\n\n"
            f"App: {requirements['app_description']}\n"
            f"Category: {requirements['app_category']}\n"
            f"Has payments: {requirements.get('has_payments', False)}\n"
            f"Has user accounts: {requirements.get('has_user_accounts', False)}\n"
            f"Has location: {requirements.get('has_location', False)}\n\n"
            f"Check: PDPL (data protection), CST (telecom/app registration), "
            f"SAMA (financial), NDMO (data governance), NCA (cybersecurity), "
            f"SDAIA (AI governance), Ministry of Commerce (business licensing).\n"
            f"Return specific requirements per regulatory body."
        ),
        state=state, action="general",
    )

    # ── Step 2: Strategist classifies and decides ──
    legal_decision = await call_strategist_with_limits(
        prompt=(
            f"LEGAL CLASSIFICATION.\n\n"
            f"App requirements:\n{json.dumps(requirements, indent=2)}\n\n"
            f"KSA regulatory research:\n{legal_research}\n\n"
            f"Classify and decide:\nReturn JSON:\n"
            f'{{\n'
            f'  "data_classification": "public|internal|confidential|restricted",\n'
            f'  "regulatory_bodies": ["CST", "SAMA", ...],\n'
            f'  "payment_mode": "SANDBOX",\n'
            f'  "feature_risk_assessment": [\n'
            f'    {{"feature": "...", "risk": "clear|flagged|blocked", '
            f'"reason": "...", "action": "..."}}\n'
            f'  ],\n'
            f'  "required_legal_docs": ["privacy_policy", "terms_of_use", ...],\n'
            f'  "required_licenses": ["ministry_of_commerce_cr" or "none"],\n'
            f'  "cross_border_data": true/false,\n'
            f'  "sama_sandbox_required": true/false,\n'
            f'  "overall_risk": "low|medium|high",\n'
            f'  "proceed": true/false,\n'
            f'  "blocking_issues": ["list of issues that must be resolved"]\n'
            f'}}'
        ),
        state=state, context="S1_LEGAL", action="decide_legal",
    )
    legal_output = json.loads(legal_decision)

    # ── Step 3: Handle blocked features ──
    blocked_features = [
        f for f in legal_output.get("feature_risk_assessment", [])
        if f["risk"] == "blocked"
    ]
    if blocked_features and state.autonomy_mode == AutonomyMode.COPILOT:
        blocked_names = [f["feature"] for f in blocked_features]
        await present_decision(
            state=state,
            question=f"Legal blocked features: {blocked_names}",
            options=[
                {"label": "Remove blocked features and proceed",
                 "recommended": True},
                {"label": "Apply for required licenses first"},
                {"label": "Proceed anyway (SANDBOX only)"},
            ],
        )

    # ── Step 4: Handle overall proceed/halt ──
    if not legal_output.get("proceed", True):
        state.legal_halt = True
        state.legal_halt_reason = (
            f"S1 Legal Gate: Blocking issues: "
            f"{legal_output.get('blocking_issues', ['Unknown'])}"
        )

    state.s1_output = legal_output

    # ── Step 5 (v5.4.1 Patch 7): Preflight App Store Compliance Gate ──
    # Non-blocking — adds warnings for operator awareness, does not halt pipeline.
    preflight_warnings = await preflight_store_compliance(state)
    if preflight_warnings:
        state.s1_output["compliance_warnings"] = preflight_warnings
        state.warnings.extend(preflight_warnings)
        await notify_operator(
            state.operator_id, NotificationType.BUDGET_ALERT,
            f"⚠️ App Store Preflight found {len(preflight_warnings)} "
            f"potential issues:\n"
            + "\n".join(
                f"  • {w['rule']}: {w['detail']}"
                for w in preflight_warnings[:5]
            ),
        )

    # ── Step 6 (v5.5 — FIX-06): Strict Compliance Enforcement (ADR-045) ──
    # When STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE=true and ComplianceGateResult has blockers
    # with confidence >0.7: HALT pipeline. Operator must /force_continue.
    # Default STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE=false: advisory only (no change from v5.4.2).
    if STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE and preflight_warnings:
        gate_result = ComplianceGateResult(
            blockers=[
                w for w in preflight_warnings
                if w.get("severity") == "high"
            ],
            warnings=[
                w for w in preflight_warnings
                if w.get("severity") != "high"
            ],
            confidence=_calculate_compliance_confidence(preflight_warnings),
            source_ids=[
                w.get("source", "unknown") for w in preflight_warnings
            ],
        )
        if gate_result.has_blockers(min_confidence=0.7):
            state.current_stage = Stage.HALTED
            state.halt_reason = (
                f"[FIX-06] Compliance blocker(s) at confidence "
                f"{gate_result.confidence:.2f}: "
                f"{gate_result.blocker_summary()}"
            )
            await notify_operator(
                state.operator_id, NotificationType.ERROR,
                f"🛑 Pipeline HALTED: {len(gate_result.blockers)} "
                f"compliance blocker(s) found.\n"
                f"Details: {gate_result.blocker_summary()}\n"
                f"Confidence: {gate_result.confidence:.0%}\n\n"
                f"Override: /force_continue (you assume all policy risk)\n"
                f'Required text: "I accept compliance risk"',
            )
            # Pipeline waits for operator action
            return state

    return state
```

#### §4.2.1 Strict Compliance Configuration (v5.5 — FIX-06)

```python
# Default false (advisory mode, v5.4.2 behavior)
STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE = os.getenv(
    "STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE", "false"
).lower() == "true"

# Tunable if false positive rate is high
# ASSUMPTION: 0.7 is conservative (30% margin).
COMPLIANCE_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD = float(
    os.getenv("COMPLIANCE_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD", "0.7")
)

def _calculate_compliance_confidence(warnings: list[dict]) -> float:
    """Estimate confidence of compliance blockers.
    High-severity warnings from Mother Memory (past rejections) get high
    confidence. Scout-sourced guideline warnings get moderate confidence
    (guidelines may be stale).
    """
    if not warnings:
        return 0.0
    high_confidence_count = sum(
        1 for w in warnings
        if w.get("severity") == "high" and w.get("source") == "mother_memory"
    )
    total = len(warnings)
    return min(1.0, 0.5 + (high_confidence_count / total) * 0.5) if total > 0 else 0.0
```

#### §4.2.2 /force_continue Telegram Command (FIX-06)

```python
async def handle_force_continue(
    operator_id: str, confirmation_text: str, state: PipelineState
):
    """Resume pipeline from HALTED after strict compliance block.
    Requires exact text: "I accept compliance risk"
    Logs ForceComplianceOverride event for audit trail.
    Resumes pipeline from HALTED → S2.
    """
    REQUIRED_TEXT = "I accept compliance risk"
    if confirmation_text.strip() != REQUIRED_TEXT:
        await bot.send_message(
            operator_id,
            f'⚠️ /force_continue requires exact confirmation text:\n'
            f'"{REQUIRED_TEXT}"\n\n'
            f'Usage: /force_continue I accept compliance risk',
        )
        return

    # Log override for audit trail
    override_event = {
        "event_type": "ForceComplianceOverride",
        "operator_id": operator_id,
        "project_id": state.project_id,
        "timestamp": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        "blockers_overridden": state.halt_reason,
        "disclaimer": "Operator accepted all compliance risk via /force_continue.",
    }
    await audit_log(operator_id, "force_compliance_override", override_event)

    # Store in Neo4j for cross-project learning
    await mother_memory_store(
        node_type="ForceComplianceOverride",
        data=override_event, project_id=state.project_id,
    )

    # Resume: HALTED → S2_BLUEPRINT
    state.current_stage = Stage.S2_BLUEPRINT
    state.halt_reason = None
    await notify_operator(
        operator_id, NotificationType.INFO,
        f"✅ Compliance override accepted. Pipeline resumed → S2 Blueprint.\n"
        f"⚠️ Override logged to audit trail. You assume all policy risk.",
    )
    log.warning(
        f"[FIX-06] ForceComplianceOverride: operator={operator_id} "
        f"project={state.project_id} blockers={state.halt_reason}"
    )
```

#### §4.2.3 Preflight App Store Compliance (v5.4.1 Patch 7)

```python
async def preflight_store_compliance(state: PipelineState) -> list[dict]:
    """Query current Apple/Google guidelines for known rejection triggers.
    Returns compliance_warnings[] — advisory, not blocking."""
    warnings = []

    # 1. Query Mother Memory for past rejection patterns
    past_rejections = await query_store_policy_events(state.project_id)
    for rejection in past_rejections:
        warnings.append({
            "source": "mother_memory",
            "rule": rejection.get("rejection_reason", "Unknown"),
            "detail": f"Previously rejected on {rejection.get('platform')}: "
                      f"{rejection.get('resolution', 'unresolved')}",
            "severity": "high",
        })

    # 2. Scout queries current Apple guidelines for high-risk areas
    requirements = state.s0_output or {}
    app_desc = requirements.get("summary", "")
    guideline_intel = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.SCOUT,
        prompt=(
            f"Check Apple App Store Review Guidelines and Google Play policies "
            f"for potential rejection risks for this app: '{app_desc}'. "
            f"Focus on: Section 3.1.1 (In-App Purchase), Section 5.1.1 "
            f"(Data Collection), Section 4.2 (Minimum Functionality), "
            f"Section 2.1 (App Completeness). "
            f"Return ONLY a JSON array of {{rule, risk_level, recommendation}}."
        ),
        state=state, action="compliance_check",
    )
    try:
        parsed = json.loads(guideline_intel)
        for item in parsed:
            warnings.append({
                "source": "scout_guidelines",
                "rule": item.get("rule", ""),
                "detail": item.get("recommendation", ""),
                "severity": item.get("risk_level", "medium"),
            })
    except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError):
        pass  # Non-critical — guideline check is advisory

    return warnings
```

---

### §4.3 S2 — BLUEPRINT + STACK SELECTION + DESIGN

**Roles:** Scout (research) + Strategist (stack + architecture + design approval) + Engineer (mocks). **Purpose:** Select tech stack, generate Blueprint, run Vibe Check, produce visual mocks. **Cost Target:** <$1.50.

This is the largest stage — it produces the master plan consumed by S3–S8.

```python
@pipeline_node(Stage.S2_BLUEPRINT)
async def s2_blueprint_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """S2: Blueprint — Stack Selection → Architecture → Design → Visual Mocks.
    The Strategist's main stage."""
    requirements = state.s0_output
    legal_output = state.s1_output

    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 1: Stack Selection
    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    if state.autonomy_mode == AutonomyMode.COPILOT:
        selected_stack = await copilot_stack_selection(
            state, requirements, legal_output
        )
    else:
        selected_stack = await select_stack(state, requirements, legal_output)

    state.selected_stack = selected_stack

    # Initialize stack-specific metadata
    stack_meta_initializers = {
        TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW: lambda: {
            "ff_project_id": "", "ff_pages": [], "ff_collections": [],
        },
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE: lambda: {
            "package_json": {}, "entry_point": "App.tsx",
        },
        TechStack.SWIFT: lambda: {
            "xcode_project_path": "",
            "bundle_id": (
                f"com.factory."
                f"{requirements['app_name'].lower().replace(' ', '')}"
            ),
            "swift_version": "5.10",
        },
        TechStack.KOTLIN: lambda: {
            "gradle_project_path": "",
            "package_name": (
                f"com.factory."
                f"{requirements['app_name'].lower().replace(' ', '')}"
            ),
            "min_sdk": 26,
        },
        TechStack.UNITY: lambda: {
            "unity_project_path": "", "unity_version": "2022.3",
            "target_platforms": requirements.get("target_platforms", []),
        },
        TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND: lambda: {
            "framework": "fastapi", "python_version": "3.11",
            "deploy_target": "cloud_run",
        },
    }
    state.project_metadata.update(stack_meta_initializers[selected_stack]())

    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 2: Architecture Design
    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    architecture = await call_strategist_with_limits(
        prompt=(
            f"DESIGN THE APP ARCHITECTURE.\n\n"
            f"App: {requirements['app_description']}\n"
            f"Stack: {selected_stack.value}\n"
            f"Features (must): {requirements.get('features_must', [])}\n"
            f"Features (nice): {requirements.get('features_nice', [])}\n"
            f"Auth: {'required' if requirements.get('has_user_accounts') else 'none'}\n"
            f"Payments: {requirements.get('has_payments', False)}\n"
            f"Legal: {json.dumps(legal_output, indent=2)}\n\n"
            f"Return JSON Blueprint:\n"
            f'{{\n'
            f'  "screens": [{{"name":"...", "purpose":"...", '
            f'"components":["..."], "data_bindings":[{{"collection":"...","field":"..."}}]}}],\n'
            f'  "data_model": [{{"collection":"...", "fields":[{{"name":"...","type":"...",\n'
            f'    "required":true}}], "indexes":["..."]}}],\n'
            f'  "api_endpoints": [{{"path":"/api/...", "method":"GET|POST|PUT|DELETE",\n'
            f'    "auth_required":true, "description":"..."}}],\n'
            f'  "auth_method": "email|phone|social|none",\n'
            f'  "payment_mode": "{legal_output.get("payment_mode", "SANDBOX")}",\n'
            f'  "business_model": "{requirements.get("monetization", "none")}",\n'
            f'  "required_legal_docs": {legal_output.get("required_legal_docs", [])}\n'
            f'}}'
        ),
        state=state, context="S2_BLUEPRINT", action="plan_architecture",
    )
    arch = json.loads(architecture)

    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 3: Design (Vibe Check)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    design = await vibe_check(state, requirements)

    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 4: Visual Mocks
    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    mock_paths, selected_mock = await generate_visual_mocks(
        state,
        Blueprint(
            project_id=state.project_id,
            app_name=requirements.get("app_name", "untitled"),
            app_description=requirements.get("app_description", ""),
            target_platforms=requirements.get("target_platforms", ["ios", "android"]),
            selected_stack=selected_stack,
            legal_classification=legal_output.get("data_classification", "internal"),
            **arch,
        ),
        design,
    )

    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 5: Assemble Final Blueprint
    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    blueprint = Blueprint(
        project_id=state.project_id,
        app_name=requirements.get("app_name", "untitled"),
        app_description=requirements.get("app_description", ""),
        target_platforms=requirements.get("target_platforms", ["ios", "android"]),
        selected_stack=selected_stack,
        legal_classification=legal_output.get("data_classification", "internal"),
        data_residency="KSA",
        color_palette=design.get("color_palette", {}),
        typography=design.get("typography", {}),
        design_system=(
            "material3" if selected_stack != TechStack.SWIFT else "cupertino"
        ),
        stack_config=state.project_metadata,
        generated_by=["scout", "strategist"],
        **arch,
    )

    # Validate
    validate_stack_metadata(state)
    state.s2_output = blueprint.model_dump()
    state.design_mocks = mock_paths

    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 6 (v5.5 — FIX-07): Compliance Artifact Generator
    # ══════════════════════════════════════
    # Generates platform-appropriate compliance templates after stack selection.
    # Templates contain TODO markers — NOT legal documents.
    # Committed to /legal/ directory in project Git.
    await generate_compliance_artifacts(state, selected_stack, legal_output)

    return state
```

#### §4.3.1 Compliance Artifact Generator (v5.5 — FIX-07)

```python
async def generate_compliance_artifacts(
    state: PipelineState, stack: TechStack, legal_output: dict,
) -> list[str]:
    """Generate platform-appropriate compliance templates at S2.
    Artifacts are templates with TODO markers. They do NOT constitute legal
    advice. Committed to /legal/ directory in project Git.
    Returns list of generated file paths.
    """
    legal_dir = f"{state.working_directory}/legal"
    generated_files = []

    # ASSUMPTION: If /legal/ directory already exists (operator pre-created),
    # merge-not-overwrite. Existing files preserved; new templates added
    # with _template suffix.
    existing_files = set()
    if os.path.exists(legal_dir):
        existing_files = set(os.listdir(legal_dir))
    os.makedirs(legal_dir, exist_ok=True)

    # ── Common templates (all projects) ──
    pp_path = _safe_write(
        legal_dir, "privacy_policy.md", existing_files,
        PRIVACY_POLICY_TEMPLATE.format(
            app_name=state.s0_output.get("app_name", "TODO_APP_NAME"),
            company_name="TODO_COMPANY_NAME",
            regulatory_bodies=", ".join(
                legal_output.get("regulatory_bodies", ["TODO"])
            ),
            data_types="TODO: List all personal data types collected",
            retention_period="TODO: Specify data retention period",
            cross_border=legal_output.get("cross_border_data", False),
        ),
    )
    generated_files.append(pp_path)

    tos_path = _safe_write(
        legal_dir, "terms_of_service.md", existing_files,
        TERMS_OF_SERVICE_TEMPLATE.format(
            app_name=state.s0_output.get("app_name", "TODO_APP_NAME"),
            company_name="TODO_COMPANY_NAME",
            governing_law="Kingdom of Saudi Arabia",
        ),
    )
    generated_files.append(tos_path)

    # Store Submission Checklist
    checklist_path = _safe_write(
        legal_dir, "store_checklist.md", existing_files,
        _generate_store_checklist(stack, legal_output),
    )
    generated_files.append(checklist_path)

    # ── iOS-specific templates ──
    if stack in (
        TechStack.SWIFT, TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW,
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE, TechStack.UNITY,
    ):
        pm_path = _safe_write(
            legal_dir, "privacy_manifest_template.plist",
            existing_files, IOS_PRIVACY_MANIFEST_TEMPLATE,
        )
        generated_files.append(pm_path)

        ats_path = _safe_write(
            legal_dir, "ats_config_stub.plist",
            existing_files, IOS_ATS_CONFIG_TEMPLATE,
        )
        generated_files.append(ats_path)

    # ── Android-specific templates ──
    if stack in (
        TechStack.KOTLIN, TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW,
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE, TechStack.UNITY,
    ):
        ds_path = _safe_write(
            legal_dir, "data_safety_form.yaml", existing_files,
            ANDROID_DATA_SAFETY_TEMPLATE.format(
                app_name=state.s0_output.get("app_name", "TODO_APP_NAME"),
                data_types="TODO: List data categories per Google Data Safety spec",
            ),
        )
        generated_files.append(ds_path)

    # ── Non-store projects (Python backend) ──
    if stack == TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND:
        pass  # Checklist already generated above with N/A markers

    # ── Strategist review for KSA-specific regulatory requirements ──
    # ASSUMPTION: Lightweight Strategist call to flag KSA-specific additions.
    # Does NOT rewrite templates — adds TODO items.
    ksa_review = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.STRATEGIST,
        prompt=(
            f"COMPLIANCE TEMPLATE REVIEW — KSA context.\n\n"
            f"App: {state.s0_output.get('app_description', '')}\n"
            f"Stack: {stack.value}\n"
            f"Regulatory bodies: {legal_output.get('regulatory_bodies', [])}\n"
            f"Data classification: "
            f"{legal_output.get('data_classification', 'internal')}\n\n"
            f"Review the generated compliance templates and flag any ADDITIONAL "
            f"KSA-specific requirements (PDPL consent flows, SAMA sandbox, NCA "
            f"cybersecurity controls, NDMO data residency). Return JSON array of "
            f"{{requirement, template_file, action_needed}}."
        ),
        state=state, action="decide_legal",
    )
    try:
        ksa_additions = json.loads(ksa_review)
        if ksa_additions:
            ksa_path = _safe_write(
                legal_dir, "ksa_regulatory_additions.md", existing_files,
                "# KSA Regulatory Additions\n\n"
                "Generated by Strategist (Opus). Review and integrate into "
                "templates.\n\n"
                + "\n".join(
                    f"- **{a['requirement']}** → {a['template_file']}: "
                    f"{a['action_needed']}"
                    for a in ksa_additions
                ),
            )
            generated_files.append(ksa_path)
    except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError, KeyError):
        pass  # Non-critical

    # Commit to Git
    await github_commit_binary(
        project_id=state.project_id, file_path=legal_dir,
        message=f"[S2/FIX-07] Add compliance artifact templates "
                f"({len(generated_files)} files)",
    )

    state.s2_output = state.s2_output or {}
    state.s2_output["compliance_artifacts"] = generated_files
    log.info(
        f"[FIX-07] Generated {len(generated_files)} compliance artifacts in /legal/"
    )
    return generated_files

def _safe_write(
    legal_dir: str, filename: str, existing: set, content: str
) -> str:
    """Write template file. If file exists, use _template suffix to
    avoid overwriting operator-created files."""
    if filename in existing:
        base, ext = os.path.splitext(filename)
        filename = f"{base}_template{ext}"
    path = os.path.join(legal_dir, filename)
    with open(path, "w") as f:
        f.write(content)
    return path
```

#### §4.3.2 Store Submission Checklist Generator (FIX-07)

```python
def _generate_store_checklist(stack: TechStack, legal_output: dict) -> str:
    """Platform-appropriate store submission checklist."""
    is_ios = stack in (
        TechStack.SWIFT, TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW,
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE, TechStack.UNITY,
    )
    is_android = stack in (
        TechStack.KOTLIN, TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW,
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE, TechStack.UNITY,
    )
    is_backend = stack == TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND

    lines = [
        "# Store Submission Checklist",
        f"# Generated by AI Factory Pipeline v5.6 at S2",
        "",
        "⚠️ DISCLAIMER: This checklist is a starting point. "
        "It does NOT constitute legal advice.",
        "Store review policies change without notice. "
        "Operator must verify all items.",
        "",
    ]

    if is_ios:
        lines.extend([
            "## Apple App Store",
            "- [ ] Privacy manifest (NSPrivacyTracking) completed",
            "- [ ] App Transport Security exceptions documented",
            "- [ ] Privacy policy URL set in App Store Connect",
            "- [ ] TODO: In-App Purchase configured (if applicable)",
            "- [ ] TODO: App Review Information complete",
            "- [ ] TODO: Age rating configured",
            "- [ ] TODO: Export compliance answered",
            "",
        ])
    if is_android:
        lines.extend([
            "## Google Play Store",
            "- [ ] Data Safety form completed",
            "- [ ] Privacy policy URL set in Play Console",
            "- [ ] TODO: Content rating questionnaire completed",
            "- [ ] TODO: Target audience configured",
            "- [ ] TODO: App access instructions for review",
            "",
        ])
    if is_backend:
        lines.extend([
            "## Backend Only (No App Store Submission)",
            "- [N/A] App Store submission not applicable",
            "- [ ] API privacy policy accessible at /privacy",
            "- [ ] TODO: Data processing agreement if handling PII",
            "",
        ])

    lines.extend([
        "## KSA Regulatory",
        f"- [ ] Regulatory bodies: "
        f"{', '.join(legal_output.get('regulatory_bodies', ['TODO']))}",
        f"- [ ] Data classification: "
        f"{legal_output.get('data_classification', 'TODO')}",
        "- [ ] TODO: PDPL consent flows implemented",
        "- [ ] TODO: Data residency requirements verified",
    ])
    return "\n".join(lines)
```

#### §4.3.3 Template Constants (FIX-07)

These are minimal scaffolds with TODO markers, not complete legal documents:

```python
PRIVACY_POLICY_TEMPLATE = """# Privacy Policy for {app_name}
**Company:** {company_name}
**Last Updated:** TODO_DATE
**Regulatory Bodies:** {regulatory_bodies}

## 1. Data We Collect
{data_types}

## 2. How We Use Your Data
TODO: Describe data usage purposes

## 3. Data Sharing
TODO: List third parties and purposes

## 4. Data Retention
{retention_period}

## 5. Cross-Border Data Transfer
TODO: Document legal basis if cross-border transfer applies.

## 6. Your Rights (PDPL)
TODO: Document data subject rights under PDPL

## 7. Contact
TODO: Data Protection Officer contact information

---
⚠️ DISCLAIMER: This is a template generated by AI Factory Pipeline v5.6.
It requires operator review and customization.
It does NOT constitute legal advice.
"""

TERMS_OF_SERVICE_TEMPLATE = """# Terms of Service for {app_name}
**Company:** {company_name}
**Governing Law:** {governing_law}

TODO: Complete all sections below.

## 1. Acceptance of Terms
## 2. Description of Service
## 3. User Obligations
## 4. Intellectual Property
## 5. Limitation of Liability
## 6. Governing Law and Jurisdiction
## 7. Contact Information

---
⚠️ DISCLAIMER: This is a template. It does NOT constitute legal advice.
"""

IOS_PRIVACY_MANIFEST_TEMPLATE = """<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!DOCTYPE plist PUBLIC "-//Apple//DTD PLIST 1.0//EN"
  "http://www.apple.com/DTDs/PropertyList-1.0.dtd">
<plist version="1.0">
<dict>
  <key>NSPrivacyTracking</key>
  <false/><!-- TODO: Set to true if using App Tracking Transparency -->
  <key>NSPrivacyTrackingDomains</key>
  <array>
    <!-- TODO: List tracking domains if NSPrivacyTracking is true -->
  </array>
  <key>NSPrivacyCollectedDataTypes</key>
  <array>
    <!-- TODO: Add collected data type dictionaries per Apple spec -->
  </array>
  <key>NSPrivacyAccessedAPITypes</key>
  <array>
    <!-- TODO: Declare required reason APIs used -->
  </array>
</dict>
</plist>
"""

IOS_ATS_CONFIG_TEMPLATE = """<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!-- App Transport Security Configuration Stub -->
<!-- TODO: Remove exceptions before production. All connections should use HTTPS. -->
<dict>
  <key>NSAppTransportSecurity</key>
  <dict>
    <key>NSAllowsArbitraryLoads</key>
    <false/>
  </dict>
</dict>
"""

ANDROID_DATA_SAFETY_TEMPLATE = """# Google Play Data Safety Form
# App: {app_name}
# Generated by AI Factory Pipeline v5.6

data_collection:
  collects_data: true  # TODO: Verify
  data_types:
    {data_types}

data_sharing:
  shares_data: false  # TODO: Verify

data_security:
  encrypted_in_transit: true
  deletion_mechanism: true  # TODO: Implement user data deletion

# DISCLAIMER: This is a scaffold. Complete per Google Play Console requirements.
"""
```

---

### §4.4 S3 — CODE GENERATION

**Role:** Engineer (primary), Quick Fix (validation). **Purpose:** Generate all code files for the selected stack based on the Blueprint. **Cost Target:** <$3.00.

```python
@pipeline_node(Stage.S3_CODEGEN)
async def s3_codegen_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """S3: CodeGen — generate all project files for the selected stack.
    On first run: full generation from Blueprint.
    On retry (from S5 test failures): targeted fixes only.
    """
    blueprint = Blueprint.model_validate(state.s2_output)
    is_retry = state.previous_stage == Stage.S5_TEST

    if is_retry:
        # ── Targeted Fix Mode ──
        test_failures = state.s5_output.get("failures", [])
        existing_files = state.s3_output.get("generated_files", {})

        for failure in test_failures:
            file_path = failure.get("file", "unknown")
            error = failure.get("error", "unknown error")

            # War Room escalation (L1 → L2 → L3)
            result = await war_room_escalate(
                state=state, error=error,
                error_context={
                    "file_content": existing_files.get(file_path, ""),
                    "files": existing_files,
                    "failure": failure,
                },
            )
            if result["resolved"]:
                if "fix_applied" in result:
                    existing_files[file_path] = result["fix_applied"]
            else:
                state.errors.append({
                    "stage": "S3_CODEGEN",
                    "type": "unresolved_war_room",
                    "file": file_path,
                    "error": error,
                })

        state.s3_output["generated_files"] = existing_files
        return state

    # ── Full Generation Mode ──
    # Step 1: Generate code files
    files = await generate_code(state, blueprint)

    # Step 2: Generate Firestore/Supabase security rules
    if blueprint.auth_method != "none":
        rules = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt=(
                f"Generate Firestore security rules for this data model:\n"
                f"{json.dumps(blueprint.data_model, indent=2)}\n\n"
                f"Auth method: {blueprint.auth_method}\n"
                f"Requirements: Users can only read/write their own data. "
                f"Public collections (if any) are read-only for non-auth users.\n"
                f"Return ONLY the firestore.rules file content."
            ),
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
        files["firestore.rules"] = rules

    # Step 3: Generate CI/CD configuration
    ci_config = await _generate_ci_config(state, blueprint)
    files.update(ci_config)

    # Step 4: Quick Fix validation pass
    validation_errors = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.QUICK_FIX,
        prompt=(
            f"Scan these files for obvious errors (syntax, missing imports, "
            f"broken references). Stack: {blueprint.selected_stack.value}\n\n"
            f"Files:\n{json.dumps({k: v[:500] for k, v in files.items()})}\n\n"
            f"Return JSON: [{{'file': '...', 'error': '...', 'fix': '...'}}]\n"
            f"Return empty list [] if no errors found."
        ),
        state=state, action="write_code",
    )
    errors = json.loads(validation_errors)
    for error in errors:
        if error["file"] in files:
            fixed = await call_ai(
                role=AIRole.QUICK_FIX,
                prompt=(
                    f"Fix this error in {error['file']}:\n"
                    f"Error: {error['error']}\n"
                    f"Suggested fix: {error['fix']}\n\n"
                    f"Current content:\n{files[error['file']][:4000]}\n\n"
                    f"Return the corrected file content ONLY."
                ),
                state=state, action="write_code",
            )
            files[error["file"]] = fixed

    # Step 5: Store in Mother Memory
    await store_generated_components(
        state.project_id, blueprint.selected_stack, files
    )

    # Step 6 (v5.4.1 Patch 1): Ingest binary assets into generated code
    if state.brand_assets:
        files = await ingest_assets(state, blueprint, files)

    state.s3_output = {
        "generated_files": files,
        "file_count": len(files),
        "stack": blueprint.selected_stack.value,
        "validation_fixes": len(errors),
    }
    return state
```

#### §4.4.1 Asset Ingestion (v5.4.1 Patch 1)

```python
async def ingest_assets(
    state: PipelineState, blueprint: Blueprint, files: dict[str, str]
) -> dict[str, str]:
    """Download brand_assets from Supabase Storage and commit them to the
    correct platform-specific locations in the project repository."""
    stack = blueprint.selected_stack

    ASSET_PATHS = {
        TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW:    "assets/",
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE:   "src/assets/",
        TechStack.SWIFT:          "Assets.xcassets/",
        TechStack.KOTLIN:         "app/src/main/res/drawable/",
        TechStack.UNITY:          "Assets/Resources/",
        TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND: "static/assets/",
    }
    base_path = ASSET_PATHS.get(stack, "assets/")

    for asset in state.brand_assets:
        filename = asset["filename"]
        storage_url = asset["storage_url"]

        async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
            resp = await client.get(storage_url)
            binary_data = resp.content

        target_path = f"{base_path}{filename}"
        await github_commit_binary(
            repo=f"factory/{state.project_id}",
            path=target_path, content=binary_data,
            message=f"Add brand asset: {filename}",
        )

    # Update platform config to reference assets
    if stack == TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW and "pubspec.yaml" in files:
        asset_entries = "\n".join(
            f"    - assets/{a['filename']}" for a in state.brand_assets
        )
        files["pubspec.yaml"] = files["pubspec.yaml"].replace(
            "  assets:", f"  assets:\n{asset_entries}"
        )

    return files
```

#### §4.4.2 CI/CD Configuration Generation

```python
async def _generate_ci_config(
    state: PipelineState, blueprint: Blueprint
) -> dict[str, str]:
    """Generate CI/CD config files based on stack."""
    stack = blueprint.selected_stack
    files = {}

    if stack == TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW:
        files[".github/workflows/build.yml"] = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt="Generate GitHub Actions workflow for FlutterFlow project. "
                   "Steps: checkout, flutter pub get, flutter build apk, "
                   "flutter build ios --no-codesign. Return ONLY the YAML content.",
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
    elif stack == TechStack.REACT_NATIVE:
        files[".github/workflows/build.yml"] = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt="Generate GitHub Actions for Expo React Native. "
                   "Steps: checkout, npm ci, npx expo-doctor, "
                   "eas build --platform all --non-interactive. Return ONLY YAML.",
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
        files["eas.json"] = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt=f"Generate eas.json for Expo project. Bundle ID: "
                   f"{state.project_metadata.get('bundle_id', 'com.factory.app')}. "
                   f"Profiles: development, preview, production. Return ONLY JSON.",
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
    elif stack == TechStack.SWIFT:
        files[".github/workflows/build.yml"] = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt="Generate GitHub Actions for Swift/Xcode project. "
                   "Runs on macos-latest. Steps: checkout, xcodebuild -scheme App "
                   "-destination 'generic/platform=iOS' build. Return ONLY YAML.",
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
    elif stack == TechStack.KOTLIN:
        files[".github/workflows/build.yml"] = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt="Generate GitHub Actions for Android Kotlin project. "
                   "Steps: checkout, setup-java@v4 (temurin 17), "
                   "./gradlew assembleRelease. Return ONLY YAML.",
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
    elif stack == TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND:
        files[".github/workflows/deploy.yml"] = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt="Generate GitHub Actions for Python FastAPI deploy to Cloud Run. "
                   "Steps: checkout, auth to GCP, docker build, push to Artifact "
                   "Registry, gcloud run deploy. Return ONLY YAML.",
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
        files["Dockerfile"] = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt="Generate Dockerfile for Python FastAPI. Python 3.11-slim, "
                   "pip install -r requirements.txt, "
                   "uvicorn main:app --port 8080. Return ONLY Dockerfile content.",
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )

    return files
```

## Part 8: Pipeline Stages — S4 through S8

*PART 4 of the specification (second half). Covers S4 (Build), S5 (Test), Pre-Deploy Gate, S6 (Deploy), S7 (Verify), S8 (Handoff), HALT Handler, and Stage Summary.*

---

### §4.5 S4 — BUILD

**Role:** Engineer (build scripts), Quick Fix (GUI supervision). **Purpose:** Compile the project using Cloud/Local/Hybrid mode. **Cost Target:** <$0.50.

FlutterFlow + Unity require GUI automation (OmniParser + UI-TARS). All other stacks use CLI-based builds.

```python
@pipeline_node(Stage.S4_BUILD)
async def s4_build_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """
    S4: Build — compile the project using Cloud/Local/Hybrid mode.
    FlutterFlow + Unity: require GUI automation (OmniParser + UI-TARS)
    All others: CLI-based builds
    """
    blueprint = Blueprint.model_validate(state.s2_output)
    files = state.s3_output.get("generated_files", {})
    stack = blueprint.selected_stack

    exec_mgr = ExecutionModeManager(state)
    criteria = STACK_SELECTION_CRITERIA[stack]
    requires_mac = criteria["requires_macincloud"]
    requires_gui = criteria["requires_gui_automation"]

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 1: Write files to workspace
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    for file_path, content in files.items():
        await exec_mgr.execute_task({
            "name": f"write_{file_path}",
            "type": "file_write",
            "command": f"mkdir -p $(dirname {file_path}) && cat > {file_path}",
            "content": content,
        }, requires_macincloud=False)

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 2: Install dependencies
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    dep_commands = {
        TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW:    ["flutter pub get"],
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE:   ["npm ci", "npx expo install"],
        TechStack.SWIFT:          ["swift package resolve"],
        TechStack.KOTLIN:         ["./gradlew dependencies"],
        TechStack.UNITY:          [],  # Unity resolves packages internally
        TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND: ["pip install --user -r requirements.txt"],
    }
    for cmd in dep_commands.get(stack, []):
        result = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
            "name": f"deps_{stack.value}",
            "type": "dependency_install",
            "command": enforce_user_space(cmd),
        }, requires_macincloud=requires_mac)
        if result.get("exit_code", 0) != 0:
            # War Room L1 for dependency errors
            await war_room_escalate(
                state, error=result.get("stderr", ""),
                error_context={"command": cmd},
            )

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 3: Build (stack-specific)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    if requires_gui:
        build_result = await _build_gui_automated(state, blueprint, exec_mgr)
    else:
        build_result = await _build_cli(state, blueprint, exec_mgr, requires_mac)

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    # Phase 4: Collect artifacts
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    state.s4_output = {
        "build_success": build_result.get("success", False),
        "artifacts": build_result.get("artifacts", {}),
        "execution_mode": state.execution_mode.value,
        "build_duration_seconds": build_result.get("duration", 0),
        "errors": build_result.get("errors", []),
    }

    if not build_result.get("success"):
        # Attempt War Room before failing
        for error in build_result.get("errors", []):
            wr = await war_room_escalate(
                state, error=error,
                error_context={"build_output": build_result},
            )
            if wr["resolved"]:
                # Rebuild after fix
                if requires_gui:
                    build_result = await _build_gui_automated(
                        state, blueprint, exec_mgr,
                    )
                else:
                    build_result = await _build_cli(
                        state, blueprint, exec_mgr, requires_mac,
                    )
                state.s4_output["build_success"] = build_result.get(
                    "success", False
                )
                state.s4_output["artifacts"] = build_result.get("artifacts", {})
                break

    return state
```

#### §4.5.1 CLI Build Path

```python
async def _build_cli(state, blueprint, exec_mgr, requires_mac) -> dict:
    """CLI-based build for React Native, Swift, Kotlin, Python."""
    stack = blueprint.selected_stack

    build_commands = {
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE: {
            "android": (
                "npx eas build --platform android "
                "--profile preview --non-interactive"
            ),
            "ios": (
                "npx eas build --platform ios "
                "--profile preview --non-interactive"
            ),
            "web": "npx expo export --platform web",
        },
        TechStack.SWIFT: {
            "ios": (
                "xcodebuild -scheme App "
                "-destination 'generic/platform=iOS' "
                "-archivePath build/App.xcarchive archive"
            ),
        },
        TechStack.KOTLIN: {
            "android": "./gradlew assembleRelease",
        },
        TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND: {
            "web": "docker build -t app . && echo 'Docker build success'",
        },
    }

    commands = build_commands.get(stack, {})
    artifacts = {}
    errors = []

    for platform, cmd in commands.items():
        if platform in blueprint.target_platforms or platform == "web":
            result = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
                "name": f"build_{platform}",
                "type": "ios_build" if platform == "ios" else "build",
                "command": enforce_user_space(cmd),
                "timeout": 1200,  # 20 min max
            }, requires_macincloud=requires_mac and platform == "ios")

            if result.get("exit_code", 0) == 0:
                artifacts[platform] = {
                    "status": "success",
                    "output": result.get("stdout", "")[-500:],
                }
            else:
                errors.append(result.get("stderr", "")[-1000:])

    return {
        "success": len(errors) == 0,
        "artifacts": artifacts,
        "errors": errors,
    }
```

#### §4.5.2 GUI Automation Build Path

```python
async def _build_gui_automated(state, blueprint, exec_mgr) -> dict:
    """
    GUI-automated build for FlutterFlow and Unity.
    Uses the 5-layer GUI automation stack from v3.6:
      Layer 1: Planner (Sonnet) — break task into GUI steps
      Layer 2: Parser (OmniParser V2) — screenshot → element map
      Layer 3: Actor (UI-TARS 1.5) — element map → actions
      Layer 4: Executor — pyautogui/adb commands
      Layer 5: Supervisor (Haiku) — before/after verification
    """
    # Step 1: Planner generates GUI action sequence
    gui_plan = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
        prompt=(
            f"Plan the GUI automation steps for building this "
            f"{blueprint.selected_stack.value} project.\n\n"
            f"Blueprint: {json.dumps(state.s2_output, indent=2)[:4000]}\n\n"
            f"Return JSON array of steps:\n"
            f'[{{"step": 1, "action": "click|type|scroll|wait", '
            f'"target": "element description", '
            f'"value": "text to type if applicable", '
            f'"expected_result": "what should appear after"}}]'
        ),
        state=state, action="write_code",
    )
    steps = json.loads(gui_plan)
    artifacts = {}
    errors = []

    # Step 2: Execute each step via OmniParser + UI-TARS on MacinCloud
    for step in steps:
        # Capture screenshot
        screenshot = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
            "name": "capture_screenshot",
            "type": "gui_automation",
            "command": "screencapture -x /tmp/screen.png",
        }, requires_macincloud=True)

        # OmniParser: parse screenshot → element map
        element_map = await call_omniparser(
            screenshot.get("screenshot_path", "/tmp/screen.png")
        )

        # UI-TARS: decide action coordinates
        action = await call_uitars(
            element_map=element_map,
            target=step["target"],
            action_type=step["action"],
        )

        # Execute the action
        await exec_mgr.execute_task({
            "name": f"gui_step_{step['step']}",
            "type": "gui_automation",
            "command": action["command"],
        }, requires_macincloud=True)

        # Supervisor: verify step succeeded
        verify_screenshot = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
            "name": "verify_screenshot",
            "type": "gui_automation",
            "command": "screencapture -x /tmp/verify.png",
        }, requires_macincloud=True)

        verification = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.QUICK_FIX,
            prompt=(
                f"Did this GUI step succeed?\n"
                f"Expected: {step['expected_result']}\n"
                f"Compare before and after screenshots.\n"
                f"Return JSON: {{'success': true/false, 'issue': '...'}}"
            ),
            state=state, action="general",
        )
        result = json.loads(verification)
        if not result["success"]:
            errors.append(
                f"Step {step['step']}: {result.get('issue', 'unknown')}"
            )

    return {
        "success": len(errors) == 0,
        "artifacts": artifacts,
        "errors": errors,
    }
```

---

### §4.6 S5 — TEST

**Role:** Engineer (test generation + analysis), Quick Fix (lightweight checks). **Purpose:** Run automated tests, analyze results, prepare for deployment or retry. **Cost Target:** <$0.50.

```python
@pipeline_node(Stage.S5_TEST)
async def s5_test_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """
    S5: Test — generate and run tests, analyze results.
    If failures: route back to S3 for fix (max 3 retries).
    """
    blueprint = Blueprint.model_validate(state.s2_output)
    files = state.s3_output.get("generated_files", {})
    stack = blueprint.selected_stack
    exec_mgr = ExecutionModeManager(state)

    # ── Step 1: Generate test suite (if not already present) ──
    test_files_exist = any("test" in k.lower() for k in files.keys())
    if not test_files_exist:
        test_files = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
            prompt=(
                f"Generate test suite for {stack.value} project.\n\n"
                f"Blueprint screens: "
                f"{[s['name'] for s in blueprint.screens]}\n"
                f"Data model: {json.dumps(blueprint.data_model)}\n"
                f"API endpoints: {json.dumps(blueprint.api_endpoints)}\n\n"
                f"Generate:\n"
                f"- Unit tests for data models\n"
                f"- Widget/component tests for key screens\n"
                f"- Integration test for auth flow (if applicable)\n\n"
                f"Return JSON: {{file_path: file_content}}"
            ),
            state=state, action="write_code",
        )
        test_dict = json.loads(test_files)
        files.update(test_dict)
        state.s3_output["generated_files"] = files

    # ── Step 2: Run tests ──
    test_commands = {
        TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW:    "flutter test",
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE:   "npx jest --ci --json",
        TechStack.SWIFT:          "swift test",
        TechStack.KOTLIN:         "./gradlew test",
        TechStack.UNITY:          (
            "unity-editor -batchmode -runTests -testResults results.xml"
        ),
        TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND: "python -m pytest --tb=short -q",
    }
    test_cmd = test_commands.get(stack, "echo 'No test runner'")
    requires_mac = STACK_SELECTION_CRITERIA[stack]["requires_macincloud"]

    result = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
        "name": "run_tests",
        "type": "build",
        "command": enforce_user_space(test_cmd),
        "timeout": 600,
    }, requires_macincloud=requires_mac)

    # ── Step 3: Analyze results ──
    analysis = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.QUICK_FIX,
        prompt=(
            f"Analyze test results.\n\n"
            f"Exit code: {result.get('exit_code', -1)}\n"
            f"Stdout:\n{result.get('stdout', '')[-3000:]}\n"
            f"Stderr:\n{result.get('stderr', '')[-2000:]}\n\n"
            f"Return JSON:\n"
            f'{{\n'
            f'  "passed": true/false,\n'
            f'  "total_tests": N,\n'
            f'  "passed_tests": N,\n'
            f'  "failed_tests": N,\n'
            f'  "security_critical": false,\n'
            f'  "failures": [{{"file": "...", "test": "...", '
            f'"error": "...", "severity": "critical|normal"}}]\n'
            f'}}'
        ),
        state=state, action="general",
    )
    test_output = json.loads(analysis)
    state.s5_output = test_output

    return state
```

#### §4.6.1 Pre-Deploy Operator Acknowledgment Gate (v5.5 — FIX-08, ADR-046)

A mandatory confirmation gate between S5 (Test) and S6 (Deploy). Copilot mode requires an explicit `/deploy_confirm` via Telegram. Autopilot mode has a 15-minute auto-approve timer with `/deploy_cancel` escape hatch. Race condition protection via Postgres advisory lock (C6 pattern).

```python
import asyncio

async def pre_deploy_gate(state: PipelineState) -> bool:
    """[FIX-08] Called after S5 completes, before S6 starts.
    Returns True if deploy is approved, False if cancelled.
    Blocks until operator responds or timeout fires.
    """
    project_name = state.s0_output.get("app_name", state.project_id)
    stack = (
        state.selected_stack.value if state.selected_stack else "unknown"
    )
    test_summary = state.s5_output or {}
    passed = test_summary.get("passed_tests", 0)
    total = test_summary.get("total_tests", 0)
    failed = test_summary.get("failed_tests", 0)

    # Determine target stores
    target_stores = []
    if state.selected_stack in (
        TechStack.SWIFT, TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW,
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE, TechStack.UNITY,
    ):
        target_stores.append("App Store")
    if state.selected_stack in (
        TechStack.KOTLIN, TechStack.FLUTTERFLOW,
        TechStack.REACT_NATIVE, TechStack.UNITY,
    ):
        target_stores.append("Google Play")
    if state.selected_stack == TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND:
        target_stores.append("Cloud Run")
    store_str = (
        " + ".join(target_stores) if target_stores else "deployment target"
    )

    # Compliance artifact status
    compliance_artifacts = state.s2_output.get("compliance_artifacts", [])
    checklist_status = (
        f"{len(compliance_artifacts)} compliance artifacts in /legal/"
    )

    if state.autonomy_mode == AutonomyMode.COPILOT:
        # ── Copilot: require explicit confirmation ──
        await notify_operator(
            state.operator_id, NotificationType.INFO,
            f"✅ Testing complete for **{project_name}**\n\n"
            f"Platform: {stack}\n"
            f"Tests: {passed}/{total} passed ({failed} failed)\n"
            f"Target: {store_str}\n"
            f"Compliance: {checklist_status}\n\n"
            f"⚠️ Deploying to {store_str} carries compliance risk.\n"
            f"Store review policies are enforced by Apple/Google, "
            f"not by this pipeline.\n\n"
            f"✅ /deploy_confirm — proceed with deployment\n"
            f"❌ /deploy_cancel — return to S5 for modifications",
        )

        # Wait for operator response (1-hour unresponsive timeout
        # per DR Scenario #10)
        # ASSUMPTION: Telegram callback handler sets a flag in state
        # when operator responds.
        # Uses Postgres advisory lock (C6 pattern) for race protection.
        result = await _wait_for_deploy_decision(
            state, timeout_seconds=3600,  # 1 hour
        )
        if result == "timeout":
            # DR Scenario #10: Operator unresponsive >1 hour → auto-approve
            log.warning(
                f"[FIX-08] Operator unresponsive for 1 hour. "
                f"Auto-approving deploy."
            )
            await _log_deploy_consent(state, method="auto_timeout_1h")
            return True
        elif result == "confirm":
            await _log_deploy_consent(state, method="copilot_confirm")
            return True
        elif result == "cancel":
            return False

    else:
        # ── Autopilot: 15-minute auto-approve timer ──
        await notify_operator(
            state.operator_id, NotificationType.INFO,
            f"⏱️ Auto-deploying **{project_name}** in 15 minutes\n\n"
            f"Platform: {stack} → {store_str}\n"
            f"Tests: {passed}/{total} passed\n\n"
            f"❌ /deploy_cancel — stop deployment within 15 minutes",
        )

        result = await _wait_for_deploy_decision(
            state, timeout_seconds=900,  # 15 minutes
        )
        if result == "cancel":
            return False
        else:
            # Timeout = auto-approve (normal Autopilot behavior)
            await _log_deploy_consent(
                state, method="autopilot_auto_15m",
            )
            return True
```

#### §4.6.2 Deploy Decision Waiting (FIX-08)

```python
async def _wait_for_deploy_decision(
    state: PipelineState, timeout_seconds: int,
) -> str:
    """[FIX-08] Wait for operator deploy decision with race protection.
    Returns: "confirm", "cancel", or "timeout"
    Uses Postgres advisory lock (C6 pattern) for atomic decision recording.
    """
    # ASSUMPTION: Deploy decision is stored in Supabase deploy_decisions table
    # with project_id + advisory lock to prevent race conditions.
    lock_key = f"deploy_gate_{state.project_id}"

    async with postgres_advisory_lock(lock_key):
        deadline = asyncio.get_event_loop().time() + timeout_seconds
        while asyncio.get_event_loop().time() < deadline:
            # Check for operator response (polled from deploy_decisions table)
            decision = await check_deploy_decision(state.project_id)
            if decision:
                return decision  # "confirm" or "cancel"
            await asyncio.sleep(5)  # Poll every 5 seconds
        return "timeout"


async def _log_deploy_consent(state: PipelineState, method: str):
    """[FIX-08] Log DeploymentConsent event for audit trail."""
    consent_event = {
        "event_type": "DeploymentConsent",
        "operator_id": state.operator_id,
        "project_id": state.project_id,
        "timestamp": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        "method": method,
        "stack": (
            state.selected_stack.value if state.selected_stack else "unknown"
        ),
        "test_results": state.s5_output,
    }
    await audit_log(state.operator_id, "deployment_consent", consent_event)
    log.info(
        f"[FIX-08] DeploymentConsent: "
        f"project={state.project_id} method={method}"
    )
```

#### §4.6.3 Deploy Decision Telegram Commands (FIX-08)

```python
async def cmd_deploy_confirm(update: Update, context):
    """[FIX-08] Operator confirms deployment."""
    operator_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    state = await get_active_state(operator_id)
    if not state or state.current_stage != Stage.S5_TEST:
        await update.message.reply_text("No pending deploy confirmation.")
        return
    await record_deploy_decision(state.project_id, "confirm")
    await update.message.reply_text("✅ Deployment confirmed. Starting S6...")


async def cmd_deploy_cancel(update: Update, context):
    """[FIX-08] Operator cancels deployment."""
    operator_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    state = await get_active_state(operator_id)
    if not state:
        await update.message.reply_text("No pending deploy to cancel.")
        return
    await record_deploy_decision(state.project_id, "cancel")
    await update.message.reply_text(
        "❌ Deployment cancelled. Project returned to S5."
    )


async def cmd_deploy_confirm_all(update: Update, context):
    """[FIX-08] Confirm all pending deploys at once."""
    operator_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    pending = await get_pending_deploys(operator_id)
    if not pending:
        await update.message.reply_text("No pending deployments.")
        return
    for project_id in pending:
        await record_deploy_decision(project_id, "confirm")
    await update.message.reply_text(
        f"✅ {len(pending)} deployments confirmed:\n"
        + "\n".join(f"  • {pid}" for pid in pending)
    )
```

**FIX-08 Integration Note:** The `pre_deploy_gate()` is called by the LangGraph conditional router `route_after_test` (§2.7) when tests pass. If the gate returns False, the router sends the project back to S5. If True, it proceeds to S6. The gate does NOT modify `VALID_TRANSITIONS` — the S5→S6 edge still exists; the gate is enforcement logic within the transition, not a new stage.

---

### §4.7 S6 — DEPLOY

**Role:** Engineer (deploy scripts), Scout (deploy docs if needed). **Purpose:** Deploy built artifacts to hosting/app stores. **Cost Target:** <$0.30.

```python
@pipeline_node(Stage.S6_DEPLOY)
async def s6_deploy_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """
    S6: Deploy — push artifacts to hosting, app stores, or API endpoints.
    API-first approach (ADR-016): no portal UI login.
    On failure: App Store Airlock (binary upload to Telegram).
    """
    blueprint = Blueprint.model_validate(state.s2_output)
    artifacts = state.s4_output.get("artifacts", {})
    stack = blueprint.selected_stack
    exec_mgr = ExecutionModeManager(state)
    deploy_results = {}

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    # v5.4.1 Patch 1: Generate Platform Icons from Brand Assets
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    logo_assets = [
        a for a in state.brand_assets if a.get("asset_type") == "logo"
    ]
    if logo_assets:
        logo_url = logo_assets[0]["storage_url"]
        icon_results = await generate_platform_icons(
            logo_url, blueprint.target_platforms, state,
        )
        deploy_results["icons_generated"] = icon_results
    else:
        # No logo provided — use placeholder and flag for operator
        await notify_operator(
            state.operator_id, NotificationType.DECISION_NEEDED,
            "📱 No logo/icon found in brand_assets. "
            "Using placeholder icon. "
            "Upload a logo via Telegram to replace it.",
        )
        deploy_results["icons_generated"] = {"placeholder": True}

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    # Web Deployment (all stacks that produce web)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    if "web" in blueprint.target_platforms:
        web_cmd = (
            "npx firebase deploy --only hosting --non-interactive"
            if stack != TechStack.PYTHON_BACKEND
            else (
                f"gcloud run deploy "
                f"{blueprint.app_name.lower().replace(' ', '-')} "
                f"--source . --region me-central1 --allow-unauthenticated"
            )
        )
        web_result = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
            "name": "deploy_web",
            "type": "backend_deploy",
            "command": enforce_user_space(web_cmd),
            "timeout": 300,
        }, requires_macincloud=False)
        deploy_results["web"] = {
            "success": web_result.get("exit_code", 0) == 0,
            "url": _extract_deploy_url(web_result.get("stdout", "")),
        }

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    # Android Deployment (API-first)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    if "android" in blueprint.target_platforms and stack != TechStack.SWIFT:
        android_result = await _deploy_android(state, blueprint, exec_mgr)
        deploy_results["android"] = android_result

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    # iOS Deployment (API-first + Airlock fallback)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════
    if "ios" in blueprint.target_platforms and stack != TechStack.KOTLIN:
        ios_result = await _deploy_ios(state, blueprint, exec_mgr)
        deploy_results["ios"] = ios_result

    state.s6_output = {
        "deployments": deploy_results,
        "all_success": all(
            d.get("success") for d in deploy_results.values()
        ),
    }
    return state
```

#### §4.7.1 Android Deployment

```python
async def _deploy_android(state, blueprint, exec_mgr) -> dict:
    """Deploy Android via Google Play API (service account, no UI)."""
    # Step 1: Sign the APK/AAB
    sign_result = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
        "name": "sign_android",
        "type": "build",
        "command": enforce_user_space(
            "jarsigner -verbose -sigalg SHA256withRSA -digestalg SHA-256 "
            "-keystore release.keystore app-release-unsigned.apk alias_name"
        ),
    }, requires_macincloud=False)

    # Step 2: Upload via Google Play Developer API
    upload_result = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
        "name": "upload_play_store",
        "type": "backend_deploy",
        "command": enforce_user_space(
            "npx google-play-cli upload "
            "--package-name "
            + state.project_metadata.get("package_name", "")
            + " --track internal "  # Start with internal track
            "--aab app-release.aab"
        ),
    }, requires_macincloud=False)

    if upload_result.get("exit_code", 0) != 0:
        # Airlock: send binary to Telegram
        await send_telegram_message(
            state.operator_id,
            f"⚠️ Google Play API upload failed.\n"
            f"Sending you the .aab file — drag-and-drop to Play Console.\n"
            f"Error: {upload_result.get('stderr', '')[:300]}",
        )
        await send_telegram_file(state.operator_id, "app-release.aab")
        return {
            "success": True, "method": "airlock_telegram",
            "manual_upload": True,
        }
    return {"success": True, "method": "api", "track": "internal"}
```

#### §4.7.2 iOS Deployment

```python
async def _deploy_ios(state, blueprint, exec_mgr) -> dict:
    """Deploy iOS via Transporter CLI (no App Store Connect UI)."""
    # Step 1: Export IPA
    export_result = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
        "name": "export_ipa",
        "type": "ios_build",
        "command": enforce_user_space(
            "xcodebuild -exportArchive "
            "-archivePath build/App.xcarchive "
            "-exportOptionsPlist ExportOptions.plist "
            "-exportPath build/ipa"
        ),
    }, requires_macincloud=True)

    # Step 2: Upload via Transporter (Apple's CLI tool)
    upload_result = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
        "name": "upload_app_store",
        "type": "ios_build",
        "command": enforce_user_space(
            "xcrun altool --upload-app "
            "-f build/ipa/App.ipa "
            "-t ios "
            f"--apiKey {await get_secret('APPLE_API_KEY_ID')} "
            f"--apiIssuer {await get_secret('APPLE_API_ISSUER_ID')}"
        ),
    }, requires_macincloud=True)

    if upload_result.get("exit_code", 0) != 0:
        # Airlock: send IPA to Telegram
        await send_telegram_message(
            state.operator_id,
            f"⚠️ App Store Connect API upload failed.\n"
            f"Sending you the .ipa — upload via Transporter app.\n"
            f"Error: {upload_result.get('stderr', '')[:300]}",
        )
        await send_telegram_file(state.operator_id, "build/ipa/App.ipa")
        return {
            "success": True, "method": "airlock_telegram",
            "manual_upload": True,
        }
    return {"success": True, "method": "api", "status": "processing"}
```

#### §4.7.3 Platform Icon Generation (v5.4.1 Patch 1)

```python
async def generate_platform_icons(
    logo_url: str, platforms: list[str], state: PipelineState,
) -> dict:
    """
    Generate platform-required icon sets from the operator's logo.
    Uses Pillow (standard image processing), NOT AI generation.
    """
    from PIL import Image
    import io

    # Download source logo
    async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
        resp = await client.get(logo_url)
        source = Image.open(io.BytesIO(resp.content)).convert("RGBA")

    results = {}

    if "ios" in platforms:
        # iOS requires 1024x1024 App Store icon + standard sizes
        ios_sizes = [
            1024, 180, 167, 152, 120, 87, 80, 76, 60, 58, 40, 29, 20,
        ]
        for size in ios_sizes:
            resized = source.resize((size, size), Image.LANCZOS)
            buf = io.BytesIO()
            resized.save(buf, format="PNG")
            await github_commit_binary(
                repo=f"factory/{state.project_id}",
                path=(
                    f"ios/Assets.xcassets/AppIcon.appiconset/"
                    f"icon_{size}x{size}.png"
                ),
                content=buf.getvalue(),
                message=f"Add iOS icon {size}x{size}",
            )
        results["ios"] = {
            "sizes": len(ios_sizes), "source": "brand_assets",
        }

    if "android" in platforms:
        # Android adaptive icon foreground
        for density, size in [
            ("mdpi", 48), ("hdpi", 72), ("xhdpi", 96),
            ("xxhdpi", 144), ("xxxhdpi", 192),
        ]:
            resized = source.resize((size, size), Image.LANCZOS)
            buf = io.BytesIO()
            resized.save(buf, format="PNG")
            await github_commit_binary(
                repo=f"factory/{state.project_id}",
                path=(
                    f"android/app/src/main/res/"
                    f"mipmap-{density}/ic_launcher.png"
                ),
                content=buf.getvalue(),
                message=f"Add Android icon {density}",
            )
        results["android"] = {
            "densities": 5, "source": "brand_assets",
        }

    return results
```

#### §4.7.4 iOS App Store Submission Protocol (FIX-21)

Defines the precise 5-step sequence for submitting iOS builds via MacinCloud. Each step has explicit retry logic with exponential backoff. This replaces the implicit "upload to TestFlight" in the deploy step.

```python
IOS_SUBMISSION_STEPS = {
    "version": "5.6",
    "steps": [
        {
            "step": 1,
            "name": "archive",
            "command": (
                "xcodebuild archive -workspace App.xcworkspace "
                "-scheme App -archivePath build/App.xcarchive"
            ),
            "timeout_seconds": 600,
            "retry": {"max_attempts": 2, "backoff_base": 30},
            "failure_action": "halt_and_notify",
        },
        {
            "step": 2,
            "name": "export",
            "command": (
                "xcodebuild -exportArchive "
                "-archivePath build/App.xcarchive "
                "-exportOptionsPlist ExportOptions.plist "
                "-exportPath build/export"
            ),
            "timeout_seconds": 300,
            "retry": {"max_attempts": 2, "backoff_base": 30},
            "failure_action": "halt_and_notify",
        },
        {
            "step": 3,
            "name": "validate",
            "command": (
                "xcrun altool --validate-app "
                "-f build/export/App.ipa -t ios "
                "--apiKey $APP_STORE_API_KEY "
                "--apiIssuer $APP_STORE_ISSUER_ID"
            ),
            "timeout_seconds": 120,
            "retry": {"max_attempts": 3, "backoff_base": 60},
            # Validation errors need human review
            "failure_action": "halt_and_notify",
        },
        {
            "step": 4,
            "name": "upload",
            "command": (
                "xcrun altool --upload-app "
                "-f build/export/App.ipa -t ios "
                "--apiKey $APP_STORE_API_KEY "
                "--apiIssuer $APP_STORE_ISSUER_ID"
            ),
            "timeout_seconds": 900,  # Large uploads can be slow
            "retry": {"max_attempts": 3, "backoff_base": 120},
            "failure_action": "halt_and_notify",
        },
        {
            "step": 5,
            "name": "poll_processing",
            "command": (
                "xcrun altool --notarization-info $REQUEST_UUID "
                "--apiKey $APP_STORE_API_KEY "
                "--apiIssuer $APP_STORE_ISSUER_ID"
            ),
            "timeout_seconds": 3600,  # Processing can take up to 1 hour
            "poll_interval_seconds": 60,
            # Linear polling, not exponential
            "retry": {"max_attempts": 60, "backoff_base": 0},
            # Processing delays are common, don't halt
            "failure_action": "notify_operator_continue",
        },
    ],
    "env_vars_required": ["APP_STORE_API_KEY", "APP_STORE_ISSUER_ID"],
    "prerequisite": "MacinCloud session active (§7.2.2)",
    "fallback": "Airlock binary delivery via Telegram (§7.6)",
}
```
