### §4.8 S7 — VERIFY

**Role:** Quick Fix (lightweight checks), Scout (guidelines check). **Purpose:** Verify deployed app is reachable, functional, and compliant. **Cost Target:** <$0.20.

```python
@pipeline_node(Stage.S7_VERIFY)
async def s7_verify_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """
    S7: Verify — smoke tests on deployed app.
    1. Web: HTTP health check
    2. Mobile: App Store processing status
    3. Legal: Final compliance verification
    """
    deployments = state.s6_output.get("deployments", {})
    checks = []

    # ── Web verification ──
    if "web" in deployments:
        web = deployments["web"]
        if web.get("url"):
            # HTTP health check
            health = await call_ai(
                role=AIRole.QUICK_FIX,
                prompt=(
                    f"Generate a curl command to health-check this URL: "
                    f"{web['url']}\nReturn ONLY the curl command."
                ),
                state=state, action="general",
            )
            exec_mgr = ExecutionModeManager(state)
            result = await exec_mgr.execute_task({
                "name": "web_health_check",
                "type": "backend_deploy",
                "command": enforce_user_space(health.strip()),
                "timeout": 30,
            }, requires_macincloud=False)
            checks.append({
                "type": "web_health",
                "passed": result.get("exit_code", 1) == 0,
                "url": web["url"],
            })

    # ── Mobile verification ──
    for platform in ("android", "ios"):
        if platform in deployments:
            deploy = deployments[platform]
            if deploy.get("method") == "api":
                checks.append({
                    "type": f"{platform}_upload",
                    "passed": True,
                    "status": deploy.get("status", "submitted"),
                })
            elif deploy.get("method") == "airlock_telegram":
                checks.append({
                    "type": f"{platform}_airlock",
                    "passed": True,
                    "note": "Binary sent to operator for manual upload",
                })

    # ── App Store guidelines check (Scout) ──
    can_research = await check_circuit_breaker(state, 0.02)
    if can_research:
        guidelines = await call_ai(
            role=AIRole.SCOUT,
            prompt=(
                f"Does this app description violate Apple App Store "
                f"or Google Play guidelines?\n"
                f"App: {state.s0_output.get('app_description', '')}\n"
                f"Category: {state.s0_output.get('app_category', '')}\n"
                f"Has payments: {state.s0_output.get('has_payments', False)}\n"
                f"Return: pass/fail with specific guideline references."
            ),
            state=state, action="general",
        )
        checks.append({
            "type": "store_guidelines",
            "passed": "pass" in guidelines.lower()[:100],
            "details": guidelines[:500],
        })

    all_passed = all(c["passed"] for c in checks)
    state.s7_output = {
        "passed": all_passed,
        "checks": checks,
    }
    return state
```

---

### §4.9 S8 — HANDOFF

**Roles:** Quick Fix (summary), Strategist (final legal sign-off), Engineer (DocuGen + Handoff Intelligence Pack [FIX-27]). **Purpose:** Generate legal docs, compile handoff package, generate operator documentation, deliver to operator. **Cost Target:** <$0.50 base + ~$0.30–$0.50 for handoff docs (4 Engineer calls); ~$0.50–$0.80 for multi-stack programs (7 Engineer calls).

#### Handoff Intelligence Pack [FIX-27]

S8 generates a tailored documentation package for the zero-IT operator. Every document uses **real values** from the actual project state — real endpoint URLs, real environment variable names, real file paths, real service names — not generic templates. All commands are copy-pasteable.

**Per-project documents (always generated — 4 docs):**

| Document | File | Purpose |
|----------|------|---------|
| Quick Start Guide | `docs/QUICK_START.md` | How to run, test, and update the app after handoff |
| Emergency Runbook | `docs/EMERGENCY_RUNBOOK.md` | "If you see X, do Y" — 8–12 most likely failure scenarios |
| Service Map | `docs/SERVICE_MAP.md` | Every external dependency, credentials, rotation instructions |
| Update Guide | `docs/UPDATE_GUIDE.md` | How to make common changes without understanding the codebase |

**Per-program documents (multi-stack only, when all siblings complete S8 — 3 docs):**

| Document | File | Purpose |
|----------|------|---------|
| Integration Test Checklist | `docs/INTEGRATION_TEST_CHECKLIST.md` | Copy-pasteable curl commands to verify cross-service communication |
| Architecture Overview | `docs/ARCHITECTURE_OVERVIEW.md` | ASCII diagram showing how sub-projects connect |
| Cross-Service Troubleshooting | `docs/CROSS_SERVICE_TROUBLESHOOTING.md` | Step-by-step diagnosis for cross-service failures |

All documents are stored in GitHub `/docs/`, persisted as `HandoffDoc` nodes in Mother Memory (Janitor-exempt, permanent), and delivered via Telegram.

```python
async def generate_handoff_intelligence_pack(
    state: PipelineState,
    blueprint: Blueprint,
) -> dict:
    """
    Generate the Operator Handoff Intelligence Pack.  [FIX-27]

    Returns dict of {filename: content} for all generated documents.
    Called from s8_handoff_node() after summary compilation.

    For multi-stack programs (program_id is not None):
    - Always generates per-project docs (4 docs)
    - Generates per-program docs (3 docs) ONLY when all siblings
      in the program_id group have reached S8
    """
    docs = {}

    # ── Gather project context for the Engineer ──
    deployments = state.s6_output.get("deployments", {})
    services = state.s2_output.get("services", {})
    env_vars = state.s3_output.get("env_vars", {})
    api_endpoints = state.s3_output.get("api_endpoints", [])
    stack = blueprint.selected_stack.value
    app_name = blueprint.app_name
    app_category = blueprint.app_category
    platforms = blueprint.target_platforms

    project_context = (
        f"App: {app_name}\n"
        f"Category: {app_category}\n"
        f"Stack: {stack}\n"
        f"Platforms: {', '.join(platforms)}\n"
        f"Deployments: {json.dumps(deployments, indent=2)}\n"
        f"Services: {json.dumps(services, indent=2)}\n"
        f"Environment Variables: {json.dumps(env_vars, indent=2)}\n"
        f"API Endpoints: {json.dumps(api_endpoints, indent=2)}\n"
        f"War Room History: {len(state.war_room_history)} activations\n"
    )

    # ── Per-Project Documents (always generated) ──

    # 3.1 Quick Start Guide
    docs["QUICK_START.md"] = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
        prompt=(
            f"Generate a Quick Start Guide for a zero-IT operator.\n\n"
            f"PROJECT CONTEXT:\n{project_context}\n\n"
            f"REQUIREMENTS:\n"
            f"- Plain language, no jargon\n"
            f"- Every command must be copy-pasteable with REAL values "
            f"(not placeholders)\n"
            f"- Numbered steps, each with: what you're doing, the exact "
            f"command/URL, what success looks like, what to do if it fails\n"
            f"- Cover: accessing the app, verifying it runs, restarting, "
            f"checking logs, updating simple content, requesting a rebuild\n"
            f"- Format as Markdown\n"
        ),
        state=state, action="general",
    )

    # 3.2 Emergency Runbook
    docs["EMERGENCY_RUNBOOK.md"] = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
        prompt=(
            f"Generate an Emergency Runbook for a zero-IT operator.\n\n"
            f"PROJECT CONTEXT:\n{project_context}\n\n"
            f"REQUIREMENTS:\n"
            f"- Cover the 8-12 most likely failure scenarios for this "
            f"specific stack ({stack}) and services\n"
            f"- Each scenario: symptom (plain English), cause (one "
            f"sentence), fix (exact copy-pasteable steps), escalation\n"
            f"- Include: app unreachable, API errors, auth failures, "
            f"third-party SDK issues, cost alerts\n"
            f"- If SAMA-regulated payments: include payment gateway "
            f"failures, webhook issues, refund procedures\n"
            f"- Format as Markdown with clear section headers\n"
        ),
        state=state, action="general",
    )

    # 3.3 Service Map
    docs["SERVICE_MAP.md"] = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
        prompt=(
            f"Generate a Service Map for a zero-IT operator.\n\n"
            f"PROJECT CONTEXT:\n{project_context}\n\n"
            f"REQUIREMENTS:\n"
            f"- List EVERY external service this app uses\n"
            f"- For each: dashboard URL, API URL, where credentials "
            f"are stored, how to rotate them, monthly cost estimate\n"
            f"- Use ASCII box diagrams for visual clarity\n"
            f"- Include: hosting, database, auth, storage, payments, "
            f"push notifications, analytics, AI APIs, domain, CDN, "
            f"email — but ONLY the ones this project actually uses\n"
            f"- Format as Markdown\n"
        ),
        state=state, action="general",
    )

    # 3.4 Update Guide
    docs["UPDATE_GUIDE.md"] = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
        prompt=(
            f"Generate an Update Guide for a zero-IT operator.\n\n"
            f"PROJECT CONTEXT:\n{project_context}\n\n"
            f"REQUIREMENTS:\n"
            f"- Table of common changes: what, difficulty (Easy/Medium/"
            f"Hard), method\n"
            f"- Easy changes: step-by-step with exact file paths, "
            f"database tables, config locations\n"
            f"- Medium changes: step-by-step with rebuild instructions\n"
            f"- Hard changes: explain that pipeline rebuild is needed "
            f"and how to request one\n"
            f"- Tailored to {app_category} — use relevant examples "
            f"(e.g., 'add menu item' for restaurant, 'add listing' "
            f"for marketplace)\n"
            f"- Format as Markdown\n"
        ),
        state=state, action="general",
    )

    # ── Per-Program Documents (multi-stack only) ──
    if state.program_id:
        # Check if all siblings have completed S8
        sibling_status = await neo4j_run("""
            MATCH (p:Project {program_id: $pgid})
            RETURN p.id AS id,
                   p.completed AS completed,
                   p.handoff_docs_stored AS docs_stored
        """, {"pgid": state.program_id})

        all_siblings_complete = all(
            row["completed"] for row in sibling_status
        )

        if all_siblings_complete:
            # Gather cross-project API contracts from Mother Memory
            contracts = await neo4j_run("""
                MATCH (p:Project {program_id: $pgid})
                      -[:HAS_API_CONTRACT]->(c:APIContract)
                RETURN p.id AS project_id,
                       p.stack AS stack,
                       c.endpoints AS endpoints,
                       c.base_url AS base_url,
                       c.auth_method AS auth_method
                ORDER BY p.id
            """, {"pgid": state.program_id})

            # Gather sibling deployment info from Mother Memory
            sibling_deployments = await neo4j_run("""
                MATCH (p:Project {program_id: $pgid})
                OPTIONAL MATCH (p)-[:HAS_HANDOFF_DOC
                    {doc_type: 'service_map'}]->(d:HandoffDoc)
                RETURN p.id AS project_id,
                       p.stack AS stack,
                       p.app_name AS app_name,
                       d.content AS service_map
                ORDER BY p.id
            """, {"pgid": state.program_id})

            program_context = (
                f"Program: {state.program_id}\n"
                f"Sub-projects:\n"
                f"{json.dumps([dict(r) for r in sibling_deployments], indent=2)}\n"
                f"API Contracts:\n"
                f"{json.dumps([dict(r) for r in contracts], indent=2)}\n"
            )

            # 4.1 Integration Test Checklist
            docs["INTEGRATION_TEST_CHECKLIST.md"] = await call_ai(
                role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
                prompt=(
                    f"Generate an Integration Test Checklist for a zero-IT "
                    f"operator to verify all sub-projects can communicate.\n\n"
                    f"PROGRAM CONTEXT:\n{program_context}\n\n"
                    f"REQUIREMENTS:\n"
                    f"- Every test is a copy-pasteable curl command with "
                    f"REAL URLs and expected response\n"
                    f"- Tests cover: authentication flow, data fetch, "
                    f"data write, every shared endpoint\n"
                    f"- Each test: what you're verifying, exact curl "
                    f"command, expected response, what to do if it fails "
                    f"(reference EMERGENCY_RUNBOOK.md section)\n"
                    f"- Header: estimated time to run all tests\n"
                    f"- Format as Markdown with numbered tests\n"
                ),
                state=state, action="general",
            )

            # 4.2 System Architecture Overview
            docs["ARCHITECTURE_OVERVIEW.md"] = await call_ai(
                role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
                prompt=(
                    f"Generate a System Architecture Overview for a zero-IT "
                    f"operator showing how all sub-projects connect.\n\n"
                    f"PROGRAM CONTEXT:\n{program_context}\n\n"
                    f"REQUIREMENTS:\n"
                    f"- ASCII diagram showing all sub-projects, databases, "
                    f"external services, and how they connect\n"
                    f"- List shared API contract: base URL, auth method, "
                    f"key endpoints\n"
                    f"- Link to each sub-project's GitHub repo\n"
                    f"- One page maximum\n"
                    f"- Format as Markdown\n"
                ),
                state=state, action="general",
            )

            # 4.3 Cross-Service Troubleshooting Guide
            docs["CROSS_SERVICE_TROUBLESHOOTING.md"] = await call_ai(
                role=AIRole.ENGINEER,
                prompt=(
                    f"Generate a Cross-Service Troubleshooting Guide for a "
                    f"zero-IT operator.\n\n"
                    f"PROGRAM CONTEXT:\n{program_context}\n\n"
                    f"REQUIREMENTS:\n"
                    f"- Cover the 5-8 most likely cross-service failures\n"
                    f"- Each problem: numbered diagnostic steps, each step "
                    f"has exact command/URL, expected result, fix if wrong\n"
                    f"- Start with most common: 'frontend can't reach "
                    f"backend', 'backend can't reach database'\n"
                    f"- Reference EMERGENCY_RUNBOOK.md for single-service "
                    f"issues\n"
                    f"- Format as Markdown\n"
                ),
                state=state, action="general",
            )
        else:
            # This project finished before siblings — store data,
            # defer program-level docs to the last sibling's S8 run
            docs["_PROGRAM_DOCS_DEFERRED"] = (
                f"Program docs deferred: not all siblings in "
                f"program_id={state.program_id} have completed S8. "
                f"Program-level docs will be generated when the last "
                f"sibling project completes."
            )

    return docs
```

```python
@pipeline_node(Stage.S8_HANDOFF)
async def s8_handoff_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """
    S8: Handoff — generate legal docs, compile summary,
    generate handoff intelligence pack, deliver everything.
    Final stage. Terminal → COMPLETED.
    """
    blueprint = Blueprint.model_validate(state.s2_output)

    # ── Step 1: Generate legal documents (DocuGen) ──
    legal_docs = await generate_legal_documents(state, blueprint)

    # ── Step 2: Compile project summary ──
    summary = await call_ai(
        role=AIRole.QUICK_FIX,
        prompt=(
            f"Compile a project handoff summary.\n\n"
            f"App: {blueprint.app_name}\n"
            f"Stack: {blueprint.selected_stack.value}\n"
            f"Platforms: {blueprint.target_platforms}\n"
            f"Deployments: "
            f"{json.dumps(state.s6_output.get('deployments', {}))}\n"
            f"Legal docs generated: {list(legal_docs.keys())}\n"
            f"Total AI cost: ${state.total_cost_usd:.2f}\n"
            f"War Room activations: {len(state.war_room_history)}\n"
            f"Snapshot ID: {state.snapshot_id}\n\n"
            f"Return a concise Markdown summary for the operator."
        ),
        state=state, action="general",
    )

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    # ── Step 2.5: Generate Handoff Intelligence Pack [FIX-27] ──
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    handoff_docs = await generate_handoff_intelligence_pack(
        state, blueprint,
    )

    # ── Step 3: Store in GitHub ──
    repo = f"factory/{state.project_id}"
    # Legal docs
    for doc_name, doc_content in legal_docs.items():
        await github_commit_file(
            repo=repo,
            path=f"legal/{doc_name}.md",
            content=doc_content,
            message=f"Add {doc_name} legal document",
        )
    # Handoff summary
    await github_commit_file(
        repo=repo, path="HANDOFF.md",
        content=summary, message="Add handoff summary",
    )
    # ═══ [FIX-27] Handoff Intelligence Pack docs ═══
    for doc_name, doc_content in handoff_docs.items():
        if doc_name.startswith("_"):
            continue  # Skip meta-entries
        await github_commit_file(
            repo=repo,
            path=f"docs/{doc_name}",
            content=doc_content,
            message=f"Add handoff doc: {doc_name}",
        )

    # ── Step 4: Store patterns in Mother Memory ──
    await store_project_patterns(
        project_id=state.project_id,
        stack=blueprint.selected_stack,
        screens=blueprint.screens,
        success=True,
        war_room_count=len(state.war_room_history),
    )
    # ═══ [FIX-27] Persist handoff docs in Mother Memory ═══
    await store_handoff_docs_in_memory(
        project_id=state.project_id,
        program_id=state.program_id,
        stack=blueprint.selected_stack.value,
        app_category=blueprint.app_category,
        docs=handoff_docs,
    )

    # ── Step 5: Deliver via Telegram ──
    deployments = state.s6_output.get("deployments", {})
    delivery_message = (
        f"🎉 **{blueprint.app_name}** is ready!\n\n"
        f"📱 Stack: {blueprint.selected_stack.value}\n"
        f"🌍 Platforms: {', '.join(blueprint.target_platforms)}\n\n"
    )
    # Add deployment URLs
    for platform, info in deployments.items():
        if info.get("url"):
            delivery_message += f"🔗 {platform}: {info['url']}\n"
        elif info.get("method") == "airlock_telegram":
            delivery_message += (
                f"📦 {platform}: Binary sent above (manual upload)\n"
            )
        else:
            delivery_message += f"✓ {platform}: Submitted for review\n"

    delivery_message += (
        f"\n📋 Legal docs: {', '.join(legal_docs.keys())}\n"
        f"💰 Total AI cost: ${state.total_cost_usd:.2f} "
        f"({state.total_cost_usd * 3.75:.2f} SAR)\n"
        f"⏪ Time-travel restore: "
        f"`/restore State_#{state.snapshot_id}`\n"
        f"📂 GitHub: {repo}\n"
    )
    # ═══ [FIX-27] Add handoff docs to delivery message ═══
    handoff_doc_names = [
        n for n in handoff_docs.keys() if not n.startswith("_")
    ]
    delivery_message += (
        f"📖 Operator docs: {', '.join(handoff_doc_names)}\n"
        f"   → All docs in GitHub: {repo}/docs/\n"
    )
    await send_telegram_message(state.operator_id, delivery_message)

    # Send legal doc files
    for doc_name, doc_content in legal_docs.items():
        await send_telegram_document(
            state.operator_id,
            content=doc_content,
            filename=f"{doc_name}.md",
        )
    # ═══ [FIX-27] Send handoff docs via Telegram ═══
    for doc_name, doc_content in handoff_docs.items():
        if doc_name.startswith("_"):
            continue
        await send_telegram_document(
            state.operator_id,
            content=doc_content,
            filename=doc_name,
        )

    state.s8_output = {
        "delivered": True,
        "summary": summary,
        "legal_docs": list(legal_docs.keys()),
        "handoff_docs": handoff_doc_names,  # [FIX-27]
        "total_cost_usd": state.total_cost_usd,
        "snapshot_id": state.snapshot_id,
    }
    return state
```

---

### §4.10 HALT Handler

```python
async def halt_handler_node(state: PipelineState) -> PipelineState:
    """Handle pipeline halt — notify operator with diagnosis."""
    reason = state.legal_halt_reason or "Unknown (check errors)"
    errors = state.errors[-5:] if state.errors else []
    war_room = (
        state.war_room_history[-3:] if state.war_room_history else []
    )

    message = (
        f"🛑 Pipeline halted at {state.current_stage.value}\n\n"
        f"Reason: {reason}\n\n"
    )

    if errors:
        message += "Recent errors:\n"
        for e in errors:
            message += (
                f"  • {e.get('type', 'unknown')}: "
                f"{e.get('error', '')[:200]}\n"
            )

    if war_room:
        message += (
            f"\nWar Room history: {len(state.war_room_history)} activations\n"
        )
        last = war_room[-1]
        message += (
            f"  Last: L{last.get('level', '?')} — "
            f"{'Resolved' if last.get('resolved') else 'FAILED'}\n"
        )

    message += (
        f"\n💰 Cost so far: ${state.total_cost_usd:.2f}\n"
        f"⏪ Restore: `/restore State_#{state.snapshot_id}`\n"
        f"▶️ Resume: `/continue`\n"
        f"❌ Cancel: `/cancel`"
    )
    await send_telegram_message(state.operator_id, message)
    return state
```

---

### §4.11 Stage Summary Table

| Stage | Primary Role | Scout | Strategist | Engineer | Quick Fix | Copilot Decision |
|-------|-------------|-------|-----------|----------|-----------|-----------------|
| S0 | Quick Fix | Market scan | — | — | Extract reqs | Confirm scope |
| S1 | Strategist | Regulation research | Classify + decide | — | — | Handle blocks |
| S2 | Strategist | Trends + framework | Stack + arch + design | Mocks (HTML) | — | Stack + design |
| S3 | Engineer | — | — | Generate all code | Validate syntax | — |
| S4 | Engineer | — | — | Build scripts | GUI supervision | Exec mode |
| S5 | Engineer | — | — | Gen tests + analyze | Analyze results | Handle failures |
| S6 | Engineer | Deploy docs | — | Deploy scripts | — | — |
| S7 | Quick Fix | Guidelines check | — | — | Health checks | — |
| S8 | Engineer | — | Legal sign-off | DocuGen render | Summary | — |

**Cost per project (AI only):** ~$8.35 across all stages. **Fixed infra per project:** ~$42.50. **Total per project:** ~$58.51 (219.41 SAR).

**Pipeline flow:**

```
S0 Intake → S1 Legal+Preflight → S2 Blueprint+ComplianceArtifacts
→ S3 CodeGen+AssetIngest → S4 Build → S5 Test → [Deploy Gate]
→ S6 Deploy+IconGen → S7 Verify → S8 Handoff → COMPLETED
```

**Terminal states:** COMPLETED (success) | HALTED (failure/manual intervention).

**Continuous Legal Thread** does not appear as a stage transition — it runs as a parallel coroutine alongside each stage (see §2.7.3). It can inject a HALT at any point S1→S8.

---

*End of Part 8 — covers S4 through S8 plus HALT Handler and Stage Summary. PART 4 (Pipeline Stages) is now complete. Reply "Cont" for Part 9 (PART 5: Control & Interface — Telegram Bot, Variable Autonomy, Operator Commands).*

### §5.1 Telegram Bot Architecture

#### §5.1.1 Bot Registration & Webhook

```python
from telegram import (
    Update, Bot, InlineKeyboardButton, InlineKeyboardMarkup,
)
from telegram.ext import (
    Application, CommandHandler, MessageHandler,
    CallbackQueryHandler,
)
import asyncio

TELEGRAM_CONFIG = {
    "bot_token": "from GCP Secret Manager",
    "webhook_url": "https://factory-bot-XXXX.run.app/webhook",
    "allowed_operators": [],  # From Supabase operator_whitelist
    "max_message_length": 4096,
    "photo_max_size_mb": 10,
    "document_max_size_mb": 50,
}


async def setup_bot() -> Application:
    app = (
        Application.builder()
        .token(await get_secret("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN"))
        .build()
    )

    # ── Project lifecycle ──
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("start", cmd_start))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("new", cmd_new_project))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("status", cmd_status))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("cost", cmd_cost))

    # ── Execution control ──
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("mode", cmd_mode))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("autonomy", cmd_autonomy))

    # ── Time travel ──
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("restore", cmd_restore))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("snapshots", cmd_snapshots))

    # ── Pipeline flow ──
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("continue", cmd_continue))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("cancel", cmd_cancel))

    # ── Diagnostics ──
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("warroom", cmd_warroom))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("legal", cmd_legal))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("help", cmd_help))

    # ── Inline + free-text ──
    app.add_handler(CallbackQueryHandler(handle_callback))
    app.add_handler(MessageHandler(
        filters.TEXT | filters.PHOTO
        | filters.Document.ALL | filters.VOICE,
        handle_message,
    ))

    return app
```

#### §5.1.2 Operator Authentication

```python
async def authenticate_operator(update: Update) -> bool:
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    result = (
        await supabase_client.table("operator_whitelist")
        .select("*").eq("telegram_id", user_id).execute()
    )
    if not result.data:
        await update.message.reply_text(
            "🚫 Unauthorized. Contact admin for access."
        )
        return False
    return True


def require_auth(fn):
    @wraps(fn)
    async def wrapper(update: Update, context):
        if not await authenticate_operator(update):
            return
        return await fn(update, context)
    return wrapper
```

#### `/new` — Start Project

```python
@require_auth
async def cmd_new_project(update: Update, context):
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    active = await get_active_project(user_id)

    if active:
        keyboard = InlineKeyboardMarkup([
            [InlineKeyboardButton(
                "Continue existing",
                callback_data="project_continue",
            )],
            [InlineKeyboardButton(
                "Archive & start new",
                callback_data="project_archive_new",
            )],
        ])
        await update.message.reply_text(
            f"📋 Active project: {active['project_id']} "
            f"at {active['current_stage']}\n"
            f"What would you like to do?",
            reply_markup=keyboard,
        )
        return

    description = " ".join(context.args) if context.args else None
    if description:
        await _start_project(update, user_id, description)
    else:
        await set_operator_state(user_id, "awaiting_project_description")
        await update.message.reply_text(
            "📝 Describe your app idea.\n"
            "Send text, screenshots, voice, or documents."
        )


async def _start_project(update, user_id, description, attachments=None):
    import uuid
    project_id = f"proj_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"
    prefs = await get_operator_preferences(user_id)

    state = PipelineState(
        project_id=project_id,
        operator_id=user_id,
        autonomy_mode=AutonomyMode(
            prefs.get("autonomy_mode", "autopilot")
        ),
        execution_mode=ExecutionMode(
            prefs.get("execution_mode", "cloud")
        ),
        project_metadata={
            "raw_input": description,
            "attachments": attachments or [],
        },
    )

    mode_emoji = {"cloud": "☁️", "local": "💻", "hybrid": "🔀"}
    auto_emoji = {"autopilot": "🤖", "copilot": "👨‍✈️"}

    await update.message.reply_text(
        f"🚀 Project {project_id} started!\n"
        f"Mode: {mode_emoji[state.execution_mode.value]} "
        f"{state.execution_mode.value}\n"
        f"Autonomy: {auto_emoji[state.autonomy_mode.value]} "
        f"{state.autonomy_mode.value}\n"
        f"Processing..."
    )

    graph = build_pipeline_graph()
    asyncio.create_task(run_pipeline(graph, state))
```

#### `/status` — Progress

```python
@require_auth
async def cmd_status(update: Update, context):
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    active = await get_active_project(user_id)
    if not active:
        await update.message.reply_text(
            "No active project. /new to start."
        )
        return

    state = PipelineState.model_validate(active["state_json"])
    stages = ["S0", "S1", "S2", "S3", "S4", "S5", "S6", "S7", "S8"]
    current_idx = next(
        (i for i, s in enumerate(stages)
         if s in state.current_stage.value), 0,
    )

    progress = ""
    for i in range(len(stages)):
        if i < current_idx:
            progress += "✅"
        elif i == current_idx:
            progress += (
                "🔴" if state.current_stage == Stage.HALTED else "🔵"
            )
        else:
            progress += "⚪"

    elapsed = (
        datetime.now(timezone.utc)
        - datetime.fromisoformat(state.created_at)
    )
    msg = (
        f"📊 {state.project_id}\n"
        f"{progress}\n"
        f"Stage: {state.current_stage.value}\n"
        f"Stack: {state.selected_stack.value "
        f"if state.selected_stack else 'Pending'}\n"
        f"Mode: {state.execution_mode.value} | "
        f"{state.autonomy_mode.value}\n"
        f"Elapsed: {elapsed.seconds // 60}m "
        f"{elapsed.seconds % 60}s\n"
        f"Cost: ${state.total_cost_usd:.2f} "
        f"({state.total_cost_usd * 3.75:.2f} SAR)\n"
        f"Snapshot: #{state.snapshot_id or 0}\n"
    )

    if state.war_room_active:
        msg += "\n🔴 WAR ROOM ACTIVE"
    if state.legal_halt:
        msg += (
            f"\n⚖️ LEGAL HALT: {state.legal_halt_reason[:80]}"
        )
    if state.circuit_breaker_triggered:
        msg += "\n💰 CIRCUIT BREAKER"

    await update.message.reply_text(msg)
```

#### `/cost` — Budget Breakdown

```python
@require_auth
async def cmd_cost(update: Update, context):
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    active = await get_active_project(user_id)

    if not active:
        monthly = await get_monthly_cost_summary(user_id)
        await update.message.reply_text(
            f"💰 Monthly ({monthly['month']}):\n"
            f"Projects: {monthly['project_count']}\n"
            f"AI: ${monthly['ai_total']:.2f} | "
            f"Infra: ${monthly['infra_fixed']:.2f}\n"
            f"Total: ${monthly['total']:.2f} "
            f"({monthly['total'] * 3.75:.2f} SAR)\n"
            f"Budget: $800 (3,000 SAR) | "
            f"Remaining: ${800 - monthly['total']:.2f}"
        )
        return

    state = PipelineState.model_validate(active["state_json"])
    msg = f"💰 {state.project_id}\n\n"
    for phase, cost in sorted(state.phase_costs.items()):
        if not phase.startswith("strategist_"):
            bar = (
                "█" * min(10, int(cost / 0.20))
                + "░" * max(0, 10 - int(cost / 0.20))
            )
            msg += f"  {phase}: ${cost:.3f} [{bar}] $2.00\n"

    msg += (
        f"\nTotal: ${state.total_cost_usd:.2f} "
        f"({state.total_cost_usd * 3.75:.2f} SAR)"
    )
    if state.war_room_history:
        msg += (
            f"\nWar Room: {len(state.war_room_history)} activations"
        )
    await update.message.reply_text(msg)
```

#### `/mode` — Execution Mode Toggle

```python
@require_auth
async def cmd_mode(update: Update, context):
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    active = await get_active_project(user_id)
    if not active:
        await update.message.reply_text("No active project.")
        return

    state = PipelineState.model_validate(active["state_json"])

    if (
        context.args
        and context.args[0].lower() in ("cloud", "local", "hybrid")
    ):
        target = context.args[0].lower()
        if target in ("local", "hybrid") and not state.local_heartbeat_alive:
            await update.message.reply_text(
                f"⚠️ Local machine not detected.\n\n"
                f"Setup:\n"
                f"1. pip install fastapi uvicorn --user\n"
                f"2. Save factory_agent.py\n"
                f"3. cloudflared tunnel run factory-agent\n"
                f"4. uvicorn factory_agent:app --port 8765"
            )
            return
        state.execution_mode = ExecutionMode(target)
        await update_project_state(state)
        emoji = {
            "cloud": "☁️", "local": "💻", "hybrid": "🔀",
        }
        await update.message.reply_text(
            f"{emoji[target]} Switched to {target.upper()}."
        )
        return

    keyboard = InlineKeyboardMarkup([
        [InlineKeyboardButton(
            f"{'✅ ' if state.execution_mode == ExecutionMode.CLOUD "
            f"else ''}Cloud",
            callback_data="mode_cloud",
        )],
        [InlineKeyboardButton(
            f"{'✅ ' if state.execution_mode == ExecutionMode.LOCAL "
            f"else ''}Local ($0)",
            callback_data="mode_local",
        )],
        [InlineKeyboardButton(
            f"{'✅ ' if state.execution_mode == ExecutionMode.HYBRID "
            f"else ''}Hybrid",
            callback_data="mode_hybrid",
        )],
    ])
    await update.message.reply_text(
        f"Current: {state.execution_mode.value}",
        reply_markup=keyboard,
    )
```

#### `/autonomy` — Toggle Autopilot/Copilot

```python
@require_auth
async def cmd_autonomy(update: Update, context):
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    active = await get_active_project(user_id)

    if not active:
        # Set default preference
        prefs = await get_operator_preferences(user_id)
        current = prefs.get("autonomy_mode", "autopilot")
        new = "copilot" if current == "autopilot" else "autopilot"
        await set_operator_preference(user_id, "autonomy_mode", new)
        emoji = "👨‍✈️" if new == "copilot" else "🤖"
        await update.message.reply_text(
            f"{emoji} Default set to {new.upper()}."
        )
        return

    state = PipelineState.model_validate(active["state_json"])
    new = (
        AutonomyMode.COPILOT
        if state.autonomy_mode == AutonomyMode.AUTOPILOT
        else AutonomyMode.AUTOPILOT
    )
    state.autonomy_mode = new
    await update_project_state(state)

    if new == AutonomyMode.COPILOT:
        await update.message.reply_text(
            "👨‍✈️ COPILOT mode.\n"
            "I'll ask at key decisions "
            "(4 options each, no typing required).\n"
            "Timeout: 1hr → auto-picks recommendation."
        )
    else:
        await update.message.reply_text(
            "🤖 AUTOPILOT mode.\n"
            "All decisions automatic. You'll be notified for: "
            "legal halts, budget breakers, completion."
        )
```

#### `/restore` — Time Travel

```python
@require_auth
async def cmd_restore(update: Update, context):
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    if not context.args:
        await update.message.reply_text(
            "Usage: /restore State_#5\nSee: /snapshots"
        )
        return

    try:
        arg = context.args[0]
        snapshot_id = (
            int(arg.replace("State_#", ""))
            if "State_#" in arg
            else int(arg)
        )
    except ValueError:
        await update.message.reply_text(
            "Invalid ID. Use: /restore State_#5"
        )
        return

    active = await get_active_project(user_id)
    if not active:
        await update.message.reply_text("No active project.")
        return

    project_id = active["project_id"]
    snapshot = (
        await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots")
        .select("stage,created_at")
        .eq("project_id", project_id)
        .eq("snapshot_id", snapshot_id)
        .single().execute()
    )
    if not snapshot.data:
        await update.message.reply_text(
            f"Snapshot #{snapshot_id} not found. Use /snapshots."
        )
        return

    keyboard = InlineKeyboardMarkup([
        [InlineKeyboardButton(
            "⏪ Confirm",
            callback_data=(
                f"restore_confirm_{project_id}_{snapshot_id}"
            ),
        )],
        [InlineKeyboardButton(
            "Cancel", callback_data="restore_cancel",
        )],
    ])
    await update.message.reply_text(
        f"⏪ Restore to #{snapshot_id}?\n"
        f"Stage: {snapshot.data['stage']}\n"
        f"Created: {snapshot.data['created_at'][:16]}\n\n"
        f"This resets Git, hides later Neo4j nodes, "
        f"resumes from that stage.",
        reply_markup=keyboard,
    )
```

#### `/snapshots` — List Snapshots

```python
@require_auth
async def cmd_snapshots(update: Update, context):
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    active = await get_active_project(user_id)
    if not active:
        await update.message.reply_text("No active project.")
        return

    snaps = (
        await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots")
        .select("snapshot_id,stage,created_at")
        .eq("project_id", active["project_id"])
        .order("snapshot_id", desc=True)
        .limit(20).execute()
    )
    if not snaps.data:
        await update.message.reply_text("No snapshots yet.")
        return

    msg = f"📸 Snapshots ({active['project_id']}):\n\n"
    for s in snaps.data:
        msg += (
            f"  #{s['snapshot_id']:3d} │ "
            f"{s['stage']:15s} │ "
            f"{s['created_at'][:16]}\n"
        )
    msg += "\n/restore State_#N to restore."
    await update.message.reply_text(msg)
```

```python
@require_auth
async def cmd_warroom(update: Update, context):
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    active = await get_active_project(user_id)
    if not active:
        await update.message.reply_text("No active project.")
        return

    state = PipelineState.model_validate(active["state_json"])
    msg = (
        "🔴 WAR ROOM ACTIVE\n\n"
        if state.war_room_active
        else "🛠️ War Room\n\n"
    )

    if not state.war_room_history:
        msg += "No activations."
    else:
        msg += f"Total: {len(state.war_room_history)}\n"
        for wr in state.war_room_history[-5:]:
            icon = "✅" if wr.get("resolved") else "❌"
            msg += (
                f"{icon} L{wr.get('level', '?')} — "
                f"{wr.get('error', '')[:80]}\n"
            )
    await update.message.reply_text(msg)
```

```python
async def cmd_legal(update: Update, context):

    active = await get_active_project(user_id)
    if not active:
        await update.message.reply_text("No active project.")

    msg = (
        f"⚖️ LEGAL HALT: {state.legal_halt_reason}\n\n"
        if state.legal_halt
        else "⚖️ Legal Log\n\n"
    )

    for check in state.legal_checks_log:
        icon = "✅" if check["passed"] else "❌"
        msg += (
            f"{icon} {check['check']} "
            f"({check['stage']}/{check['phase']})\n"
        )

    if state.legal_documents:
        msg += (
            f"\n📋 Docs: {', '.join(state.legal_documents.keys())}"
        )
    await update.message.reply_text(msg)
```

#### `/continue` — Resume Halted Pipeline

```python
@require_auth
async def cmd_continue(update: Update, context):
    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    active = await get_active_project(user_id)
    if not active:
        await update.message.reply_text("No active project.")
        return

    state = PipelineState.model_validate(active["state_json"])
    if (
        state.current_stage != Stage.HALTED
        and not state.legal_halt
        and not state.circuit_breaker_triggered
    ):
        await update.message.reply_text(
            "Pipeline running. /status to check."
        )
        return

    state.legal_halt = False
    state.legal_halt_reason = None
    state.circuit_breaker_triggered = False

    if state.current_stage == Stage.HALTED and state.previous_stage:
        state.current_stage = state.previous_stage
    await update_project_state(state)

    await update.message.reply_text(
        f"▶️ Resuming from {state.current_stage.value}..."
    )
    graph = build_pipeline_graph()
    asyncio.create_task(run_pipeline(graph, state))
```

### §5.3 Callback Handler + Free-Text Handler

```python
async def handle_callback(update: Update, context):
    query = update.callback_query
    await query.answer()
    data = query.data
    user_id = str(query.from_user.id)

    if data.startswith("mode_"):
        mode = data.replace("mode_", "")
        active = await get_active_project(user_id)
        if active:
            state = PipelineState.model_validate(active["state_json"])
            if (
                mode in ("local", "hybrid")
                and not state.local_heartbeat_alive
            ):
                await query.edit_message_text(
                    "⚠️ Local not detected. Setup Cloudflare Tunnel."
                )
                return
            state.execution_mode = ExecutionMode(mode)
            await update_project_state(state)
            emoji_map = ["☁️", "💻", "🔀"]
            idx = ["cloud", "local", "hybrid"].index(mode)
            await query.edit_message_text(
                f"{emoji_map[idx]} {mode.upper()}"
            )

    elif data.startswith("restore_confirm_"):
        _, _, project_id, snap_id = data.rsplit("_", 3)
        await query.edit_message_text("⏪ Restoring...")
        await restore_state(project_id, int(snap_id))

    elif data.startswith("cancel_confirm_"):
        pid = data.replace("cancel_confirm_", "")
        await archive_project(pid)
        await query.edit_message_text(f"🗑️ {pid} archived.")

    elif data.startswith("decision_"):
        await store_operator_decision(
            user_id, data.replace("decision_", ""),
        )


async def handle_message(update: Update, context):
    if not await authenticate_operator(update):
        return

    user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)
    op_state = await get_operator_state(user_id)

    if op_state == "awaiting_project_description":
        desc = update.message.text or ""
        attachments = []

        # ── Photo attachments ──
        if update.message.photo:
            photo = update.message.photo[-1]
            f = await photo.get_file()
            tmp_path = f"/tmp/intake_{user_id}.jpg"
            await f.download_to_drive(tmp_path)
            # v5.4.1 Patch 1: Upload to Supabase Storage for durability
            storage_url = await upload_asset_to_storage(
                user_id, tmp_path, "screenshot",
                f"intake_{user_id}.jpg",
            )
            attachments.append({
                "type": "image", "path": tmp_path,
                "storage_url": storage_url,
            })
            import os
            os.remove(tmp_path)  # Delete ephemeral /tmp copy

        # ── Voice attachments ──
        if update.message.voice:
            voice = update.message.voice
            f = await voice.get_file()
            tmp_path = f"/tmp/voice_{user_id}.ogg"
            await f.download_to_drive(tmp_path)
            transcript = await transcribe_voice(tmp_path)
            desc += f" {transcript}"
            # v5.4.1 Patch 1: Upload voice to Supabase Storage
            storage_url = await upload_asset_to_storage(
                user_id, tmp_path, "voice_memo",
                f"voice_{user_id}.ogg",
            )
            attachments.append({
                "type": "voice", "path": tmp_path,
                "storage_url": storage_url,
            })
            import os
            os.remove(tmp_path)

        # ── Document attachments ──
        if update.message.document:
            doc = update.message.document
            f = await doc.get_file()
            tmp_path = f"/tmp/doc_{user_id}_{doc.file_name}"
            await f.download_to_drive(tmp_path)
            storage_url = await upload_asset_to_storage(
                user_id, tmp_path, "document", doc.file_name,
            )
            attachments.append({
                "type": "document", "path": tmp_path,
                "storage_url": storage_url,
            })
            import os
            os.remove(tmp_path)

        await clear_operator_state(user_id)
        await _start_project(update, user_id, desc, attachments)

    elif op_state and op_state.startswith("awaiting_decision"):
        await store_operator_decision(
            user_id, update.message.text or "1",
        )
        await clear_operator_state(user_id)

    elif update.message.text:
        active = await get_active_project(user_id)
        if active:
            await update.message.reply_text(
                "Active project running. /status or /new."
            )
        else:
            await _start_project(update, user_id, update.message.text)
```

#### §5.3.1 Durable Asset Storage Helper (v5.4.1 Patch 1)

```python
async def upload_asset_to_storage(
    operator_id: str, local_path: str,
    asset_type: str, filename: str,
) -> str:
    """Upload file from /tmp to Supabase Storage. Returns durable URL."""
    project_id = (
        (await get_active_project(operator_id) or {})
        .get("project_id", operator_id)
    )
    bucket_path = f"project-assets/{project_id}/{filename}"

    with open(local_path, "rb") as f:
        await supabase_client.storage.from_(
            "project-assets"
        ).upload(bucket_path, f)

    storage_url = (
        supabase_client.storage.from_("project-assets")
        .get_public_url(bucket_path)
    )
    return storage_url

# In _start_project(), after creating PipelineState, populate brand_assets:
# for att in attachments:
#     if att.get("storage_url"):
#         state.brand_assets.append({
#             "asset_type": att["type"],
#             "filename": att.get("path", "").split("/")[-1],
#             "storage_url": att["storage_url"],
#             "uploaded_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
#         })
```

### §5.4 Notification System

```python
class NotificationType(str, Enum):
    STAGE_COMPLETE  = "stage_complete"
    DECISION_NEEDED = "decision_needed"
    LEGAL_HALT      = "legal_halt"
    BUDGET_ALERT    = "budget_alert"
    WAR_ROOM        = "war_room"
    PROJECT_COMPLETE = "project_complete"
    HEARTBEAT_LOST  = "heartbeat_lost"
    ERROR           = "error"


NOTIFICATION_FILTER = {
    AutonomyMode.AUTOPILOT: {
        NotificationType.STAGE_COMPLETE:   False,
        NotificationType.DECISION_NEEDED:  False,
        NotificationType.LEGAL_HALT:       True,
        NotificationType.BUDGET_ALERT:     True,
        NotificationType.WAR_ROOM:         False,  # Unless L3
        NotificationType.PROJECT_COMPLETE: True,
        NotificationType.HEARTBEAT_LOST:   True,
        NotificationType.ERROR:            True,
    },
    AutonomyMode.COPILOT: {
        t: True for t in NotificationType
    },
}


async def notify_operator(state, ntype, message, keyboard=None) -> bool:
    should_send = NOTIFICATION_FILTER[state.autonomy_mode].get(
        ntype, True,
    )
    if ntype == NotificationType.WAR_ROOM and state.war_room_active:
        should_send = True  # L3 always notifies

    if not should_send:
        return False

    await send_telegram_message(
        state.operator_id, message, reply_markup=keyboard,
    )
    return True
```

**Notification behavior by autonomy mode:**

| Notification | Autopilot | Copilot |
|-------------|-----------|---------|
| Stage complete | Silent | Sent |
| Decision needed | Silent (auto-picks) | Sent |
| Legal halt | **Sent** | Sent |
| Budget alert | **Sent** | Sent |
| War Room | Silent (unless L3) | Sent |
| Project complete | **Sent** | Sent |
| Heartbeat lost | **Sent** | Sent |
| Error | **Sent** | Sent |

---

### §5.5 Decision Queue (Copilot Async)

```python
from collections import defaultdict

_decision_queues: dict[str, asyncio.Queue] = defaultdict(asyncio.Queue)


async def wait_for_operator_reply(
    operator_id: str, timeout: int = 3600, default: str = "1",
) -> str:
    try:
        return await asyncio.wait_for(
            _decision_queues[operator_id].get(),
            timeout=timeout,
        )
    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
        await send_telegram_message(
            operator_id,
            f"⏰ Timeout. Auto-selected option {default}.",
        )
        return default


async def store_operator_decision(operator_id: str, decision: str):
    await _decision_queues[operator_id].put(decision)
```

```sql
CREATE TABLE operator_whitelist (
    telegram_id  TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    name         TEXT,
    invite_code  TEXT,
    created_at   TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    preferences  JSONB DEFAULT '{}'
);

CREATE TABLE operator_state (
    telegram_id  TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    state        TEXT,
    context      JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    updated_at   TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE active_projects (
    operator_id   TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    project_id    TEXT NOT NULL,
    current_stage TEXT,
    state_json    JSONB NOT NULL,
    started_at    TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at    TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE archived_projects (
    id            BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    project_id    TEXT UNIQUE,
    operator_id   TEXT,
    final_stage   TEXT,
    total_cost_usd REAL,
    state_json    JSONB NOT NULL,
    archived_at   TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE monthly_costs (
    id             BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    operator_id    TEXT,
    month          TEXT,
    project_count  INT DEFAULT 0,
    ai_total_usd   REAL DEFAULT 0,
    infra_total_usd REAL DEFAULT 0,
    UNIQUE(operator_id, month)
);
```

## Part 10: Memory & State

*PART 6 of the specification. Covers Time Machine deep dive, Delta Engine, Mother Memory v2 knowledge graph, Cross-Project Learning, Janitor Agent scheduling, Memory Growth Projections, State Consistency, and Vector Search Backend.*

---

# PART 6 — MEMORY & STATE

Time Machine · Delta Engine · Mother Memory v2 · Cross-Project Learning · Janitor Agent

---

### §6.1 Time Machine (Deep Dive)

**[M7] How It Actually Works.** The Time Machine is three `git reset --hard` + one Supabase JSON upsert + one Neo4j visibility toggle. When the operator says `/restore State_#5`, the pipeline: (1) reads snapshot #5 from the `state_snapshots` table in Supabase, (2) runs `git reset --hard <sha>` to restore code, (3) upserts the saved PipelineState JSON back to `pipeline_states`, and (4) marks all Neo4j knowledge nodes created after snapshot #5 as `:PostSnapshot` (hidden from queries, not deleted). Total latency: ~2 seconds. No "time travel database" — just coordinated rollback of three existing stores. Checksum validation (SHA-256 of state JSON) ensures the restored state matches the original. See `persist_snapshot()` and `restore_state()` implementations in §2.9.

#### §6.1.0 Restore Scope Boundary (v5.5 — FIX-10)

**CAN restore:**

1. Pipeline state JSON (stage, decisions, metadata, costs) — from Supabase `state_snapshots` table
2. Git repository code (source files, configs, legal docs) — via `git reset --hard <commit_sha>`
3. Knowledge graph visibility (Neo4j node labels toggled via `_hidden` flags) — post-snapshot nodes hidden, not deleted
4. Circuit breaker counters (reset to snapshot values) — included in PipelineState JSON

**CANNOT restore:**

1. Production app databases or user data (Firebase, Supabase app data)
2. App Store / Play Store submission state (review status, approval, listing content)
3. External billing or payment events (Apple/Google revenue, in-app purchases)
4. Third-party API state (Telegram message history, Perplexity cache, MacinCloud session logs)
5. Operator decisions made outside the pipeline (manual file edits, portal changes, email communications)

**Example — Can Do:** After a failed S3 refactor corrupts the codebase, `/restore State_#12` rolls back to the last successful S2 blueprint: Git resets to the S2 commit, pipeline state returns to S2 COMPLETE, and Mother Memory nodes created after S2 are hidden. The operator can re-run S3 with a different approach. Cost: ~2 seconds, zero API calls.

**Example — Cannot Do:** After a deployed app (S7) collects user data for 3 days, `/restore State_#15` cannot undo the user data collected in Firebase, cannot retract the app from the App Store, and cannot reverse any charges processed through in-app purchases. The pipeline state and code revert to snapshot #15, but the external world does not.

**Checksum Failure Behavior:** If SHA-256 checksum mismatch is detected during restore, the restore is aborted. The operator is notified via Telegram with: (1) the mismatched component (Git, Supabase, or Neo4j), (2) the expected vs. actual checksum, and (3) instruction to attempt restore to an earlier snapshot or perform manual recovery. The pipeline does NOT proceed with an inconsistent state.

#### §6.1.1 What Is a Snapshot?

A snapshot is an atomic triple:

```
Snapshot = (Git Commit SHA) + (Supabase JSON) + (Neo4j Node State)
```

| Component | Captures | Restored Via |
|-----------|----------|-------------|
| Git Commit | Source files, configs, legal docs | `git reset --hard <sha>` |
| Supabase JSON | Full PipelineState | Upsert into `pipeline_states` |
| Neo4j State | Knowledge nodes up to that point | Post-snapshot nodes → `:PostSnapshot` hidden |

#### §6.1.2 Snapshot Lifecycle

```
Stage completes → persist_state()
  ├─→ Supabase: upsert pipeline_states (current)
  ├─→ Supabase: INSERT state_snapshots (append-only)
  ├─→ GitHub: commit state JSON
  └─→ Backfill: git_commit_hash into snapshot row
  → snapshot_id incremented
  → Operator can: /restore State_#N
```

#### §6.1.3 Storage Budget

Each snapshot ~25 KB. Per project ~10 snapshots = 250 KB. Monthly (4 projects) ~1 MB Supabase, ~80 KB GitHub. Annual ~12 MB — well within Supabase Pro 8 GB and GitHub free unlimited.

#### §6.1.4 Snapshot Pruning

```python
SNAPSHOT_RETENTION = {
    "active_project": "ALL",
    "archived_30d":  "ALL",
    "archived_90d":  "STAGE_GATES",   # Only stage-boundary snapshots
    "archived_180d": "FIRST_LAST",
    "archived_365d": "LAST_ONLY",
}


async def prune_snapshots() -> dict:
    """Monthly. Prunes old snapshots per retention.
    Never touches active projects."""
    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
    pruned = {"total": 0}

    archives = (
        await supabase_client.table("archived_projects")
        .select("project_id, archived_at").execute()
    )

    for arch in archives.data:
        age = now - datetime.fromisoformat(arch["archived_at"])
        pid = arch["project_id"]
        if age < timedelta(days=30):
            continue

        snaps = (
            await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots")
            .select("snapshot_id, stage")
            .eq("project_id", pid)
            .order("snapshot_id").execute()
        )
        if not snaps.data or len(snaps.data) <= 2:
            continue

        keep = set()
        if age < timedelta(days=90):
            # STAGE_GATES: keep one snapshot per stage
            seen = set()
            for s in snaps.data:
                if s["stage"] not in seen:
                    keep.add(s["snapshot_id"])
                    seen.add(s["stage"])
        elif age < timedelta(days=180):
            # FIRST_LAST
            keep = {
                snaps.data[0]["snapshot_id"],
                snaps.data[-1]["snapshot_id"],
            }
        else:
            # LAST_ONLY
            keep = {snaps.data[-1]["snapshot_id"]}

        to_del = [
            s["snapshot_id"]
            for s in snaps.data
            if s["snapshot_id"] not in keep
        ]
        if to_del:
            await (
                supabase_client.table("state_snapshots")
                .delete()
                .eq("project_id", pid)
                .in_("snapshot_id", to_del)
                .execute()
            )
            pruned["total"] += len(to_del)

    return pruned
```

#### §6.1.5 Forward Restore

Time travel is bidirectional. Restoring to #5 doesn't delete #6–#10. Operator can `/restore State_#8` to go forward again.

```python
async def list_available_restores(project_id: str) -> list[dict]:
    current = (
        await supabase_client.table("pipeline_states")
        .select("snapshot_id")
        .eq("project_id", project_id)
        .single().execute()
    )
    current_id = current.data["snapshot_id"] if current.data else 0

    all_snaps = (
        await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots")
        .select("snapshot_id, stage, created_at")
        .eq("project_id", project_id)
        .order("snapshot_id").execute()
    )

    return [
        {
            **s,
            "position": (
                "past" if s["snapshot_id"] < current_id
                else "current" if s["snapshot_id"] == current_id
                else "future"
            ),
            "restorable": s["snapshot_id"] != current_id,
        }
        for s in all_snaps.data
    ]
```

---

### §6.2 Delta Engine

Computes differences between any two snapshots for progress reports, cost attribution, and rollback previews.

```python
from deepdiff import DeepDiff


async def compute_delta(
    project_id: str, from_snap: int, to_snap: int,
) -> dict:
    s1 = (
        await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots")
        .select("state_json,stage,created_at")
        .eq("project_id", project_id)
        .eq("snapshot_id", from_snap)
        .single().execute()
    ).data

    s2 = (
        await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots")
        .select("state_json,stage,created_at")
        .eq("project_id", project_id)
        .eq("snapshot_id", to_snap)
        .single().execute()
    ).data

    j1, j2 = s1["state_json"], s2["state_json"]
    from_hist = j1.get("stage_history", [])
    to_hist = j2.get("stage_history", [])
    from_files = set(
        (j1.get("s3_output") or {}).get("generated_files", {}).keys()
    )
    to_files = set(
        (j2.get("s3_output") or {}).get("generated_files", {}).keys()
    )

    return {
        "from_snapshot": from_snap,
        "to_snapshot": to_snap,
        "from_stage": s1["stage"],
        "to_stage": s2["stage"],
        "stages_traversed": [
            h["stage"] for h in to_hist[len(from_hist):]
        ],
        "files_added": len(to_files - from_files),
        "files_in_common": len(from_files & to_files),
        "cost_delta": (
            j2.get("total_cost_usd", 0)
            - j1.get("total_cost_usd", 0)
        ),
        "war_room_delta": (
            len(j2.get("war_room_history", []))
            - len(j1.get("war_room_history", []))
        ),
        "legal_checks_delta": (
            len(j2.get("legal_checks_log", []))
            - len(j1.get("legal_checks_log", []))
        ),
    }
```

---

### §6.3 Mother Memory v2 (Knowledge Graph)

**[M7] How It Actually Works.** Mother Memory is a Neo4j AuraDB graph database (GA, $65/mo) storing 7 node types and 10 relationship types. When the pipeline starts a new project, it queries Mother Memory for: past error patterns matching the current stack (`ErrorPattern` nodes), reusable UI components (`Component` nodes with high `success_count`), and regulatory decisions that haven't expired (`RegulatoryDecision` nodes). These queries use standard Cypher, not vector search. Vector similarity search (for finding similar components) uses pgvector [C8] by default. Neo4j is used purely for graph traversal (relationship patterns). The Janitor Agent prunes stale nodes weekly. There is no "memory" in the AI model sense — it's a queryable database that the pipeline reads before each stage.

**[FIX-11] Storage Scope:** Mother Memory stores knowledge nodes (patterns, decisions, relationships, metadata references) — not raw binary assets. Binary brand assets (logos, images, fonts, certificates, provisioning profiles) are stored in Git (committed to project repo) and/or Supabase Storage (for large binaries via `upload_to_temp_storage()` [C3]). Mother Memory may store metadata nodes that reference these assets (hash, URI, timestamps, design DNA extracted from them) but never the binary content itself. Example: a `DesignDNA` node stores `color_palette: {primary: "#1A73E8"}` and `logo_hash: "a3f8..."` — but the actual logo file lives in Git at `/assets/logo.png`.

#### §6.3.1 Node Schema

```cypher
// Core (preserved from v3.6)
(:Project {
    id, name, description, stack, business_model,
    completed, total_cost_usd, created_at, completed_at,
    screen_names
})

(:Component {
    id, type, name, stack, code_hash,
    success_count, failure_count, created_at
})

(:RegulatoryDecision {
    id, body, feature, decision, conditions,
    date, expires_at
})

(:ErrorPattern {
    id, error_signature, stack, fix_description,
    fix_code, war_room_level, occurrences, last_seen
})

// New v5.4
(:StackPattern {
    id, stack, pattern_type, description, code_template,
    dependencies, success_rate, used_in_projects, created_at
})

(:DesignDNA {
    id, category, color_palette, typography, spacing,
    visual_style, approval_rate, used_in_projects
})

(:LegalDocTemplate {
    id, doc_type, business_model, template_hash,
    quality_score, used_in_projects
})

(:Graveyard {
    id, original_label, archived_at, archived_reason
})

// [FIX-27] Operator Handoff Intelligence Pack documentation
(:HandoffDoc {
    project_id,          // Project that generated this doc
    program_id,          // Program group (null for single-stack)
    stack,               // Tech stack (e.g., "react_native")
    app_category,        // App category (e.g., "restaurant_booking")
    doc_type,            // e.g., "quick_start", "emergency_runbook"
    filename,            // e.g., "QUICK_START.md"
    content,             // Full Markdown content (capped at 50KB)
    generated_at,        // Generation timestamp
    permanent            // Always true — exempt from Janitor pruning
})
```

#### §6.3.2 Relationships

```cypher
(:Project)-[:USES_STACK]->(:StackPattern)
(:Project)-[:USED_COMPONENT]->(:Component)
(:Project)-[:APPLIED_DESIGN]->(:DesignDNA)
(:Project)-[:GENERATED_DOC]->(:LegalDocTemplate)
(:Project)-[:ENCOUNTERED_ERROR]->(:ErrorPattern)
(:Project)-[:HAS_DECISION]->(:RegulatoryDecision)
(:Project)-[:HAS_HANDOFF_DOC {doc_type: str}]->(:HandoffDoc)  // [FIX-27]
(:Component)-[:DEPENDS_ON]->(:Component)
(:Component)-[:REPLACES]->(:Component)
(:ErrorPattern)-[:FIXED_BY]->(:Component)
(:DesignDNA)-[:DERIVED_FROM]->(:DesignDNA)
```

#### §6.3.3 Query Functions

```python
async def query_mother_memory(
    stack: str, screens: list[str], auth_method: str,
) -> dict:
    """Find reusable components + auth patterns
    for this stack and screens."""
    components = await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (c:Component)
        WHERE c.stack = $stack
          AND c.success_count > 0
          AND c.failure_count < c.success_count
          AND NOT c:Graveyard AND NOT c:PostSnapshot
        OPTIONAL MATCH (c)<-[:USED_COMPONENT]-(p:Project)
        WHERE ANY(s IN $screens WHERE s IN p.screen_names)
        WITH c, count(p) AS relevance,
          toFloat(c.success_count)
          / (c.success_count + c.failure_count) AS rate
        RETURN c.id AS id, c.type AS type,
               c.name AS name, rate, relevance
        ORDER BY rate * (1 + relevance) DESC
        LIMIT 20
    """, {"stack": stack, "screens": screens})

    auth = []
    if auth_method != "none":
        auth = await neo4j_run("""
            MATCH (sp:StackPattern)
            WHERE sp.stack = $stack
              AND sp.pattern_type = 'auth_flow'
              AND sp.success_rate > 0.7
              AND NOT sp:Graveyard
            RETURN sp.code_template AS template,
                   sp.success_rate AS rate
            ORDER BY rate DESC LIMIT 3
        """, {"stack": stack})

    return {
        "reusable_components": [dict(r) for r in components],
        "auth_patterns": [dict(r) for r in auth],
    }


async def query_error_fixes(
    error_sig: str, stack: str,
) -> list[dict]:
    """Find known fixes for an error pattern."""
    import re
    norm = re.sub(
        r'line \d+', 'line N',
        re.sub(r'/[\w/]+\.\w+', 'FILE', error_sig),
    )

    results = await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (ep:ErrorPattern)
        WHERE ep.stack = $stack
          AND ep.error_signature CONTAINS $frag
          AND NOT ep:Graveyard
        RETURN ep.fix_description AS desc,
               ep.fix_code AS code,
               ep.war_room_level AS level,
               ep.occurrences AS seen
        ORDER BY ep.occurrences DESC LIMIT 5
    """, {"stack": stack, "frag": norm[:200]})
    return [dict(r) for r in results]


async def query_design_dna(category: str) -> list[dict]:
    results = await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (d:DesignDNA)
        WHERE d.category = $cat
          AND d.approval_rate > 0.5
          AND NOT d:Graveyard
        RETURN d.color_palette AS palette,
               d.typography AS typo,
               d.spacing AS spacing,
               d.visual_style AS style,
               d.approval_rate AS rate
        ORDER BY d.approval_rate * d.used_in_projects DESC
        LIMIT 5
    """, {"cat": category})

    for r in results:
        for f in ("palette", "typo", "spacing"):
            if isinstance(r[f], str):
                r[f] = json.loads(r[f])
    return [dict(r) for r in results]


async def query_legal_templates(
    doc_type: str, biz_model: str,
) -> Optional[dict]:
    result = await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (lt:LegalDocTemplate)
        WHERE lt.doc_type = $dt
          AND lt.business_model = $bm
          AND lt.quality_score > 0.7
          AND NOT lt:Graveyard
        RETURN lt.template_hash AS hash,
               lt.quality_score AS score
        ORDER BY score DESC LIMIT 1
    """, {"dt": doc_type, "bm": biz_model})
    return dict(result[0]) if result else None
```

#### §6.3.4 Storage Functions

```python
async def store_project_patterns(
    project_id, stack, screens, success, war_room_count,
):
    await neo4j_run("""
        MERGE (p:Project {id: $pid})
        SET p.completed = $ok,
            p.stack = $stk,
            p.screen_names = $scr,
            p.completed_at = datetime(),
            p.war_room_count = $wr
    """, {
        "pid": project_id,
        "ok": success,
        "stk": stack.value,
        "scr": [s["name"] for s in screens],
        "wr": war_room_count,
    })

    count_field = "success_count" if success else "failure_count"
    await neo4j_run(f"""
        MATCH (p:Project {{id: $pid}})-[:USED_COMPONENT]->(c:Component)
        SET c.{count_field} = c.{count_field} + 1
    """, {"pid": project_id})


async def store_error_pattern(error, stack, fix, level):
    import re, hashlib
    norm = re.sub(
        r'line \d+', 'line N',
        re.sub(r'/[\w/]+\.\w+', 'FILE', error),
    )
    sig = hashlib.sha256(norm[:500].encode()).hexdigest()[:16]

    await neo4j_run("""
        MERGE (ep:ErrorPattern {id: $id})
        ON CREATE SET
            ep.error_signature = $sig,
            ep.stack = $stk,
            ep.fix_description = $fix,
            ep.war_room_level = $lvl,
            ep.occurrences = 1,
            ep.last_seen = datetime(),
            ep.created_at = datetime()
        ON MATCH SET
            ep.occurrences = ep.occurrences + 1,
            ep.last_seen = datetime(),
            ep.fix_description = $fix
    """, {
        "id": f"err_{sig}",
        "sig": norm[:500],
        "stk": stack,
        "fix": fix[:2000],
        "lvl": level,
    })


async def store_design_dna(project_id, category, design):
    import hashlib
    h = hashlib.sha256(
        json.dumps(design, sort_keys=True).encode()
    ).hexdigest()[:16]

    await neo4j_run("""
        MERGE (d:DesignDNA {id: $id})
        ON CREATE SET
            d.category = $cat,
            d.color_palette = $p,
            d.typography = $t,
            d.spacing = $s,
            d.visual_style = $vs,
            d.approval_rate = 0.5,
            d.used_in_projects = 1,
            d.created_at = datetime()
        ON MATCH SET
            d.used_in_projects = d.used_in_projects + 1
    """, {
        "id": f"design_{h}",
        "cat": category,
        "p": json.dumps(design.get("color_palette", {})),
        "t": json.dumps(design.get("typography", {})),
        "s": json.dumps(design.get("spacing", {})),
        "vs": design.get("visual_style", "minimal"),
    })

    await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (p:Project {id: $pid}), (d:DesignDNA {id: $did})
        MERGE (p)-[:APPLIED_DESIGN]->(d)
    """, {"pid": project_id, "did": f"design_{h}"})


# ═══ [FIX-27] Handoff Intelligence Pack storage ═══
async def store_handoff_docs_in_memory(
    project_id: str,
    program_id: Optional[str],
    stack: str,
    app_category: str,
    docs: dict,
) -> None:
    """
    Persist Handoff Intelligence Pack documents as HandoffDoc nodes
    in Mother Memory (Neo4j).  [FIX-27]

    Each document becomes a node with:
    - project_id, program_id, stack, app_category for cross-project lookup
    - doc_type derived from filename
    - content stored as text property
    - No TTL — Janitor treats these as permanent (high-value operator knowledge)

    Enables: future projects in same category can reference prior handoff
    docs to produce better, more informed guidance.
    """
    for filename, content in docs.items():
        if filename.startswith("_"):
            continue  # Skip meta-entries like _PROGRAM_DOCS_DEFERRED

        doc_type = filename.replace(".md", "").lower()

        await neo4j_run("""
            MERGE (d:HandoffDoc {
                project_id: $pid,
                doc_type: $dtype
            })
            SET d.program_id = $pgid,
                d.stack = $stk,
                d.app_category = $cat,
                d.content = $content,
                d.filename = $fname,
                d.generated_at = datetime(),
                d.permanent = true
            WITH d
            MATCH (p:Project {id: $pid})
            MERGE (p)-[:HAS_HANDOFF_DOC {doc_type: $dtype}]->(d)
        """, {
            "pid": project_id,
            "pgid": program_id,
            "stk": stack,
            "cat": app_category,
            "content": content[:50000],  # Cap at 50KB per doc
            "dtype": doc_type,
            "fname": filename,
        })
```

---

### §6.4 Cross-Project Learning

#### §6.4.1 War Room Memory Pre-Check

```python
async def war_room_consult_memory(
    state, error,
) -> Optional[dict]:
    """Check Mother Memory before War Room starts.
    Skip L1 if known fix exists."""
    stack = (
        state.selected_stack.value
        if state.selected_stack
        else "unknown"
    )
    fixes = await query_error_fixes(error, stack)
    if not fixes:
        return None

    best = fixes[0]
    if best["seen"] >= 3 and best.get("code"):
        return {
            "source": "mother_memory",
            "fix_code": best["code"],
            "confidence": min(best["seen"] / 10, 1.0),
        }

    return {
        "source": "hint",
        "hint": best["desc"],
        "previous_level": best["level"],
    }
```

#### §6.4.2 Pattern Extraction (Post-Project)

```python
async def extract_and_store_patterns(
    project_id, blueprint, files,
) -> int:
    stack = blueprint.selected_stack.value
    stored = 0

    pattern_extractors = [
        (
            "auth", "auth_flow",
            lambda k: "auth" in k.lower(),
            blueprint.auth_method != "none",
        ),
        (
            "nav", "navigation",
            lambda k: "nav" in k.lower() or "router" in k.lower(),
            True,
        ),
        (
            "payment", "payment_integration",
            lambda k: any(
                p in k.lower()
                for p in ("payment", "checkout", "cart", "mada")
            ),
            blueprint.payment_mode != "none",
        ),
    ]

    for prefix, ptype, file_filter, condition in pattern_extractors:
        if not condition:
            continue
        matched = {
            k: v for k, v in files.items() if file_filter(k)
        }
        if not matched:
            continue

        pid = (
            f"pattern_{stack}_{prefix}_"
            f"{blueprint.auth_method if prefix == 'auth' "
            f"else len(blueprint.screens)}"
        )
        await neo4j_run("""
            MERGE (sp:StackPattern {id: $id})
            ON CREATE SET
                sp.stack = $stk,
                sp.pattern_type = $pt,
                sp.description = $desc,
                sp.code_template = $code,
                sp.success_rate = 1.0,
                sp.used_in_projects = 1,
                sp.created_at = datetime()
            ON MATCH SET
                sp.used_in_projects = sp.used_in_projects + 1,
                sp.updated_at = datetime()
        """, {
            "id": pid,
            "stk": stack,
            "pt": ptype,
            "desc": f"{ptype} for {stack}",
            "code": json.dumps(matched)[:5000],
        })
        stored += 1

    return stored
```

### §6.5 Janitor Agent Scheduling

```python
JANITOR_SCHEDULE = {
    "janitor_clean":    "every 6 hours",
    "snapshot_prune":   "1st of month",
    "memory_stats":     "every 24 hours",
    "heartbeat_check":  "every 30 seconds (in-process)",
}


async def collect_memory_stats() -> dict:
    counts = await neo4j_run("""
        CALL db.labels() YIELD label
        CALL apoc.cypher.run(
            'MATCH (n:' + label + ') RETURN count(n) AS c', {}
        ) YIELD value
        RETURN label, value.c AS count
    """)

    graveyard = await neo4j_run(
        "MATCH (g:Graveyard) RETURN count(g) AS c"
    )
    success = await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (c:Component)
        WHERE c.success_count + c.failure_count > 0
          AND NOT c:Graveyard
        RETURN avg(
            toFloat(c.success_count)
            / (c.success_count + c.failure_count)
        ) AS rate
    """)
    errors = await neo4j_run(
        "MATCH (ep:ErrorPattern) "
        "WHERE NOT ep:Graveyard "
        "RETURN count(ep) AS c"
    )

    stats = {
        "node_counts": {
            r["label"]: r["count"] for r in counts
        },
        "graveyard": graveyard[0]["c"] if graveyard else 0,
        "avg_component_success": (
            success[0]["rate"] if success else 0
        ),
        "error_patterns": errors[0]["c"] if errors else 0,
    }

    await supabase_client.table("memory_stats").insert({
        "stats": stats,
        "collected_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
    }).execute()
    return stats
```

### §6.6 Memory Growth Projections

| Metric | Month 1 | Month 6 | Month 12 |
|--------|---------|---------|----------|
| Projects | 4 | 24 | 48 |
| Components | ~40 | ~150 | ~200 |
| StackPatterns | ~12 | ~40 | ~60 |
| ErrorPatterns | ~20 | ~80 | ~120 |
| DesignDNA | ~4 | ~15 | ~25 |
| HandoffDocs [FIX-27] | ~16 | ~96 | ~192 |
| Graveyard | 0 | ~30 | ~80 |
| Neo4j storage | ~6 MB | ~30 MB | ~50 MB |
| Supabase storage | ~2 MB | ~10 MB | ~18 MB |

The factory gets smarter over time: fewer War Room L3 escalations, faster code generation, better mocks, faster DocuGen. HandoffDocs accumulate permanently (~4 per project) and enable cross-project learning — future handoff quality improves as the pipeline builds more apps in the same category.
