## 8.3  v3.6 → v5.6 Migration Map

### 8.3.1  Breaking Changes

| Component | v3.6 State | v5.4 State | Migration Action |
|-----------|-----------|-----------|-----------------|
| `PipelineState.ff_project_id` | Direct field | Inside `project_metadata` | Move to `project_metadata["ff_project_id"]` |
| `PipelineState.ff_pages` | Direct field | Inside `project_metadata` | Move to `project_metadata["ff_pages"]` |
| `PipelineState.ff_collections` | Direct field | Inside `project_metadata` | Move to `project_metadata["ff_collections"]` |
| `PipelineState.yaml_blocks` | Direct field | Inside `project_metadata` | Move to `project_metadata["yaml_blocks"]` |
| OpenAI API key | Required | Optional | Remove from `REQUIRED_SECRETS` |
| Perplexity API key | Not present | Required | Add `PERPLEXITY_API_KEY` |
| AI model routing | Ad-hoc | Role contracts | Replace all `call_claude()` with `call_ai(role, ...)` |
| Error handling | Simple retry | War Room L1→L2→L3 | Replace retry loops with `war_room_escalate()` |
| State persistence | Dual-write | Triple-write + snapshots | Add `state_snapshots` table, add Git commit |
| Neo4j schema | 4 node types | 7 node types + Graveyard | Run Neo4j migration, add new constraints |
| Supabase schema | `pipeline_states` only | 8 tables | Run Supabase migration |


### 8.3.2  Migration Script

```python
async def migrate_v36_to_v54():
    """
    One-time migration. Run before first v5.4 project.
    Preserves all v3.6 data while upgrading schema.
    """
    print("═══ v3.6 → v5.4 Migration ═══\n")

    # ── 1. Supabase schema upgrade ──
    print("[1/5] Upgrading Supabase schema...")

    # Add new columns to pipeline_states
    await supabase_run_sql("""
        ALTER TABLE pipeline_states
        ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS snapshot_id       INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS selected_stack     TEXT DEFAULT 'flutterflow',
        ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS execution_mode     TEXT DEFAULT 'cloud',
        ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS autonomy_mode      TEXT DEFAULT 'autopilot',
        ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS project_metadata   JSONB DEFAULT '{}';
    """)

    # Create new tables
    await supabase_run_sql("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS state_snapshots (
            id              BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
            project_id      TEXT NOT NULL,
            snapshot_id     INTEGER NOT NULL,
            stage           TEXT NOT NULL,
            state_json      JSONB NOT NULL,
            git_commit_hash TEXT,
            created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
            UNIQUE(project_id, snapshot_id)
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS operator_whitelist (
            telegram_id  TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            name         TEXT,
            created_at   TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
            preferences  JSONB DEFAULT '{}'
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS operator_state (
            telegram_id  TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            state        TEXT,
            updated_at   TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS active_projects (
            operator_id    TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            project_id     TEXT NOT NULL,
            current_stage  TEXT,
            state_json     JSONB NOT NULL,
            started_at     TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS archived_projects (
            id             BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
            project_id     TEXT UNIQUE,
            operator_id    TEXT,
            final_stage    TEXT,
            total_cost_usd REAL,
            state_json     JSONB NOT NULL,
            archived_at    TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS monthly_costs (
            id              BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
            operator_id     TEXT,
            month           TEXT,
            project_count   INT DEFAULT 0,
            ai_total_usd    REAL DEFAULT 0,
            infra_total_usd REAL DEFAULT 0,
            UNIQUE(operator_id, month)
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS audit_log (
            id          BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
            operator_id TEXT,
            project_id  TEXT,
            action      TEXT NOT NULL,
            details     JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
            timestamp   TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS pipeline_metrics (
            id             BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
            project_id     TEXT,
            stack          TEXT,
            completed      BOOLEAN,
            total_cost_usd REAL,
            timestamp      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS memory_stats (
            id           BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
            stats        JSONB,
            collected_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
        );
    """)

    # ── 2. Migrate existing pipeline_states ──
    print("[2/5] Migrating existing project states...")

    existing = await supabase_client.table("pipeline_states") \
        .select("*").execute()

    for row in existing.data:
        state = row.get("state_json", {})

        # Move FF-specific fields into project_metadata
        metadata = {}
        for ff_field in [
            "ff_project_id", "ff_pages", "ff_collections", "yaml_blocks"
        ]:
            if ff_field in state:
                metadata[ff_field] = state.pop(ff_field)

        state["project_metadata"]  = metadata
        state["selected_stack"]    = "flutterflow"   # v3.6 was FF-only
        state["execution_mode"]    = "cloud"
        state["autonomy_mode"]     = "autopilot"
        state["snapshot_id"]       = 0
        state["phase_costs"]       = state.get("phase_costs", {})
        state["war_room_history"]  = state.get("war_room_history", [])
        state["legal_checks_log"]  = state.get("legal_checks_log", [])

        await supabase_client.table("pipeline_states") \
            .update({
                "state_json":     state,
                "selected_stack": "flutterflow",
                "snapshot_id":    0,
            }) \
            .eq("project_id", row["project_id"]).execute()

    # ── 3. Neo4j schema upgrade ──
    print("[3/5] Upgrading Neo4j schema...")

    # Add new constraints
    await neo4j_run(
        "CREATE CONSTRAINT IF NOT EXISTS "
        "FOR (sp:StackPattern) REQUIRE sp.id IS UNIQUE"
    )
    await neo4j_run(
        "CREATE CONSTRAINT IF NOT EXISTS "
        "FOR (d:DesignDNA) REQUIRE d.id IS UNIQUE"
    )
    await neo4j_run(
        "CREATE CONSTRAINT IF NOT EXISTS "
        "FOR (lt:LegalDocTemplate) REQUIRE lt.id IS UNIQUE"
    )
    await neo4j_run(
        "CREATE CONSTRAINT IF NOT EXISTS "
        "FOR (g:Graveyard) REQUIRE g.id IS UNIQUE"
    )
    await neo4j_run(
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS "
        "FOR (c:Component) ON (c.stack)"
    )
    await neo4j_run(
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS "
        "FOR (ep:ErrorPattern) ON (ep.stack)"
    )
    await neo4j_run(
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS "
        "FOR (sp:StackPattern) ON (sp.stack, sp.pattern_type)"
    )

    # Seed initial FlutterFlow stack patterns from v3.6 components
    await neo4j_run("""
        MATCH (c:Component) WHERE c.stack IS NULL
        SET c.stack = 'flutterflow'
    """)

    # ── 4. Verify migration ──
    print("[4/5] Verifying migration...")

    # Check all tables exist
    tables = [
        "pipeline_states", "state_snapshots", "operator_whitelist",
        "active_projects", "archived_projects", "monthly_costs",
        "audit_log", "pipeline_metrics", "memory_stats"
    ]
    for table in tables:
        result = await supabase_client.table(table) \
            .select("count").limit(1).execute()
        print(f"  ✅ {table}")

    # Check Neo4j constraints
    constraints = await neo4j_run("SHOW CONSTRAINTS")
    print(f"  ✅ Neo4j: {len(constraints)} constraints")

    # ── 5. Create initial snapshot for existing projects ──
    print("[5/5] Creating initial snapshots...")

    for row in existing.data:
        await supabase_client.table("state_snapshots").insert({
            "project_id":  row["project_id"],
            "snapshot_id": 0,
            "stage":       row.get("current_stage", "S0_INTAKE"),
            "state_json":  row["state_json"],
        }).execute()

    print(f"\n✅ Migration complete! {len(existing.data)} projects migrated.")
```

---

## 8.4  ADR Updates (Addendum to Part 1)

### New ADRs for v5.4

| ADR | Title | Decision |
|-----|-------|----------|
| ADR-018 | Polyglot State Model | Use `project_metadata: dict` with stack-specific Pydantic validators instead of per-stack state fields |
| ADR-019 | AI Role Contracts | Hardcode 4 immutable role contracts (Scout/Strategist/Engineer/QuickFix) with code-enforced boundaries |
| ADR-020 | War Room Escalation | 3-level escalation (Haiku→Scout+Sonnet→Opus) instead of flat retry loops |
| ADR-021 | Stack Selector Brain | Strategist selects stack at S2 using criteria dict, not hardcoded to FlutterFlow |
| ADR-022 | Triple-Write Persistence | Current state + append-only snapshots + Git commits for time travel |
| ADR-023 | Circuit Breaker Threshold | $2.00/phase hard limit. Chosen because typical phase costs $0.10–$1.50; $2 catches runaway loops without blocking normal work |
| ADR-024 | Copilot 4-Way Decisions | Always exactly 4 options (3 AI + 1 custom). Reduces operator cognitive load vs. open-ended questions |
| ADR-025 | Design Engine (Vibe Check) | AI-driven design discovery replaces static templates. Grid Enforcer validates programmatically |
| ADR-026 | Snapshot Retention Policy | 5-tier pruning (all → stage-gates → first-last → last-only) balances storage vs. recovery ability |
| ADR-027 | Forward Restore | Snapshots are never deleted by `/restore`. Bidirectional time travel preserves all history |
| ADR-028 | Degraded Mode | Pipeline continues with reduced capability when non-critical services (Neo4j, Perplexity, GitHub) are down |
| ADR-029 | Input Sanitization | All operator text filtered for prompt injection and shell injection before processing |
| ADR-030 | Immutable Audit Log | Supabase RLS: insert-only, no update/delete. Compliance trail for KSA regulatory audits |

### v5.4.1 Patch ADRs

| ADR | Title | Decision |
|-----|-------|----------|
| ADR-031 | Binary Assets to Supabase Storage | Upload all intake artifacts from `/tmp` to Supabase Storage immediately; store durable URL in `brand_assets[]`; delete `/tmp` reference |
| ADR-032 | Per-Role Circuit Breaker | Replace flat $2/phase with 8 role-aware limits ($2–$25); add $25/project and $80/month global caps |
| ADR-033 | Perplexity Model Deprecation | Remove `sonar-reasoning`; use `sonar`, `sonar-pro`, `sonar-reasoning-pro` only |
| ADR-034 | FlutterFlow Growth Plan | Standard Plan discontinued; Growth at $80/mo is minimum for API/Git access |
| ADR-035 | Transactional Snapshot Writes | Wrap triple-write in try/catch/rollback; compute snapshot checksum after success |
| ADR-036 | Stuck Project Auto-Recovery | 15-min Cloud Scheduler detects stale projects; auto-resumes from last completed stage |
| ADR-037 | Preflight Compliance Gate | Non-blocking App Store guidelines check at end of S1; logs `StorePolicyEvent` nodes |
| ADR-038 | One Stack Per Project | Explicit constraint; multi-stack apps split into separate projects with shared Mother Memory |
| ADR-039 | Model Abstraction Layer | All model version strings via `MODEL_CONFIG` env var overrides with sensible defaults |
| ADR-040 | DocuGen Requires Legal Review | All AI-generated legal docs flagged `REQUIRES_LEGAL_REVIEW`; operator notified via Telegram |
| ADR-041 | pgvector Fallback | `VECTOR_BACKEND=pgvector` env var enables Supabase pgvector when Neo4j costs exceed threshold |
| ADR-042 | Failover = Resume-from-Checkpoint | Auto-failover does not transfer in-progress local state; resumes from last persisted snapshot |

### v5.4.2 + v5.6 Patch ADRs

| ADR | Title | Decision |
|-----|-------|----------|
| ADR-043 | Runtime Model Override for Emergency Downgrade | [FIX-03] `{ROLE}_MODEL_OVERRIDE` env vars allow emergency model swap without redeployment. Precedence: operator override > Budget Governor > default chain. Invalid overrides rejected with Telegram warning. |
| ADR-044 | Graduated Budget Degradation | [FIX-05] Budget Governor module with 4 tiers: GREEN (0-79%), AMBER (80-94%, degrade models), RED (95-99%, block intake), BLACK (100%, hard stop). Wraps existing circuit breaker. Disabled via `BUDGET_GOVERNOR_ENABLED=false`. |
| ADR-045 | Strict Compliance Enforcement with Operator Override | [FIX-06] When `STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE=true` and `ComplianceGateResult` has blockers with confidence >0.7: pipeline HALTED. `/force_continue` requires typed "I accept compliance risk" confirmation. Default remains false (advisory). |
| ADR-046 | Pre-Deploy Operator Acknowledgment Gate | [FIX-08] Mandatory Telegram confirmation between S5→S6. Copilot: `/deploy_confirm` required. Autopilot: 15-min auto-approve timer. 1-hour unresponsive timeout triggers auto-approval per DR Scenario #10. Race protection via C6 advisory lock. |

### v5.6 Clean Room ADRs

| ADR | Title | Decision |
|-----|-------|----------|
| ADR-047 | Version Hygiene Enforcement | [FIX-16] Automated `spec_lint.py` for version contamination. All governance text references v5.6; CI blocks v5.4/v5.5 string literals. |
| ADR-048 | Budget Buffer Segmentation | [FIX-17] $544.70 split into 4 purpose-specific reserves: $200 GCP (infra), $200 AI (model costs), $100 variable services, $44.70 float (exchange rate). |
| ADR-049 | Scout Context-Tier Ceiling | [FIX-19] `SCOUT_MAX_CONTEXT_TIER` env var prevents cost spikes. Enforcement in `call_perplexity_safe()` caps context window selection. |
| ADR-050 | Telegram-Native Operator Recovery | [FIX-20] 3AM runbook uses only `/admin` commands. GCP Console instructions moved to §7.3.2a Advanced. |
| ADR-051 | Operator Handoff Intelligence Pack | [FIX-27] S8 generates 4 per-project docs (Quick Start, Emergency Runbook, Service Map, Update Guide) + 3 per-program docs (Integration Test Checklist, Architecture Overview, Cross-Service Troubleshooting) for multi-stack splits. All docs use real project values, stored as permanent HandoffDoc nodes in Mother Memory. Cost: ~$0.30–$0.50/project, ~$0.50–$0.80 multi-stack. Janitor-exempt. |

## 8.6  Implementation Priority Order

Build in this order to get to first working project fastest:

| Phase | Files | What It Enables | Effort |
|-------|-------|----------------|--------|
| **P0: Core** | `state.py`, `roles.py`, `stages.py`, `secrets.py` | State model + role enforcement compiles | 1 day |
| **P1: Telegram** | `bot.py`, `commands.py`, `messages.py` | `/start`, `/new`, `/status` work | 1 day |
| **P2: Pipeline Shell** | `graph.py`, `s0_intake.py` through `s8_handoff.py` (stubs) | Full DAG runs end-to-end with mocks | 1 day |
| **P3: Intelligence** | `perplexity.py`, `strategist.py`, `circuit_breaker.py` | Scout + Strategist produce real outputs | 1 day |
| **P4: FlutterFlow** | S3 FF generator, S4 GUI automation, `gui_automation.py` | First real app built (FF stack) | 2 days |
| **P5: State** | `persistence.py`, `snapshots.py`, `supabase.py`, `github.py` | Triple-write + time travel works | 1 day |
| **P6: Memory** | `neo4j_client.py`, `queries.py`, `storage.py`, `janitor.py` | Mother Memory learns from first project | 1 day |
| **P7: Design** | `design_engine.py`, `docugen.py` | Vibe Check + legal docs generated | 1 day |
| **P8: Other Stacks** | RN, Swift, Kotlin generators in S3 | Polyglot code generation | 2 days |
| **P9: Ops** | `health.py`, `metrics.py`, `security/*`, migration | Production hardening | 1 day |

**Total: ~12 days to full implementation from spec.**

## 8.7  Final Architecture Summary

```
         OPERATOR (Telegram)
              │
        ┌─────┴──────┐
        │  TELEGRAM   │
        │  COMMAND    │  13 commands + free-text + media
        │  CENTER     │  Autopilot / Copilot mode
        └─────┬──────┘
              │
        ┌─────┴──────┐
        │  PIPELINE   │  S0→S1→S2→S3→S4→S5→S6→S7→S8
        │  DAG        │  LangGraph state machine
        │             │  @pipeline_node decorator
        └─────┬──────┘
              │
   ┌──────────┼──────────┐
   │          │          │
┌──┴───┐  ┌──┴───┐  ┌──┴───┐
│ INTEL│  │ EXEC │  │STATE │
│ LAYER│  │ LAYER│  │LAYER │
│      │  │      │  │      │
│Scout │  │Cloud │  │Supa  │
│Strat │  │Local │  │Neo4j │
│Engr  │  │Hybrid│  │GitHub│
│QFix  │  │GUI   │  │Snaps │
└──────┘  └──────┘  └──────┘
   │          │          │
   └──────────┼──────────┘
              │
   ┌──────────┼──────────┐
   │          │          │
┌──┴───┐  ┌──┴───┐  ┌──┴───┐
│SAFETY│  │MEMORY│  │LEGAL │
│      │  │      │  │      │
│Circui│  │Mother│  │Contin│
│Breake│  │Memory│  │Thread│
│UserSp│  │Janit │  │DocuGe│
│Audit │  │Patte │  │RegMap│
└──────┘  └──────┘  └──────┘
```

### What v5.4 Achieves Over v3.6

1. **Universal**: 6 tech stacks instead of 1 (FlutterFlow-only → any mobile/web/backend/game)
2. **Intelligent**: 4 specialized AI roles with enforced boundaries instead of ad-hoc model calls
3. **Resilient**: 3-level War Room + cross-project error memory instead of simple retry loops
4. **Time-Traveling**: Bidirectional snapshot restore instead of no recovery
5. **Legal**: Continuous compliance thread S1→S8 instead of single-gate
6. **Autonomous**: Variable Autopilot/Copilot with 4-way decisions instead of all-or-nothing
7. **Flexible**: Cloud/Local/Hybrid execution instead of cloud-only
8. **Safe**: $2/phase circuit breaker, user-space enforcement, audit log, input sanitization
9. **Learning**: Mother Memory v2 with 7 node types, Janitor Agent, pattern extraction
10. **Designed**: AI-driven Vibe Check + Grid Enforcer instead of manual templates


### Cost Per App (Average)

```
Variable per project (from BUDGET_CONFIG):
  AI calls:    ~$8.44  (Opus $1.44 + Sonnet $5.25 + Haiku $0.55
                         + Perplexity $1.15 + UI-TARS $3.00)
  MacinCloud:  ~$7.50  (~7.5 hrs × $1/hr)
  ─────────────────────────
  Per app variable: ~$18.89

Fixed monthly (from BUDGET_CONFIG) [FIX-01]:
  Neo4j + Supabase + FlutterFlow + DNS + Apple Dev = $179.75
  Per app share:  ~$44.94  (÷4 projects)

Per app total:   ~$63.83 (239.35 SAR)
Monthly (4 apps): ~$255.30 (957.38 SAR)
Annual:          ~$3,064 (11,489 SAR)
```

**An app that would cost $5,000–$50,000 from a developer is built for ~$14.**

## 8.8  What's NOT In v5.6 (Deliberate Exclusions)

| Excluded | Reason | Future Version? |
|----------|--------|-----------------|
| Web dashboard | Telegram is sufficient for solo operator | v6.0 if multi-operator |
| Multi-operator support | Solo operator assumed | v6.0 |
| A/B testing | Overkill for MVP apps | v6.0 |
| Analytics integration | Operator can add manually | v5.6 |
| CI/CD pipeline monitoring | GitHub Actions UI is sufficient | v5.6 |
| Custom domain management | Operator handles DNS | v5.6 |
| Billing/invoicing | Solo operator doesn't invoice themselves | v6.0 |
| Voice interface | Telegram voice input is transcribed; no conversational AI | v6.0 |

## 8.9  Environment Variable Reference (v5.6)

All environment variables used by the pipeline, with defaults and governing section.

| Variable | Default | Section | Purpose |
|----------|---------|---------|---------|
| `GCP_PROJECT_ID` | *(required)* | §7.7.1 | Google Cloud project ID |
| `STRATEGIST_MODEL` | `claude-opus-4-6` | §2.6 | Opus model for strategic decisions |
| `ENGINEER_MODEL` | `claude-sonnet-4-5-20250929` | §2.6 | Sonnet model for code generation |
| `QUICKFIX_MODEL` | `claude-haiku-4-5-20251001` | §2.6 | Haiku model for quick fixes |
| `GUI_SUPERVISOR_MODEL` | `claude-haiku-4-5-20251001` | §2.6 | Haiku model for GUI supervision |
| `SCOUT_MODEL` | `sonar-pro` | §2.6 | Perplexity search model |
| `SCOUT_REASONING_MODEL` | `sonar-reasoning-pro` | §2.6 | Perplexity reasoning model |
| `SCOUT_MAX_CONTEXT_TIER` | `medium` | §2.6 | [FIX-19] `small\|medium\|large` — controls Perplexity query depth (ADR-049) |
| `STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE` | `false` | §7.6 | [FIX-06] Advisory (false) vs blocking (true) store compliance |
| `COMPLIANCE_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD` | `0.7` | §7.6 | Minimum confidence to trigger compliance block |
| `BUDGET_GOVERNOR_ENABLED` | `true` | §2.14 | Enable/disable budget governor |
| `VECTOR_BACKEND` | `pgvector` | §6.7 | Vector search backend (`pgvector\|neo4j_native`) |
| `TELEGRAM_FILE_LIMIT_MB` | `50` | §7.5 | Telegram bot file size limit [V12] |
| `SOFT_FILE_LIMIT_MB` | `200` | §7.5 | Temp storage file limit |
| `ARTIFACT_TTL_HOURS` | `72` | §7.5 | Artifact expiry for temp storage |
| `STRATEGIST_MODEL_OVERRIDE` | *(none)* | §2.6 | Override Strategist model |
| `ENGINEER_MODEL_OVERRIDE` | *(none)* | §2.6 | Override Engineer model |
| `QUICKFIX_MODEL_OVERRIDE` | *(none)* | §2.6 | Override Quick Fix model |
| `APP_STORE_API_KEY` | *(required for iOS)* | §4.7 | [FIX-21] App Store Connect API key |
| `APP_STORE_ISSUER_ID` | *(required for iOS)* | §4.7 | [FIX-21] App Store Connect issuer ID |

## 8.10  Function Contract Reference (v5.6 — FIX-04)

Every function called in this specification has either an inline definition or a contract in this table. These are **contracts** (what a function does), not **implementations** (how it does it). For inline definitions, see the referenced section. For functions defined here, the implementation must conform to this contract.

### Contract 1: `upload_to_temp_storage`

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `file_path: str`, `project_id: str`, `ttl_hours: int = 72` |
| **Return Type** | `str` (signed URL) |
| **Side Effects** | Uploads to Supabase Storage bucket `build-artifacts`; records in `temp_artifacts` table; computes SHA-256 |
| **Error Behavior** | Raises `StorageError` on upload failure; retries 3× with backoff |
| **Defined In** | §7.5 (inline) |
| **Target File** | `file_delivery.py` |


### Contract 2: `send_telegram_file`

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `operator_id: str`, `file_path: str`, `project_id: str` |
| **Return Type** | `dict` (delivery receipt) |
| **Side Effects** | ≤50MB: Telegram `sendDocument` API; >50MB: uploads to Supabase, sends signed URL; >200MB: uploads with warning |
| **Error Behavior** | Raises `TelegramAPIError` on send failure; falls back to signed URL on Telegram error |
| **Defined In** | §7.5 (inline) |
| **Target File** | `file_delivery.py` |


### Contract 3: `apply_and_test_fix`

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `state: PipelineState`, `fix: dict`, `test_cmd: str` |
| **Return Type** | `dict` (`{applied: bool, test_passed: bool, output: str}`) |
| **Side Effects** | Applies code fix to working directory; runs test command; reverts on test failure |
| **Error Behavior** | Returns `{applied: False}` on apply error; reverts and logs on test failure |
| **Defined In** | Referenced in §2.2.2 |
| **Target File** | `war_room.py` |


### Contract 4: `execute_command`

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `cmd: str`, `cwd: str`, `timeout: int = 300`, `env: dict = None` |
| **Return Type** | `tuple[int, str, str]` (`exit_code, stdout, stderr`) |
| **Side Effects** | Runs subprocess in `cwd` with optional env vars; respects Zero Sudo (§2.5) |
| **Error Behavior** | Returns non-zero exit code on failure; raises `TimeoutError` after timeout seconds; blocks sudo commands |
| **Defined In** | Referenced in §4.4, §4.5 |
| **Target File** | `executor.py` |


### Contract 5: `write_file`

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `path: str`, `content: str`, `project_id: str` |
| **Return Type** | `bool` (success) |
| **Side Effects** | Writes content to path; validates against User-Space Enforcer (§2.5); records in audit log |
| **Error Behavior** | Raises `UserSpaceViolation` if path is outside allowed directories; returns `False` on I/O error |
| **Defined In** | Referenced in §4.4 |
| **Target File** | `executor.py` |


### Contract 6: `github_commit_binary`

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `project_id: str`, `file_path: str`, `message: str`, `branch: str = "main"` |
| **Return Type** | `str` (commit SHA) |
| **Side Effects** | Commits binary file to project repo via GitHub API; updates `state.git_commit_sha` |
| **Error Behavior** | Raises `GitHubAPIError` on API failure; retries 3× with backoff |
| **Defined In** | Referenced in §4.5, §4.9 |
| **Target File** | `github_client.py` |


### Contract 7: `github_reset_to_commit`

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `project_id: str`, `commit_sha: str` |
| **Return Type** | `bool` (success) |
| **Side Effects** | Resets local working directory to specified commit via `git reset --hard` |
| **Error Behavior** | Raises `GitError` if commit SHA not found; logs error and returns `False` |
| **Defined In** | Referenced in §6.1 (Time Machine) |
| **Target File** | `github_client.py` |


### Contract 8: `query_store_policy_events`

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `platform: str`, `category: str = None`, `limit: int = 10` |
| **Return Type** | `list[dict]` (matching `StorePolicyEvent` nodes) |
| **Side Effects** | Queries Neo4j for `StorePolicyEvent` nodes matching platform/category; read-only |
| **Error Behavior** | Returns empty list on Neo4j connection error (non-blocking); logs warning |
| **Defined In** | Referenced in §4.2, §7.6 |
| **Target File** | `mother_memory.py` |


### Contract 9: `generate_handoff_intelligence_pack` [FIX-27]

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `state: PipelineState`, `blueprint: Blueprint` |
| **Return Type** | `dict[str, str]` (filename → Markdown content) |
| **Side Effects** | Calls Engineer (Sonnet) 4× for per-project docs; if multi-stack and all siblings complete, calls Engineer 3× more for program docs; reads Mother Memory for sibling data |
| **Error Behavior** | If any individual doc generation fails, logs warning and continues with remaining docs (partial pack is better than no pack); raises only if ALL docs fail |
| **Cost** | ~$0.30–$0.50 per project (4 Engineer calls); ~$0.50–$0.80 for multi-stack programs (7 Engineer calls) |
| **Defined In** | §4.9 Step 2.5 (FIX-27) |
| **Target File** | `s8_handoff.py` |


### Contract 10: `store_handoff_docs_in_memory` [FIX-27]

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Parameters** | `project_id: str`, `program_id: Optional[str]`, `stack: str`, `app_category: str`, `docs: dict[str, str]` |
| **Return Type** | `None` |
| **Side Effects** | Creates/updates `HandoffDoc` nodes in Neo4j; creates `HAS_HANDOFF_DOC` relationships to `Project` node; sets `permanent = true` on all nodes |
| **Error Behavior** | Logs and continues on individual doc storage failure; does not halt pipeline |
| **Janitor Behavior** | `permanent = true` — Janitor Agent skips these nodes (no TTL pruning); high-value operator knowledge preserved indefinitely |
| **Defined In** | §6.3.4 (FIX-27) |
| **Target File** | `storage.py` |

> **[FIX-04, FIX-27] Cross-reference**: All 10 functions above appear in the §8.7 implementation manifest under their respective target files. Every call site in the spec that references one of these functions can be traced to this contract table. Contracts 9–10 added by FIX-27 (Operator Handoff Intelligence Pack).

---

## 8.11  Internal Consistency Verification (v5.6 — FIX-15+FIX-16)

This checklist is run as the final step before any version freeze. Each item is machine-checkable (grep, code analysis) or human-auditable.

| # | Check | Method | Expected Result |
|---|-------|--------|-----------------|
| 1 | All budget totals derive from `BUDGET_CONFIG` | grep for dollar amounts outside BUDGET_CONFIG → each must be in Verification Ledger or tagged "(illustrative)" | Zero orphan dollar amounts |
| 2 | All model references use `MODEL_CONFIG` fallback chains | grep for hardcoded model strings outside MODEL_CONFIG/MODEL_OVERRIDES | Zero hardcoded model strings |
| 3 | Every function call site has a contract in §8.10 or inline definition | grep for function names → each maps to §8.10 entry or inline def | 100% coverage |
| 4 | Every stage transition follows `VALID_TRANSITIONS` map | Code analysis: no direct `state.current_stage = X` outside `transition_to()` | Zero direct stage assignments |
| 5 | All env var defaults documented match code defaults | Compare §8.8 env var table against code `os.getenv()` defaults | 100% match |
| 6 | `VERIFICATION_LEDGER` entries match current web-verifiable pricing | Spot-check 5 random ledger entries against source URLs | All match within ±5% |
| 7 | No module referenced without a definition or implementation manifest entry | Cross-reference §8.7 manifest against all `import` and `from` statements in spec code | Zero undefined modules |
| 8 | All "optional/premium" items clearly separated from baseline | grep for items not in BUDGET_CONFIG → must be in §8.2.5 Additional Costs or tagged `[OPTIONAL]` | Zero ambiguous items |
| 9 | Key invariants stated in exactly one canonical location | Check: "zero sudo" (§2.5), "no ungrounded research" (§2.2.1/C5), "one stack per project" (§2.1.3b/H4), "user-space only" (§2.5) → each in one place, never contradicted | Zero duplicated invariants |
| 10 | All patches (v5.4.2 C1-C9/H1-H6/M1-M8 + v5.6 FIX-01 to FIX-27) have changelog entries | Count changelog entries vs. patch IDs | 38 + 12 = 50 entries |
| 11 | [FIX-16] Version contamination | grep for "v5.4" or "v5.5" in governance text (headers, footers, closings, status blocks). Historical appendixes (D/E) exempt. | Zero version contamination in governance text |

```python
# [FIX-16] Recommended: automated version lint
# Save as spec_lint.py and run after each edit:
#
# #!/usr/bin/env python3
# """spec_lint.py — AI Factory spec version contamination checker."""
# import re, sys
# CURRENT_VERSION = "5.6"
# EXEMPT_PATTERNS = [
#     "APPENDIX D", "APPENDIX E", "Supersedes",
#     "CHANGELOG", "FIX-0", "Delta"
# ]
# with open(sys.argv[1]) as f:
#     for i, line in enumerate(f, 1):
#         if any(p in line for p in EXEMPT_PATTERNS):
#             continue
#         if re.search(r"v5\.[0-4]|v5\.5", line) \
#                 and "governance" not in line.lower():
#             # Check if it's in a header/footer/status/closing context
#             if any(kw in line for kw in [
#                 "SPECIFICATION", "END OF", "STATUS",
#                 "UNIVERSAL MASTER", "Ready to Build"
#             ]):
#                 print(f"FAIL: Line {i}: {line.strip()}")
#                 sys.exit(1)
# print(f"PASS: Zero version contamination (v{CURRENT_VERSION})")
```

> **[FIX-15] Usage**: Run this checklist after every spec modification. If any check fails, the spec cannot be frozen — fix the inconsistency first, then re-run. The checklist itself is immutable within a version; it is updated only when new fix categories are added.

## APPENDIX C: GLOSSARY

| Term | Definition |
|------|-----------|
| **Airlock** | Fallback protocol: when API deploy fails, binary is sent to Telegram for manual upload |
| **Autopilot** | Full autonomous mode — pipeline makes all decisions automatically |
| **Blueprint** | The master specification generated at S2, consumed by S3–S8 |
| **Circuit Breaker** | $2/phase cost limit that pauses the pipeline when exceeded |
| **Copilot** | Semi-autonomous mode — pipeline presents 4-way decisions to operator via Telegram |
| **Delta Engine** | Computes differences between two snapshots for progress/rollback analysis |
| **DocuGen** | Module that generates legal documents (privacy policy, terms, etc.) at S8 |
| **Engineer** | Claude Sonnet 4.5 — writes code, generates files, applies fixes |
| **Graveyard** | Neo4j label for archived/rotting nodes (preserved but hidden) |
| **Grid Enforcer** | Pydantic validator ensuring 4px spacing and WCAG AA contrast |
| **Janitor Agent** | 6-hour scheduled task that archives broken/expired/orphaned graph nodes |
| **Mother Memory** | Neo4j knowledge graph that learns across projects |
| **PostSnapshot** | Neo4j label for nodes created after a time-travel restore point |
| **Quick Fix** | Claude Haiku 4.5 — lightweight syntax fixes and GUI supervision |
| **Scout** | Perplexity Sonar — read-only research agent |
| **Snapshot** | Atomic triple: Git commit + Supabase JSON + Neo4j node state |
| **Stack Selector Brain** | Strategist-powered module that chooses optimal tech stack at S2 |
| **Strategist** | Claude Opus 4.6 — architectural decisions, legal risk, War Room management |
| **Vibe Check** | Design Engine that discovers trending app aesthetics and generates design specs |
| **War Room** | 3-level error escalation: L1 (Haiku) → L2 (Scout+Sonnet) → L3 (Opus rewrite plan) |

**v5.4.1 Additions:**

| Term | Definition |
|------|-----------|
| **AssetRef** | Pydantic model for durable binary asset references (Supabase Storage URL) |
| **brand_assets** | PipelineState field containing list of AssetRef entries uploaded during S0 intake |
| **ingest_assets** | S3 CodeGen tool that downloads brand assets and places them in platform-specific locations |
| **MODEL_CONFIG** | Environment variable abstraction layer for AI model version strings |
| **Preflight Compliance Gate** | Non-blocking check at end of S1 that queries App Store guidelines for rejection risks |
| **StorePolicyEvent** | Neo4j node tracking App Store/Play Store rejection reasons for cross-project learning |
| **Stuck Project Detection** | 15-minute Cloud Scheduler job that detects and auto-recovers crashed pipelines |
| **Snapshot Checksum** | SHA-256 hash of `git_sha + state_hash + snapshot_id`, validated on restore |

**v5.4.2 Additions:**

| Term | Definition |
|------|-----------|
| **BUDGET_CONFIG** | [C2] Single canonical budget object (§1.4.0) from which ALL dollar references derive |
| **COMPLETED** | [C1] Terminal success state — project finished all stages S0→S8 successfully |
| **ComplianceGateResult** | [H2] Structured output from S1 App Store compliance preflight with blockers/warnings/confidence |
| **crash loop detection** | [H1] >3 crashes in 10 minutes triggers SAFE MODE — pipeline stops restarting |
| **CLAUDE_MAX_CONTEXT** | [C7] Env var controlling Claude context window (default: 200000, max: 1000000 for tier 4+) |
| **GUI Stack Pivot** | [H3] 3 consecutive GUI failures trigger War Room L3 and CLI-native stack proposal |
| **idempotency key** | [C6] UUID ensuring crash recovery doesn't double-execute side effects |
| **kill switch** | [C9] OS-level `shutdown -h +60` on MacinCloud sessions preventing runaway billing |
| **one-click agent** | [H6] PyInstaller binary bundling Python+Uvicorn+Cloudflared for terminal-free local setup |
| **pgvector** | [C8] Default vector search backend (Supabase, GA); replaces Neo4j vector (Public Preview) |
| **program_id** | [H4] Groups related single-stack projects that together form a multi-stack application |
| **RESEARCH_DEGRADATION_POLICY** | [C5] Safe fallback chain: cached→operator→UNVERIFIED (no ungrounded LLM) |
| **STRICT_STORE_COMPLIANCE** | [H2] Flag (default false) — advisory vs blocking store compliance gate |
| **VECTOR_BACKEND** | [C8] Env var: default `pgvector` (GA), opt-in `neo4j_vector` (Public Preview) |

**v5.6 Clean Room Additions:**

| Term | Definition |
|------|-----------|
| **Handoff Intelligence Pack** | [FIX-27] Set of 4 per-project + 3 per-program operational docs auto-generated at S8 for zero-IT operators |
| **HandoffDoc** | [FIX-27] Neo4j node storing generated operational documentation; permanent (Janitor-exempt); composite key on project_id + doc_type |
| **HAS_HANDOFF_DOC** | [FIX-27] Neo4j relationship linking a Project node to its HandoffDoc nodes |
| **Quick Start Guide** | [FIX-27] Per-project handoff doc: launch commands, URLs, environment setup for operator |
| **Emergency Runbook** | [FIX-27] Per-project handoff doc: common failure scenarios with step-by-step recovery procedures |
| **Service Map** | [FIX-27] Per-project handoff doc: visual/textual map of all services, endpoints, and dependencies |
| **Update Guide** | [FIX-27] Per-project handoff doc: how to apply updates, redeploy, and manage configuration changes |

---

## APPENDIX D: NO MAGIC HANDOFFS CHECKLIST (v5.4.2)

**Invariant**: Every piece of data produced by one stage and consumed by another must have a defined format, storage location, and retrieval method. No stage should "assume" data exists without checking.

| # | Handoff | Producer | Consumer | Format | Storage | Retrieval |
|---|---------|----------|----------|--------|---------|-----------|
| 1 | User brief → Requirements | Operator (Telegram) | S0 Intake (Haiku) | Free text + attachments | Telegram msg + Supabase | `state.s0_output` |
| 2 | Brand assets → Storage | S0 (Telegram uploads) | S3, S6, S7 | Binary files | Supabase Storage [C3] | `state.brand_assets[].storage_url` |
| 3 | S0 output → S1 Legal | S0 Intake | S1 Legal Gate | JSON dict | `state.s0_output` | Direct field access |
| 4 | Legal output → S2 Blueprint | S1 Legal | S2 Blueprint | JSON dict | `state.s1_output` | Direct field access |
| 5 | Blueprint → All later stages | S2 Blueprint | S3–S8 | Pydantic Blueprint | `state.s2_output` | `Blueprint.model_validate()` |
| 6 | Code files → Build | S3 CodeGen | S4 Build | Files in Git repo | GitHub repository | `git clone` / `git pull` |
| 7 | Build binary → Deploy | S4 Build | S6 Deploy | `.ipa` / `.aab` | Local → Supabase Storage | `state.s4_output["binary_path"]` |
| 8 | Build binary → Telegram | S6 Airlock | Operator | Binary file | Supabase Storage [C3] | `send_telegram_file()` [C3] |
| 9 | Test results → Verify | S5 Test | S7 Verify | JSON dict | `state.s5_output` | Direct field access |
| 10 | Legal docs → Handoff | S8 DocuGen | Operator (Telegram) | Markdown/PDF | `state.legal_documents` | Direct field access |
| 11 | Snapshot → Any stage | Time Machine | Any stage exit `/restore` command | JSON + Git SHA | Supabase `state_snapshots` | `restore_state()` |
| 12 | Error → War Room | Any stage | War Room L1/L2/L3 | JSON dict | `war_room_history` | Direct field access |
| 13 | Pattern → Future project | Mother Memory | Stage exit → Future project intake | Neo4j node | Neo4j AuraDB | Cypher query |
| 14 | Advisory lock → Stage gate | `@stage_gate` [C6] | Stage execution | Postgres lock | Postgres | `pg_try_advisory_lock()` |
| 15 | Kill switch → Mac session | Mac build [C9] | `start_mac_session_safe()` | OS timer | MacinCloud OS | `shutdown -h +N` |
| 16 | Handoff docs → Operator | S8 `generate_handoff_intelligence_pack()` [FIX-27] | Operator (Telegram + GitHub `/docs/`) | Markdown files | GitHub `/docs/` + HandoffDoc (Neo4j) | `state.s8_output["handoff_docs"]` |
